# World English Bible Updated

## License Information

**World English Bible Updated** is based on and adapted from: _World English Bible Updated_, [Public Domain](None), None, which is licensed under a [Public Domain CC0](https://creativecommons.org/public-domain/cc0/).

This markdown version is provided under the same license.



--------------------------------

## Psalms 1:1 (id: 1819001001)

1Blessed is the man who doesn’t walk in the counsel of the wicked, nor stand on the path of sinners, nor sit in the seat of scoffers;


## Psalms 1:2 (id: 1819001002)

2but his delight is in the LORD’s law. On his law he meditates day and night.


## Psalms 1:3 (id: 1819001003)

3He will be like a tree planted by the streams of water, that produces its fruit in its season, whose leaf also does not wither. Whatever he does shall prosper.


## Psalms 1:4 (id: 1819001004)

4The wicked are not so, but are like the chaff which the wind drives away.


## Psalms 1:5 (id: 1819001005)

5Therefore the wicked shall not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.


## Psalms 1:6 (id: 1819001006)

6For the LORD knows the way of the righteous, but the way of the wicked shall perish.


## Psalms 2:1 (id: 1819002001)

1Why do the nations rage, and the peoples plot a vain thing?


## Psalms 2:2 (id: 1819002002)

2The kings of the earth take a stand, and the rulers take counsel together, against the LORD, and against his Anointed, saying,


## Psalms 2:3 (id: 1819002003)

3“Let’s break their bonds apart, and cast their cords from us.”


## Psalms 2:4 (id: 1819002004)

4He who sits in the heavens will laugh. The Lord will have them in derision.


## Psalms 2:5 (id: 1819002005)

5Then he will speak to them in his anger, and terrify them in his wrath:


## Psalms 2:6 (id: 1819002006)

6“Yet I have set my King on my holy hill of Zion.”


## Psalms 2:7 (id: 1819002007)

7I will tell of the decree: The LORD said to me, “You are my son. Today I have become your father.


## Psalms 2:8 (id: 1819002008)

8Ask of me, and I will give the nations for your inheritance, the uttermost parts of the earth for your possession.


## Psalms 2:9 (id: 1819002009)

9You shall break them with a rod of iron. You shall dash them in pieces like a potter’s vessel.”


## Psalms 2:10 (id: 1819002010)

10Now therefore be wise, you kings. Be instructed, you judges of the earth.


## Psalms 2:11 (id: 1819002011)

11Serve the LORD with fear, and rejoice with trembling.


## Psalms 2:12 (id: 1819002012)

12Give sincere homage to the Son, lest he be angry, and you perish on the way, for his wrath will soon be kindled. Blessed are all those who take refuge in him.


## Psalms 3:1 (id: 1819003001)

1A Psalm by David, when he fled from Absalom his son. LORD, how my adversaries have increased! Many are those who rise up against me.


## Psalms 3:2 (id: 1819003002)

2Many there are who say of my soul, “There is no help for him in God.” Selah.


## Psalms 3:3 (id: 1819003003)

3But you, LORD, are a shield around me, my glory, and the one who lifts up my head.


## Psalms 3:4 (id: 1819003004)

4I cry to the LORD with my voice, and he answers me out of his holy hill. Selah.


## Psalms 3:5 (id: 1819003005)

5I laid myself down and slept. I awakened, for the LORD sustains me.


## Psalms 3:6 (id: 1819003006)

6I will not be afraid of tens of thousands of people who have set themselves against me on every side.


## Psalms 3:7 (id: 1819003007)

7Arise, LORD! Save me, my God! For you have struck all of my enemies on the cheek bone. You have broken the teeth of the wicked.


## Psalms 3:8 (id: 1819003008)

8Salvation belongs to the LORD. May your blessing be on your people. Selah.


## Psalms 4:1 (id: 1819004001)

1For the Chief Musician; on stringed instruments. A Psalm by David. Answer me when I call, God of my righteousness. Give me relief from my distress. Have mercy on me, and hear my prayer.


## Psalms 4:2 (id: 1819004002)

2You sons of men, how long shall my glory be turned into dishonor? Will you love vanity and seek after falsehood? Selah.


## Psalms 4:3 (id: 1819004003)

3But know that the LORD has set apart for himself him who is godly; The LORD will hear when I call to him.


## Psalms 4:4 (id: 1819004004)

4Stand in awe, and don’t sin. Search your own heart on your bed, and be still. Selah.


## Psalms 4:5 (id: 1819004005)

5Offer the sacrifices of righteousness. Put your trust in the LORD.


## Psalms 4:6 (id: 1819004006)

6Many say, “Who will show us any good?” LORD, let the light of your face shine on us.


## Psalms 4:7 (id: 1819004007)

7You have put gladness in my heart, more than when their grain and their new wine are increased.


## Psalms 4:8 (id: 1819004008)

8In peace I will both lay myself down and sleep, for you alone, LORD, make me live in safety.


## Psalms 5:1 (id: 1819005001)

1For the Chief Musician, with the flutes. A Psalm by David. Give ear to my words, LORD. Consider my meditation.


## Psalms 5:2 (id: 1819005002)

2Listen to the voice of my cry, my King and my God, for I pray to you.


## Psalms 5:3 (id: 1819005003)

3LORD, in the morning you will hear my voice. In the morning I will lay my requests before you, and will watch expectantly.


## Psalms 5:4 (id: 1819005004)

4For you are not a God who has pleasure in wickedness. Evil can’t live with you.


## Psalms 5:5 (id: 1819005005)

5The arrogant will not stand in your sight. You hate all workers of iniquity.


## Psalms 5:6 (id: 1819005006)

6You will destroy those who speak lies. The LORD abhors the bloodthirsty and deceitful man.


## Psalms 5:7 (id: 1819005007)

7But as for me, in the abundance of your loving kindness I will come into your house. I will bow toward your holy temple in reverence of you.


## Psalms 5:8 (id: 1819005008)

8Lead me, LORD, in your righteousness because of my enemies. Make your way straight before my face.


## Psalms 5:9 (id: 1819005009)

9For there is no faithfulness in their mouth. Their heart is destruction. Their throat is an open tomb. They flatter with their tongue.


## Psalms 5:10 (id: 1819005010)

10Hold them guilty, God. Let them fall by their own counsels. Thrust them out in the multitude of their transgressions, for they have rebelled against you.


## Psalms 5:11 (id: 1819005011)

11But let all those who take refuge in you rejoice. Let them always shout for joy, because you defend them. Let them also who love your name be joyful in you.


## Psalms 5:12 (id: 1819005012)

12For you will bless the righteous. LORD, you will surround him with favor as with a shield.


## Psalms 6:1 (id: 1819006001)

1For the Chief Musician; on stringed instruments, upon the eight\-stringed lyre. A Psalm by David. LORD, don’t rebuke me in your anger, neither discipline me in your wrath.


## Psalms 6:2 (id: 1819006002)

2Have mercy on me, LORD, for I am faint. LORD, heal me, for my bones are troubled.


## Psalms 6:3 (id: 1819006003)

3My soul is also in great anguish. But you, LORD—how long?


## Psalms 6:4 (id: 1819006004)

4Return, LORD. Deliver my soul, and save me for your loving kindness’ sake.


## Psalms 6:5 (id: 1819006005)

5For in death there is no memory of you. In Sheol, who shall give you thanks?


## Psalms 6:6 (id: 1819006006)

6I am weary with my groaning. Every night I flood my bed. I drench my couch with my tears.


## Psalms 6:7 (id: 1819006007)

7My eye wastes away because of grief. It grows old because of all my adversaries.


## Psalms 6:8 (id: 1819006008)

8Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity, for the LORD has heard the voice of my weeping.


## Psalms 6:9 (id: 1819006009)

9The LORD has heard my supplication. The LORD accepts my prayer.


## Psalms 6:10 (id: 1819006010)

10May all my enemies be ashamed and dismayed. They shall turn back, they shall be disgraced suddenly.


## Psalms 7:1 (id: 1819007001)

1A meditation by David, which he sang to the LORD, concerning the words of Cush, the Benjamite. LORD, my God, I take refuge in you. Save me from all those who pursue me, and deliver me,


## Psalms 7:2 (id: 1819007002)

2lest they tear apart my soul like a lion, ripping it in pieces, while there is no one to deliver.


## Psalms 7:3 (id: 1819007003)

3LORD, my God, if I have done this, if there is iniquity in my hands,


## Psalms 7:4 (id: 1819007004)

4if I have rewarded evil to him who was at peace with me (yes, I have plundered him who without cause was my adversary),


## Psalms 7:5 (id: 1819007005)

5let the enemy pursue my soul, and overtake it; yes, let him tread my life down to the earth, and lay my glory in the dust. Selah.


## Psalms 7:6 (id: 1819007006)

6Arise, LORD, in your anger. Lift up yourself against the rage of my adversaries. Awake for me. You have commanded judgment.


## Psalms 7:7 (id: 1819007007)

7Let the congregation of the peoples surround you. Rule over them on high.


## Psalms 7:8 (id: 1819007008)

8The LORD administers judgment to the peoples. Judge me, LORD, according to my righteousness, and to my integrity that is in me.


## Psalms 7:9 (id: 1819007009)

9Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end, but establish the righteous; their minds and hearts are searched by the righteous God.


## Psalms 7:10 (id: 1819007010)

10My shield is with God, who saves the upright in heart.


## Psalms 7:11 (id: 1819007011)

11God is a righteous judge, yes, a God who has indignation every day.


## Psalms 7:12 (id: 1819007012)

12If a man doesn’t repent, he will sharpen his sword; he has bent and strung his bow.


## Psalms 7:13 (id: 1819007013)

13He has also prepared for himself the instruments of death. He makes ready his flaming arrows.


## Psalms 7:14 (id: 1819007014)

14Behold, he travails with iniquity. Yes, he has conceived mischief, and brought out falsehood.


## Psalms 7:15 (id: 1819007015)

15He has dug a hole, and has fallen into the pit which he made.


## Psalms 7:16 (id: 1819007016)

16The trouble he causes shall return to his own head. His violence shall come down on the crown of his own head.


## Psalms 7:17 (id: 1819007017)

17I will give thanks to the LORD according to his righteousness, and will sing praise to the name of the LORD Most High.


## Psalms 8:1 (id: 1819008001)

1For the Chief Musician; on an instrument of Gath. A Psalm by David. LORD, our Lord, how majestic is your name in all the earth! You have set your glory above the heavens!


## Psalms 8:2 (id: 1819008002)

2From the lips of babes and infants you have established strength, because of your adversaries, that you might silence the enemy and the avenger.


## Psalms 8:3 (id: 1819008003)

3When I consider your heavens, the work of your fingers, the moon and the stars, which you have ordained,


## Psalms 8:4 (id: 1819008004)

4what is man, that you think of him? What is the son of man, that you care for him?


## Psalms 8:5 (id: 1819008005)

5For you have made him a little lower than the angels, and crowned him with glory and honor.


## Psalms 8:6 (id: 1819008006)

6You make him ruler over the works of your hands. You have put all things under his feet:


## Psalms 8:7 (id: 1819008007)

7All sheep and cattle, yes, and the animals of the field,


## Psalms 8:8 (id: 1819008008)

8the birds of the sky, the fish of the sea, and whatever passes through the paths of the seas.


## Psalms 8:9 (id: 1819008009)

9LORD, our Lord, how majestic is your name in all the earth!


## Psalms 9:1 (id: 1819009001)

1For the Chief Musician. Set to “The Death of the Son.” A Psalm by David. I will give thanks to the LORD with my whole heart. I will tell of all your marvelous works.


## Psalms 9:2 (id: 1819009002)

2I will be glad and rejoice in you. I will sing praise to your name, O Most High.


## Psalms 9:3 (id: 1819009003)

3When my enemies turn back, they stumble and perish in your presence.


## Psalms 9:4 (id: 1819009004)

4For you have maintained my just cause. You sit on the throne judging righteously.


## Psalms 9:5 (id: 1819009005)

5You have rebuked the nations. You have destroyed the wicked. You have blotted out their name forever and ever.


## Psalms 9:6 (id: 1819009006)

6The enemy is overtaken by endless ruin. The very memory of the cities which you have overthrown has perished.


## Psalms 9:7 (id: 1819009007)

7But the LORD reigns forever. He has prepared his throne for judgment.


## Psalms 9:8 (id: 1819009008)

8He will judge the world in righteousness. He will administer judgment to the peoples in uprightness.


## Psalms 9:9 (id: 1819009009)

9The LORD will also be a high tower for the oppressed; a high tower in times of trouble.


## Psalms 9:10 (id: 1819009010)

10Those who know your name will put their trust in you, for you, LORD, have not forsaken those who seek you.


## Psalms 9:11 (id: 1819009011)

11Sing praises to the LORD, who dwells in Zion, and declare among the people what he has done.


## Psalms 9:12 (id: 1819009012)

12For he who avenges blood remembers them. He doesn’t forget the cry of the afflicted.


## Psalms 9:13 (id: 1819009013)

13Have mercy on me, LORD. See my affliction by those who hate me, and lift me up from the gates of death,


## Psalms 9:14 (id: 1819009014)

14that I may show all of your praise. I will rejoice in your salvation in the gates of the daughter of Zion.


## Psalms 9:15 (id: 1819009015)

15The nations have sunk down in the pit that they made. In the net which they hid, their own foot is taken.


## Psalms 9:16 (id: 1819009016)

16The LORD has made himself known. He has executed judgment. The wicked is snared by the work of his own hands. Meditation. Selah.


## Psalms 9:17 (id: 1819009017)

17The wicked shall be turned back to Sheol, even all the nations that forget God.


## Psalms 9:18 (id: 1819009018)

18For the needy shall not always be forgotten, nor the hope of the poor perish forever.


## Psalms 9:19 (id: 1819009019)

19Arise, LORD! Don’t let man prevail. Let the nations be judged in your sight.


## Psalms 9:20 (id: 1819009020)

20Put them in fear, LORD. Let the nations know that they are only men. Selah.


## Psalms 10:1 (id: 1819010001)

1Why do you stand far off, LORD? Why do you hide yourself in times of trouble?


## Psalms 10:2 (id: 1819010002)

2In arrogance, the wicked hunt down the weak. They are caught in the schemes that they devise.


## Psalms 10:3 (id: 1819010003)

3For the wicked boasts of his heart’s cravings. He blesses the greedy and condemns the LORD.


## Psalms 10:4 (id: 1819010004)

4The wicked, in the pride of his face, has no room in his thoughts for God.


## Psalms 10:5 (id: 1819010005)

5His ways are prosperous at all times. He is arrogant, and your laws are far from his sight. As for all his adversaries, he sneers at them.


## Psalms 10:6 (id: 1819010006)

6He says in his heart, “I shall not be shaken. For generations I shall have no trouble.”


## Psalms 10:7 (id: 1819010007)

7His mouth is full of cursing, deceit, and oppression. Under his tongue is mischief and iniquity.


## Psalms 10:8 (id: 1819010008)

8He lies in wait near the villages. From ambushes, he murders the innocent. His eyes are secretly set against the helpless.


## Psalms 10:9 (id: 1819010009)

9He lurks in secret as a lion in his ambush. He lies in wait to catch the helpless. He catches the helpless when he draws him in his net.


## Psalms 10:10 (id: 1819010010)

10The helpless are crushed. They collapse. They fall under his strength.


## Psalms 10:11 (id: 1819010011)

11He says in his heart, “God has forgotten. He hides his face. He will never see it.”


## Psalms 10:12 (id: 1819010012)

12Arise, LORD! God, lift up your hand! Don’t forget the helpless.


## Psalms 10:13 (id: 1819010013)

13Why does the wicked person condemn God, and say in his heart, “God won’t call me into account”?


## Psalms 10:14 (id: 1819010014)

14But you do see trouble and grief. You consider it to take it into your hand. You help the victim and the fatherless.


## Psalms 10:15 (id: 1819010015)

15Break the arm of the wicked. As for the evil man, seek out his wickedness until you find none.


## Psalms 10:16 (id: 1819010016)

16The LORD is King forever and ever! The nations will perish out of his land.


## Psalms 10:17 (id: 1819010017)

17LORD, you have heard the desire of the humble. You will prepare their heart. You will cause your ear to hear,


## Psalms 10:18 (id: 1819010018)

18to judge the fatherless and the oppressed, that man who is of the earth may terrify no more.


## Psalms 11:1 (id: 1819011001)

1For the Chief Musician. By David. In the LORD, I take refuge. How can you say to my soul, “Flee as a bird to your mountain”?


## Psalms 11:2 (id: 1819011002)

2For, behold, the wicked bend their bows. They set their arrows on the strings, that they may shoot in darkness at the upright in heart.


## Psalms 11:3 (id: 1819011003)

3If the foundations are destroyed, what can the righteous do?


## Psalms 11:4 (id: 1819011004)

4The LORD is in his holy temple. The LORD is on his throne in heaven. His eyes observe. His eyes examine the children of men.


## Psalms 11:5 (id: 1819011005)

5The LORD examines the righteous, but his soul hates the wicked and him who loves violence.


## Psalms 11:6 (id: 1819011006)

6On the wicked he will rain blazing coals; fire, sulfur, and scorching wind shall be the portion of their cup.


## Psalms 11:7 (id: 1819011007)

7For the LORD is righteous. He loves righteousness. The upright shall see his face.


## Psalms 12:1 (id: 1819012001)

1For the Chief Musician; upon an eight\-stringed lyre. A Psalm of David. Help, LORD; for the godly man ceases. For the faithful fail from among the children of men.


## Psalms 12:2 (id: 1819012002)

2Everyone lies to his neighbor. They speak with flattering lips, and with a double heart.


## Psalms 12:3 (id: 1819012003)

3May the LORD cut off all flattering lips, and the tongue that boasts,


## Psalms 12:4 (id: 1819012004)

4who have said, “With our tongue we will prevail. Our lips are our own. Who is lord over us?”


## Psalms 12:5 (id: 1819012005)

5“Because of the oppression of the weak and because of the groaning of the needy, I will now arise,” says the LORD; “I will set him in safety from those who malign him.”


## Psalms 12:6 (id: 1819012006)

6The LORD’s words are flawless words, as silver refined in a clay furnace, purified seven times.


## Psalms 12:7 (id: 1819012007)

7You will keep them, LORD. You will preserve them from this generation forever.


## Psalms 12:8 (id: 1819012008)

8The wicked walk on every side, when what is vile is exalted among the sons of men.


## Psalms 13:1 (id: 1819013001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. How long, LORD? Will you forget me forever? How long will you hide your face from me?


## Psalms 13:2 (id: 1819013002)

2How long shall I take counsel in my soul, having sorrow in my heart every day? How long shall my enemy triumph over me?


## Psalms 13:3 (id: 1819013003)

3Behold, and answer me, LORD, my God. Give light to my eyes, lest I sleep in death;


## Psalms 13:4 (id: 1819013004)

4lest my enemy say, “I have prevailed against him;” lest my adversaries rejoice when I fall.


## Psalms 13:5 (id: 1819013005)

5But I trust in your loving kindness. My heart rejoices in your salvation.


## Psalms 13:6 (id: 1819013006)

6I will sing to the LORD, because he has been good to me.


## Psalms 14:1 (id: 1819014001)

1For the Chief Musician. By David. The fool has said in his heart, “There is no God.” They are corrupt. They have done abominable deeds. There is no one who does good.


## Psalms 14:2 (id: 1819014002)

2The LORD looked down from heaven on the children of men, to see if there were any who understood, who sought after God.


## Psalms 14:3 (id: 1819014003)

3They have all gone aside. They have together become corrupt. There is no one who does good, no, not one.


## Psalms 14:4 (id: 1819014004)

4Have all the workers of iniquity no knowledge, who eat up my people as they eat bread, and don’t call on the LORD?


## Psalms 14:5 (id: 1819014005)

5There they were in great fear, for God is in the generation of the righteous.


## Psalms 14:6 (id: 1819014006)

6You frustrate the plan of the poor, because the LORD is his refuge.


## Psalms 14:7 (id: 1819014007)

7Oh that the salvation of Israel would come out of Zion! When the LORD restores the fortunes of his people, then Jacob shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad.


## Psalms 15:1 (id: 1819015001)

1A Psalm by David. LORD, who shall dwell in your sanctuary? Who shall live on your holy hill?


## Psalms 15:2 (id: 1819015002)

2He who walks blamelessly and does what is right, and speaks truth in his heart;


## Psalms 15:3 (id: 1819015003)

3he who doesn’t slander with his tongue, nor does evil to his friend, nor casts slurs against his fellow man;


## Psalms 15:4 (id: 1819015004)

4in whose eyes a vile man is despised, but who honors those who fear the LORD; he who keeps an oath even when it hurts, and doesn’t change;


## Psalms 15:5 (id: 1819015005)

5he who doesn’t lend out his money for usury, nor take a bribe against the innocent. He who does these things shall never be shaken.


## Psalms 16:1 (id: 1819016001)

1A Poem by David. Preserve me, God, for I take refuge in you.


## Psalms 16:2 (id: 1819016002)

2My soul, you have said to the LORD, “You are my Lord. Apart from you I have no good thing.”


## Psalms 16:3 (id: 1819016003)

3As for the saints who are in the earth, they are the excellent ones in whom is all my delight.


## Psalms 16:4 (id: 1819016004)

4Their sorrows shall be multiplied who give gifts to another god. Their drink offerings of blood I will not offer, nor take their names on my lips.


## Psalms 16:5 (id: 1819016005)

5The LORD assigned my portion and my cup. You made my lot secure.


## Psalms 16:6 (id: 1819016006)

6The lines have fallen to me in pleasant places. Yes, I have a good inheritance.


## Psalms 16:7 (id: 1819016007)

7I will bless the LORD, who has given me counsel. Yes, my heart instructs me in the night seasons.


## Psalms 16:8 (id: 1819016008)

8I have set the LORD always before me. Because he is at my right hand, I shall not be moved.


## Psalms 16:9 (id: 1819016009)

9Therefore my heart is glad, and my tongue rejoices. My body shall also dwell in safety.


## Psalms 16:10 (id: 1819016010)

10For you will not leave my soul in Sheol, neither will you allow your holy one to see corruption.


## Psalms 16:11 (id: 1819016011)

11You will show me the path of life. In your presence is fullness of joy. In your right hand there are pleasures forever more.


## Psalms 17:1 (id: 1819017001)

1A Prayer by David. Hear, LORD, my righteous plea. Give ear to my prayer that doesn’t go out of deceitful lips.


## Psalms 17:2 (id: 1819017002)

2Let my sentence come out of your presence. Let your eyes look on equity.


## Psalms 17:3 (id: 1819017003)

3You have proved my heart. You have visited me in the night. You have tried me, and found nothing. I have resolved that my mouth shall not disobey.


## Psalms 17:4 (id: 1819017004)

4As for the deeds of men, by the word of your lips, I have kept myself from the ways of the violent.


## Psalms 17:5 (id: 1819017005)

5My steps have held fast to your paths. My feet have not slipped.


## Psalms 17:6 (id: 1819017006)

6I have called on you, for you will answer me, God. Turn your ear to me. Hear my speech.


## Psalms 17:7 (id: 1819017007)

7Show your marvelous loving kindness, you who save those who take refuge by your right hand from their enemies.


## Psalms 17:8 (id: 1819017008)

8Keep me as the apple of your eye. Hide me under the shadow of your wings,


## Psalms 17:9 (id: 1819017009)

9from the wicked who oppress me, my deadly enemies, who surround me.


## Psalms 17:10 (id: 1819017010)

10They close up their callous hearts. With their mouth they speak proudly.


## Psalms 17:11 (id: 1819017011)

11They have now surrounded us in our steps. They set their eyes to cast us down to the earth.


## Psalms 17:12 (id: 1819017012)

12He is like a lion that is greedy of his prey, as it were a young lion lurking in secret places.


## Psalms 17:13 (id: 1819017013)

13Arise, LORD, confront him. Cast him down. Deliver my soul from the wicked by your sword,


## Psalms 17:14 (id: 1819017014)

14from men by your hand, LORD, from men of the world, whose portion is in this life. You fill the belly of your cherished ones. Your sons have plenty, and they store up wealth for their children.


## Psalms 17:15 (id: 1819017015)

15As for me, I shall see your face in righteousness. I shall be satisfied, when I awake, with seeing your form.


## Psalms 18:1 (id: 1819018001)

1For the Chief Musician. By David the servant of the LORD, who spoke to the LORD the words of this song in the day that the LORD delivered him from the hand of all his enemies, and from the hand of Saul. He said, I love you, LORD, my strength.


## Psalms 18:2 (id: 1819018002)

2The LORD is my rock, my fortress, and my deliverer; my God, my rock, in whom I take refuge; my shield, and the horn of my salvation, my high tower.


## Psalms 18:3 (id: 1819018003)

3I call on the LORD, who is worthy to be praised; and I am saved from my enemies.


## Psalms 18:4 (id: 1819018004)

4The cords of death surrounded me. The floods of ungodliness made me afraid.


## Psalms 18:5 (id: 1819018005)

5The cords of Sheol were around me. The snares of death came on me.


## Psalms 18:6 (id: 1819018006)

6In my distress I called on the LORD, and cried to my God. He heard my voice out of his temple. My cry before him came into his ears.


## Psalms 18:7 (id: 1819018007)

7Then the earth shook and trembled. The foundations also of the mountains quaked and were shaken, because he was angry.


## Psalms 18:8 (id: 1819018008)

8Smoke went out of his nostrils. Consuming fire came out of his mouth. Coals were kindled by it.


## Psalms 18:9 (id: 1819018009)

9He bowed the heavens also, and came down. Thick darkness was under his feet.


## Psalms 18:10 (id: 1819018010)

10He rode on a cherub, and flew. Yes, he soared on the wings of the wind.


## Psalms 18:11 (id: 1819018011)

11He made darkness his hiding place, his pavilion around him, darkness of waters, thick clouds of the skies.


## Psalms 18:12 (id: 1819018012)

12At the brightness before him his thick clouds passed, hailstones and coals of fire.


## Psalms 18:13 (id: 1819018013)

13The LORD also thundered in the sky. The Most High uttered his voice: hailstones and coals of fire.


## Psalms 18:14 (id: 1819018014)

14He sent out his arrows, and scattered them. He routed them with great lightning bolts.


## Psalms 18:15 (id: 1819018015)

15Then the channels of waters appeared. The foundations of the world were laid bare at your rebuke, LORD, at the blast of the breath of your nostrils.


## Psalms 18:16 (id: 1819018016)

16He sent from on high. He took me. He drew me out of many waters.


## Psalms 18:17 (id: 1819018017)

17He delivered me from my strong enemy, from those who hated me; for they were too mighty for me.


## Psalms 18:18 (id: 1819018018)

18They came on me in the day of my calamity, but the LORD was my support.


## Psalms 18:19 (id: 1819018019)

19He brought me out also into a large place. He delivered me, because he delighted in me.


## Psalms 18:20 (id: 1819018020)

20The LORD has rewarded me according to my righteousness. According to the cleanness of my hands, he has recompensed me.


## Psalms 18:21 (id: 1819018021)

21For I have kept the ways of the LORD, and have not wickedly departed from my God.


## Psalms 18:22 (id: 1819018022)

22For all his ordinances were before me. I didn’t put away his statutes from me.


## Psalms 18:23 (id: 1819018023)

23I was also blameless with him. I kept myself from my iniquity.


## Psalms 18:24 (id: 1819018024)

24Therefore the LORD has rewarded me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in his eyesight.


## Psalms 18:25 (id: 1819018025)

25With the merciful you will show yourself merciful. With the perfect man, you will show yourself perfect.


## Psalms 18:26 (id: 1819018026)

26With the pure, you will show yourself pure. With the crooked you will show yourself shrewd.


## Psalms 18:27 (id: 1819018027)

27For you will save the afflicted people, but the arrogant eyes you will bring down.


## Psalms 18:28 (id: 1819018028)

28For you will light my lamp, LORD. My God will light up my darkness.


## Psalms 18:29 (id: 1819018029)

29For by you, I advance through a troop. By my God, I leap over a wall.


## Psalms 18:30 (id: 1819018030)

30As for God, his way is perfect. The LORD’s word is tried. He is a shield to all those who take refuge in him.


## Psalms 18:31 (id: 1819018031)

31For who is God, except the LORD? Who is a rock, besides our God,


## Psalms 18:32 (id: 1819018032)

32the God who arms me with strength, and makes my way perfect?


## Psalms 18:33 (id: 1819018033)

33He makes my feet like deer’s feet, and sets me on my high places.


## Psalms 18:34 (id: 1819018034)

34He teaches my hands to war, so that my arms bend a bow of bronze.


## Psalms 18:35 (id: 1819018035)

35You have also given me the shield of your salvation. Your right hand sustains me. Your gentleness has made me great.


## Psalms 18:36 (id: 1819018036)

36You have enlarged my steps under me, My feet have not slipped.


## Psalms 18:37 (id: 1819018037)

37I will pursue my enemies, and overtake them. I won’t turn away until they are consumed.


## Psalms 18:38 (id: 1819018038)

38I will strike them through, so that they will not be able to rise. They shall fall under my feet.


## Psalms 18:39 (id: 1819018039)

39For you have armed me with strength to the battle. You have subdued under me those who rose up against me.


## Psalms 18:40 (id: 1819018040)

40You have also made my enemies turn their backs to me, that I might cut off those who hate me.


## Psalms 18:41 (id: 1819018041)

41They cried, but there was no one to save; even to the LORD, but he didn’t answer them.


## Psalms 18:42 (id: 1819018042)

42Then I beat them small as the dust before the wind. I cast them out as the mire of the streets.


## Psalms 18:43 (id: 1819018043)

43You have delivered me from the strivings of the people. You have made me the head of the nations. A people whom I have not known shall serve me.


## Psalms 18:44 (id: 1819018044)

44As soon as they hear of me they shall obey me. The foreigners shall submit themselves to me.


## Psalms 18:45 (id: 1819018045)

45The foreigners shall fade away, and shall come trembling out of their strongholds.


## Psalms 18:46 (id: 1819018046)

46The LORD lives! Blessed be my rock. Exalted be the God of my salvation,


## Psalms 18:47 (id: 1819018047)

47even the God who executes vengeance for me, and subdues peoples under me.


## Psalms 18:48 (id: 1819018048)

48He rescues me from my enemies. Yes, you lift me up above those who rise up against me. You deliver me from the violent man.


## Psalms 18:49 (id: 1819018049)

49Therefore I will give thanks to you, LORD, among the nations, and will sing praises to your name.


## Psalms 18:50 (id: 1819018050)

50He gives great deliverance to his king, and shows loving kindness to his anointed, to David and to his offspring, forever more.


## Psalms 19:1 (id: 1819019001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. The heavens declare the glory of God. The expanse shows his handiwork.


## Psalms 19:2 (id: 1819019002)

2Day after day they pour out speech, and night after night they display knowledge.


## Psalms 19:3 (id: 1819019003)

3There is no speech nor language where their voice is not heard.


## Psalms 19:4 (id: 1819019004)

4Their voice has gone out through all the earth, their words to the end of the world. In them he has set a tent for the sun,


## Psalms 19:5 (id: 1819019005)

5which is as a bridegroom coming out of his room, like a strong man rejoicing to run his course.


## Psalms 19:6 (id: 1819019006)

6His going out is from the end of the heavens, his circuit to its ends. There is nothing hidden from its heat.


## Psalms 19:7 (id: 1819019007)

7The LORD’s law is perfect, restoring the soul. The LORD’s covenant is sure, making wise the simple.


## Psalms 19:8 (id: 1819019008)

8The LORD’s precepts are right, rejoicing the heart. The LORD’s commandment is pure, enlightening the eyes.


## Psalms 19:9 (id: 1819019009)

9The fear of the LORD is clean, enduring forever. The LORD’s ordinances are true, and righteous altogether.


## Psalms 19:10 (id: 1819019010)

10They are more to be desired than gold, yes, than much fine gold, sweeter also than honey and the extract of the honeycomb.


## Psalms 19:11 (id: 1819019011)

11Moreover your servant is warned by them. In keeping them there is great reward.


## Psalms 19:12 (id: 1819019012)

12Who can discern his errors? Forgive me from hidden errors.


## Psalms 19:13 (id: 1819019013)

13Keep back your servant also from presumptuous sins. Let them not have dominion over me. Then I will be upright. I will be blameless and innocent of great transgression.


## Psalms 19:14 (id: 1819019014)

14Let the words of my mouth and the meditation of my heart be acceptable in your sight, LORD, my rock, and my redeemer.


## Psalms 20:1 (id: 1819020001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. May the LORD answer you in the day of trouble. May the name of the God of Jacob set you up on high,


## Psalms 20:2 (id: 1819020002)

2send you help from the sanctuary, grant you support from Zion,


## Psalms 20:3 (id: 1819020003)

3remember all your offerings, and accept your burned sacrifice. Selah.


## Psalms 20:4 (id: 1819020004)

4May he grant you your heart’s desire, and fulfill all your counsel.


## Psalms 20:5 (id: 1819020005)

5We will triumph in your salvation. In the name of our God, we will set up our banners. May the LORD grant all your requests.


## Psalms 20:6 (id: 1819020006)

6Now I know that the LORD saves his anointed. He will answer him from his holy heaven, with the saving strength of his right hand.


## Psalms 20:7 (id: 1819020007)

7Some trust in chariots, and some in horses, but we trust in the name of the LORD our God.


## Psalms 20:8 (id: 1819020008)

8They are bowed down and fallen, but we rise up, and stand upright.


## Psalms 20:9 (id: 1819020009)

9Save, LORD! Let the King answer us when we call!


## Psalms 21:1 (id: 1819021001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. The king rejoices in your strength, LORD! How greatly he rejoices in your salvation!


## Psalms 21:2 (id: 1819021002)

2You have given him his heart’s desire, and have not withheld the request of his lips. Selah.


## Psalms 21:3 (id: 1819021003)

3For you meet him with the blessings of goodness. You set a crown of fine gold on his head.


## Psalms 21:4 (id: 1819021004)

4He asked life of you and you gave it to him, even length of days forever and ever.


## Psalms 21:5 (id: 1819021005)

5His glory is great in your salvation. You lay honor and majesty on him.


## Psalms 21:6 (id: 1819021006)

6For you make him most blessed forever. You make him glad with joy in your presence.


## Psalms 21:7 (id: 1819021007)

7For the king trusts in the LORD. Through the loving kindness of the Most High, he shall not be moved.


## Psalms 21:8 (id: 1819021008)

8Your hand will find out all of your enemies. Your right hand will find out those who hate you.


## Psalms 21:9 (id: 1819021009)

9You will make them as a fiery furnace in the time of your anger. The LORD will swallow them up in his wrath. The fire shall devour them.


## Psalms 21:10 (id: 1819021010)

10You will destroy their descendants from the earth, their posterity from among the children of men.


## Psalms 21:11 (id: 1819021011)

11For they intended evil against you. They plotted evil against you which cannot succeed.


## Psalms 21:12 (id: 1819021012)

12For you will make them turn their back, when you aim drawn bows at their face.


## Psalms 21:13 (id: 1819021013)

13Be exalted, LORD, in your strength, so we will sing and praise your power.


## Psalms 22:1 (id: 1819022001)

1For the Chief Musician; set to “The Doe of the Morning.” A Psalm by David. My God, my God, why have you forsaken me? Why are you so far from helping me, and from the words of my groaning?


## Psalms 22:2 (id: 1819022002)

2My God, I cry in the daytime, but you don’t answer; in the night season, and am not silent.


## Psalms 22:3 (id: 1819022003)

3But you are holy, you who inhabit the praises of Israel.


## Psalms 22:4 (id: 1819022004)

4Our fathers trusted in you. They trusted, and you delivered them.


## Psalms 22:5 (id: 1819022005)

5They cried to you, and were delivered. They trusted in you, and were not disappointed.


## Psalms 22:6 (id: 1819022006)

6But I am a worm, and no man; a reproach of men, and despised by the people.


## Psalms 22:7 (id: 1819022007)

7All those who see me mock me. They insult me with their lips. They shake their heads, saying,


## Psalms 22:8 (id: 1819022008)

8“He trusts in the LORD. Let him deliver him. Let him rescue him, since he delights in him.”


## Psalms 22:9 (id: 1819022009)

9But you brought me out of the womb. You made me trust while at my mother’s breasts.


## Psalms 22:10 (id: 1819022010)

10I was thrown on you from my mother’s womb. You are my God since my mother bore me.


## Psalms 22:11 (id: 1819022011)

11Don’t be far from me, for trouble is near. For there is no one to help.


## Psalms 22:12 (id: 1819022012)

12Many bulls have surrounded me. Strong bulls of Bashan have encircled me.


## Psalms 22:13 (id: 1819022013)

13They open their mouths wide against me, lions tearing prey and roaring.


## Psalms 22:14 (id: 1819022014)

14I am poured out like water. All my bones are out of joint. My heart is like wax. It is melted within me.


## Psalms 22:15 (id: 1819022015)

15My strength is dried up like a potsherd. My tongue sticks to the roof of my mouth. You have brought me into the dust of death.


## Psalms 22:16 (id: 1819022016)

16For dogs have surrounded me. A company of evildoers have enclosed me. They have pierced my hands and feet.


## Psalms 22:17 (id: 1819022017)

17I can count all of my bones. They look and stare at me.


## Psalms 22:18 (id: 1819022018)

18They divide my garments among them. They cast lots for my clothing.


## Psalms 22:19 (id: 1819022019)

19But don’t be far off, LORD. You are my help. Hurry to help me!


## Psalms 22:20 (id: 1819022020)

20Deliver my soul from the sword, my precious life from the power of the dog.


## Psalms 22:21 (id: 1819022021)

21Save me from the lion’s mouth! Yes, you have rescued me from the horns of the wild oxen.


## Psalms 22:22 (id: 1819022022)

22I will declare your name to my brothers. Among the assembly, I will praise you.


## Psalms 22:23 (id: 1819022023)

23You who fear the LORD, praise him! All you descendants of Jacob, glorify him! Stand in awe of him, all you descendants of Israel!


## Psalms 22:24 (id: 1819022024)

24For he has not despised nor abhorred the affliction of the afflicted, neither has he hidden his face from him; but when he cried to him, he heard.


## Psalms 22:25 (id: 1819022025)

25My praise of you comes in the great assembly. I will pay my vows before those who fear him.


## Psalms 22:26 (id: 1819022026)

26The humble shall eat and be satisfied. They shall praise the LORD who seek after him. Let your hearts live forever.


## Psalms 22:27 (id: 1819022027)

27All the ends of the earth shall remember and turn to the LORD. All the relatives of the nations shall worship before you.


## Psalms 22:28 (id: 1819022028)

28For the kingdom is the LORD’s. He is the ruler over the nations.


## Psalms 22:29 (id: 1819022029)

29All the rich ones of the earth shall eat and worship. All those who go down to the dust shall bow before him, even he who can’t keep his soul alive.


## Psalms 22:30 (id: 1819022030)

30Posterity shall serve him. Future generations shall be told about the Lord.


## Psalms 22:31 (id: 1819022031)

31They shall come and shall declare his righteousness to a people that shall be born, for he has done it.


## Psalms 23:1 (id: 1819023001)

1A Psalm by David. The LORD is my shepherd; I shall lack nothing.


## Psalms 23:2 (id: 1819023002)

2He makes me lie down in green pastures. He leads me beside still waters.


## Psalms 23:3 (id: 1819023003)

3He restores my soul. He guides me in the paths of righteousness for his name’s sake.


## Psalms 23:4 (id: 1819023004)

4Even though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil, for you are with me. Your rod and your staff, they comfort me.


## Psalms 23:5 (id: 1819023005)

5You prepare a table before me in the presence of my enemies. You anoint my head with oil. My cup runs over.


## Psalms 23:6 (id: 1819023006)

6Surely goodness and loving kindness shall follow me all the days of my life, and I will dwell in the LORD’s house forever.


## Psalms 24:1 (id: 1819024001)

1A Psalm by David. The earth is the LORD’s, with its fullness; the world, and those who dwell in it.


## Psalms 24:2 (id: 1819024002)

2For he has founded it on the seas, and established it on the floods.


## Psalms 24:3 (id: 1819024003)

3Who may ascend to the LORD’s hill? Who may stand in his holy place?


## Psalms 24:4 (id: 1819024004)

4He who has clean hands and a pure heart; who has not lifted up his soul to falsehood, and has not sworn deceitfully.


## Psalms 24:5 (id: 1819024005)

5He shall receive a blessing from the LORD, righteousness from the God of his salvation.


## Psalms 24:6 (id: 1819024006)

6This is the generation of those who seek Him, who seek your face—even Jacob. Selah.


## Psalms 24:7 (id: 1819024007)

7Lift up your heads, you gates! Be lifted up, you everlasting doors, and the King of glory will come in.


## Psalms 24:8 (id: 1819024008)

8Who is the King of glory? The LORD strong and mighty, the LORD mighty in battle.


## Psalms 24:9 (id: 1819024009)

9Lift up your heads, you gates; yes, lift them up, you everlasting doors, and the King of glory will come in.


## Psalms 24:10 (id: 1819024010)

10Who is this King of glory? The LORD of Armies is the King of glory! Selah.


## Psalms 25:1 (id: 1819025001)

1By David. To you, LORD, I lift up my soul.


## Psalms 25:2 (id: 1819025002)

2My God, I have trusted in you. Don’t let me be shamed. Don’t let my enemies triumph over me.


## Psalms 25:3 (id: 1819025003)

3Yes, no one who waits for you will be shamed. They will be shamed who deal treacherously without cause.


## Psalms 25:4 (id: 1819025004)

4Show me your ways, LORD. Teach me your paths.


## Psalms 25:5 (id: 1819025005)

5Guide me in your truth, and teach me, for you are the God of my salvation. I wait for you all day long.


## Psalms 25:6 (id: 1819025006)

6LORD, remember your tender mercies and your loving kindness, for they are from old times.


## Psalms 25:7 (id: 1819025007)

7Don’t remember the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions. Remember me according to your loving kindness, for your goodness’ sake, LORD.


## Psalms 25:8 (id: 1819025008)

8Good and upright is the LORD, therefore he will instruct sinners in the way.


## Psalms 25:9 (id: 1819025009)

9He will guide the humble in justice. He will teach the humble his way.


## Psalms 25:10 (id: 1819025010)

10All the paths of the LORD are loving kindness and truth to such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.


## Psalms 25:11 (id: 1819025011)

11For your name’s sake, LORD, pardon my iniquity, for it is great.


## Psalms 25:12 (id: 1819025012)

12What man is he who fears the LORD? He shall instruct him in the way that he shall choose.


## Psalms 25:13 (id: 1819025013)

13His soul will dwell at ease. His offspring will inherit the land.


## Psalms 25:14 (id: 1819025014)

14The friendship of the LORD is with those who fear him. He will show them his covenant.


## Psalms 25:15 (id: 1819025015)

15My eyes are ever on the LORD, for he will pluck my feet out of the net.


## Psalms 25:16 (id: 1819025016)

16Turn to me, and have mercy on me, for I am desolate and afflicted.


## Psalms 25:17 (id: 1819025017)

17The troubles of my heart are enlarged. Oh bring me out of my distresses.


## Psalms 25:18 (id: 1819025018)

18Consider my affliction and my travail. Forgive all my sins.


## Psalms 25:19 (id: 1819025019)

19Consider my enemies, for they are many. They hate me with cruel hatred.


## Psalms 25:20 (id: 1819025020)

20Oh keep my soul, and deliver me. Let me not be disappointed, for I take refuge in you.


## Psalms 25:21 (id: 1819025021)

21Let integrity and uprightness preserve me, for I wait for you.


## Psalms 25:22 (id: 1819025022)

22God, redeem Israel out of all his troubles.


## Psalms 26:1 (id: 1819026001)

1By David. Judge me, LORD, for I have walked in my integrity. I have trusted also in the LORD without wavering.


## Psalms 26:2 (id: 1819026002)

2Examine me, LORD, and prove me. Try my heart and my mind.


## Psalms 26:3 (id: 1819026003)

3For your loving kindness is before my eyes. I have walked in your truth.


## Psalms 26:4 (id: 1819026004)

4I have not sat with deceitful men, neither will I go in with hypocrites.


## Psalms 26:5 (id: 1819026005)

5I hate the assembly of evildoers, and will not sit with the wicked.


## Psalms 26:6 (id: 1819026006)

6I will wash my hands in innocence, so I will go about your altar, LORD,


## Psalms 26:7 (id: 1819026007)

7that I may make the voice of thanksgiving to be heard and tell of all your wondrous deeds.


## Psalms 26:8 (id: 1819026008)

8LORD, I love the habitation of your house, the place where your glory dwells.


## Psalms 26:9 (id: 1819026009)

9Don’t gather my soul with sinners, nor my life with bloodthirsty men


## Psalms 26:10 (id: 1819026010)

10in whose hands is wickedness; their right hand is full of bribes.


## Psalms 26:11 (id: 1819026011)

11But as for me, I will walk in my integrity. Redeem me, and be merciful to me.


## Psalms 26:12 (id: 1819026012)

12My foot stands in an even place. In the congregations I will bless the LORD.


## Psalms 27:1 (id: 1819027001)

1By David. The LORD is my light and my salvation. Whom shall I fear? The LORD is the strength of my life. Of whom shall I be afraid?


## Psalms 27:2 (id: 1819027002)

2When evildoers came at me to eat up my flesh, even my adversaries and my foes, they stumbled and fell.


## Psalms 27:3 (id: 1819027003)

3Though an army should encamp against me, my heart shall not fear. Though war should rise against me, even then I will be confident.


## Psalms 27:4 (id: 1819027004)

4One thing I have asked of the LORD, that I will seek after: that I may dwell in the LORD’s house all the days of my life, to see the LORD’s beauty, and to inquire in his temple.


## Psalms 27:5 (id: 1819027005)

5For in the day of trouble, he will keep me secretly in his pavilion. In the secret place of his tabernacle, he will hide me. He will lift me up on a rock.


## Psalms 27:6 (id: 1819027006)

6Now my head will be lifted up above my enemies around me. I will offer sacrifices of joy in his tent. I will sing, yes, I will sing praises to the LORD.


## Psalms 27:7 (id: 1819027007)

7Hear, LORD, when I cry with my voice. Have mercy also on me, and answer me.


## Psalms 27:8 (id: 1819027008)

8When you said, “Seek my face,” my heart said to you, “I will seek your face, LORD.”


## Psalms 27:9 (id: 1819027009)

9Don’t hide your face from me. Don’t put your servant away in anger. You have been my help. Don’t abandon me, neither forsake me, God of my salvation.


## Psalms 27:10 (id: 1819027010)

10When my father and my mother forsake me, then the LORD will take me up.


## Psalms 27:11 (id: 1819027011)

11Teach me your way, LORD. Lead me in a straight path, because of my enemies.


## Psalms 27:12 (id: 1819027012)

12Don’t deliver me over to the desire of my adversaries, for false witnesses have risen up against me, such as breathe out cruelty.


## Psalms 27:13 (id: 1819027013)

13I am still confident of this: I will see the goodness of the LORD in the land of the living.


## Psalms 27:14 (id: 1819027014)

14Wait for the LORD. Be strong, and let your heart take courage. Yes, wait for the LORD.


## Psalms 28:1 (id: 1819028001)

1By David. To you, LORD, I call. My rock, don’t be deaf to me, lest, if you are silent to me, I would become like those who go down into the pit.


## Psalms 28:2 (id: 1819028002)

2Hear the voice of my petitions, when I cry to you, when I lift up my hands toward your Most Holy Place.


## Psalms 28:3 (id: 1819028003)

3Don’t draw me away with the wicked, with the workers of iniquity who speak peace with their neighbors, but mischief is in their hearts.


## Psalms 28:4 (id: 1819028004)

4Give them according to their work, and according to the wickedness of their doings. Give them according to the operation of their hands. Bring back on them what they deserve.


## Psalms 28:5 (id: 1819028005)

5Because they don’t respect the works of the LORD, nor the operation of his hands, he will break them down and not build them up.


## Psalms 28:6 (id: 1819028006)

6Blessed be the LORD, because he has heard the voice of my petitions.


## Psalms 28:7 (id: 1819028007)

7The LORD is my strength and my shield. My heart has trusted in him, and I am helped. Therefore my heart greatly rejoices. With my song I will thank him.


## Psalms 28:8 (id: 1819028008)

8The LORD is their strength. He is a stronghold of salvation to his anointed.


## Psalms 28:9 (id: 1819028009)

9Save your people, and bless your inheritance. Be their shepherd also, and bear them up forever.


## Psalms 29:1 (id: 1819029001)

1A Psalm by David. Ascribe to the LORD, you sons of the mighty, ascribe to the LORD glory and strength.


## Psalms 29:2 (id: 1819029002)

2Ascribe to the LORD the glory due to his name. Worship the LORD in holy array.


## Psalms 29:3 (id: 1819029003)

3The LORD’s voice is on the waters. The God of glory thunders, even the LORD on many waters.


## Psalms 29:4 (id: 1819029004)

4The LORD’s voice is powerful. The LORD’s voice is full of majesty.


## Psalms 29:5 (id: 1819029005)

5The LORD’s voice breaks the cedars. Yes, the LORD breaks in pieces the cedars of Lebanon.


## Psalms 29:6 (id: 1819029006)

6He makes them also to skip like a calf; Lebanon and Sirion like a young, wild ox.


## Psalms 29:7 (id: 1819029007)

7The LORD’s voice strikes with flashes of lightning.


## Psalms 29:8 (id: 1819029008)

8The LORD’s voice shakes the wilderness. The LORD shakes the wilderness of Kadesh.


## Psalms 29:9 (id: 1819029009)

9The LORD’s voice makes the deer calve, and strips the forests bare. In his temple everything says, “Glory!”


## Psalms 29:10 (id: 1819029010)

10The LORD sat enthroned at the Flood. Yes, the LORD sits as King forever.


## Psalms 29:11 (id: 1819029011)

11The LORD will give strength to his people. The LORD will bless his people with peace.


## Psalms 30:1 (id: 1819030001)

1A Psalm. A Song for the Dedication of the Temple. By David. I will extol you, LORD, for you have raised me up, and have not made my foes to rejoice over me.


## Psalms 30:2 (id: 1819030002)

2LORD my God, I cried to you, and you have healed me.


## Psalms 30:3 (id: 1819030003)

3LORD, you have brought up my soul from Sheol. You have kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.


## Psalms 30:4 (id: 1819030004)

4Sing praise to the LORD, you saints of his. Give thanks to his holy name.


## Psalms 30:5 (id: 1819030005)

5For his anger is but for a moment. His favor is for a lifetime. Weeping may stay for the night, but joy comes in the morning.


## Psalms 30:6 (id: 1819030006)

6As for me, I said in my prosperity, “I shall never be moved.”


## Psalms 30:7 (id: 1819030007)

7You, LORD, when you favored me, made my mountain stand strong; but when you hid your face, I was troubled.


## Psalms 30:8 (id: 1819030008)

8I cried to you, LORD. I made supplication to the Lord:


## Psalms 30:9 (id: 1819030009)

9“What profit is there in my destruction, if I go down to the pit? Shall the dust praise you? Shall it declare your truth?


## Psalms 30:10 (id: 1819030010)

10Hear, LORD, and have mercy on me. LORD, be my helper.”


## Psalms 30:11 (id: 1819030011)

11You have turned my mourning into dancing for me. You have removed my sackcloth, and clothed me with gladness,


## Psalms 30:12 (id: 1819030012)

12to the end that my heart may sing praise to you, and not be silent. LORD my God, I will give thanks to you forever!


## Psalms 31:1 (id: 1819031001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. In you, LORD, I take refuge. Let me never be disappointed. Deliver me in your righteousness.


## Psalms 31:2 (id: 1819031002)

2Bow down your ear to me. Deliver me speedily. Be to me a strong rock, a house of defense to save me.


## Psalms 31:3 (id: 1819031003)

3For you are my rock and my fortress, therefore for your name’s sake lead me and guide me.


## Psalms 31:4 (id: 1819031004)

4Pluck me out of the net that they have laid secretly for me, for you are my stronghold.


## Psalms 31:5 (id: 1819031005)

5Into your hand I commend my spirit. You redeem me, LORD, God of truth.


## Psalms 31:6 (id: 1819031006)

6I hate those who regard lying vanities, but I trust in the LORD.


## Psalms 31:7 (id: 1819031007)

7I will be glad and rejoice in your loving kindness, for you have seen my affliction. You have known my soul in adversities.


## Psalms 31:8 (id: 1819031008)

8You have not shut me up into the hand of the enemy. You have set my feet in a large place.


## Psalms 31:9 (id: 1819031009)

9Have mercy on me, LORD, for I am in distress. My eye, my soul, and my body waste away with grief.


## Psalms 31:10 (id: 1819031010)

10For my life is spent with sorrow, my years with sighing. My strength fails because of my iniquity. My bones are wasted away.


## Psalms 31:11 (id: 1819031011)

11Because of all my adversaries I have become utterly contemptible to my neighbors, a horror to my acquaintances. Those who saw me on the street fled from me.


## Psalms 31:12 (id: 1819031012)

12I am forgotten from their hearts like a dead man. I am like broken pottery.


## Psalms 31:13 (id: 1819031013)

13For I have heard the slander of many, terror on every side, while they conspire together against me, they plot to take away my life.


## Psalms 31:14 (id: 1819031014)

14But I trust in you, LORD. I said, “You are my God.”


## Psalms 31:15 (id: 1819031015)

15My times are in your hand. Deliver me from the hand of my enemies, and from those who persecute me.


## Psalms 31:16 (id: 1819031016)

16Make your face to shine on your servant. Save me in your loving kindness.


## Psalms 31:17 (id: 1819031017)

17Let me not be disappointed, LORD, for I have called on you. Let the wicked be disappointed. Let them be silent in Sheol.


## Psalms 31:18 (id: 1819031018)

18Let the lying lips be mute, which speak against the righteous insolently, with pride and contempt.


## Psalms 31:19 (id: 1819031019)

19Oh how great is your goodness, which you have laid up for those who fear you, which you have worked for those who take refuge in you, before the sons of men!


## Psalms 31:20 (id: 1819031020)

20In the shelter of your presence you will hide them from the plotting of man. You will keep them secretly in a dwelling away from the strife of tongues.


## Psalms 31:21 (id: 1819031021)

21Praise be to the LORD, for he has shown me his marvelous loving kindness in a strong city.


## Psalms 31:22 (id: 1819031022)

22As for me, I said in my haste, “I am cut off from before your eyes.” Nevertheless you heard the voice of my petitions when I cried to you.


## Psalms 31:23 (id: 1819031023)

23Oh love the LORD, all you his saints! The LORD preserves the faithful, and fully recompenses him who behaves arrogantly.


## Psalms 31:24 (id: 1819031024)

24Be strong, and let your heart take courage, all you who hope in the LORD.


## Psalms 32:1 (id: 1819032001)

1By David. A contemplative psalm. Blessed is he whose disobedience is forgiven, whose sin is covered.


## Psalms 32:2 (id: 1819032002)

2Blessed is the man to whom the LORD doesn’t impute iniquity, in whose spirit there is no deceit.


## Psalms 32:3 (id: 1819032003)

3When I kept silence, my bones wasted away through my groaning all day long.


## Psalms 32:4 (id: 1819032004)

4For day and night your hand was heavy on me. My strength was sapped in the heat of summer. Selah.


## Psalms 32:5 (id: 1819032005)

5I acknowledged my sin to you. I didn’t hide my iniquity. I said, I will confess my transgressions to the LORD, and you forgave the iniquity of my sin. Selah.


## Psalms 32:6 (id: 1819032006)

6For this, let everyone who is godly pray to you in a time when you may be found. Surely when the great waters overflow, they shall not reach to him.


## Psalms 32:7 (id: 1819032007)

7You are my hiding place. You will preserve me from trouble. You will surround me with songs of deliverance. Selah.


## Psalms 32:8 (id: 1819032008)

8I will instruct you and teach you in the way which you shall go. I will counsel you with my eye on you.


## Psalms 32:9 (id: 1819032009)

9Don’t be like the horse, or like the mule, which have no understanding, who are controlled by bit and bridle, or else they will not come near to you.


## Psalms 32:10 (id: 1819032010)

10Many sorrows come to the wicked, but loving kindness shall surround him who trusts in the LORD.


## Psalms 32:11 (id: 1819032011)

11Be glad in the LORD, and rejoice, you righteous! Shout for joy, all you who are upright in heart!


## Psalms 33:1 (id: 1819033001)

1Rejoice in the LORD, you righteous! Praise is fitting for the upright.


## Psalms 33:2 (id: 1819033002)

2Give thanks to the LORD with the lyre. Sing praises to him with the harp of ten strings.


## Psalms 33:3 (id: 1819033003)

3Sing to him a new song. Play skillfully with a shout of joy!


## Psalms 33:4 (id: 1819033004)

4For the LORD’s word is right. All his work is done in faithfulness.


## Psalms 33:5 (id: 1819033005)

5He loves righteousness and justice. The earth is full of the loving kindness of the LORD.


## Psalms 33:6 (id: 1819033006)

6By the LORD’s word, the heavens were made: all their army by the breath of his mouth.


## Psalms 33:7 (id: 1819033007)

7He gathers the waters of the sea together as a heap. He lays up the deeps in storehouses.


## Psalms 33:8 (id: 1819033008)

8Let all the earth fear the LORD. Let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.


## Psalms 33:9 (id: 1819033009)

9For he spoke, and it was done. He commanded, and it stood firm.


## Psalms 33:10 (id: 1819033010)

10The LORD brings the counsel of the nations to nothing. He makes the thoughts of the peoples to be of no effect.


## Psalms 33:11 (id: 1819033011)

11The counsel of the LORD stands fast forever, the thoughts of his heart to all generations.


## Psalms 33:12 (id: 1819033012)

12Blessed is the nation whose God is the LORD, the people whom he has chosen for his own inheritance.


## Psalms 33:13 (id: 1819033013)

13The LORD looks from heaven. He sees all the sons of men.


## Psalms 33:14 (id: 1819033014)

14From the place of his habitation he looks out on all the inhabitants of the earth,


## Psalms 33:15 (id: 1819033015)

15he who fashions all of their hearts; and he considers all of their works.


## Psalms 33:16 (id: 1819033016)

16There is no king saved by the multitude of an army. A mighty man is not delivered by great strength.


## Psalms 33:17 (id: 1819033017)

17A horse is a vain thing for safety, neither does he deliver any by his great power.


## Psalms 33:18 (id: 1819033018)

18Behold, the LORD’s eye is on those who fear him, on those who hope in his loving kindness,


## Psalms 33:19 (id: 1819033019)

19to deliver their soul from death, to keep them alive in famine.


## Psalms 33:20 (id: 1819033020)

20Our soul has waited for the LORD. He is our help and our shield.


## Psalms 33:21 (id: 1819033021)

21For our heart rejoices in him, because we have trusted in his holy name.


## Psalms 33:22 (id: 1819033022)

22Let your loving kindness be on us, LORD, since we have hoped in you.


## Psalms 34:1 (id: 1819034001)

1By David; when he pretended to be insane before Abimelech, who drove him away, and he departed. I will bless the LORD at all times. His praise will always be in my mouth.


## Psalms 34:2 (id: 1819034002)

2My soul shall boast in the LORD. The humble shall hear of it and be glad.


## Psalms 34:3 (id: 1819034003)

3Oh magnify the LORD with me. Let’s exalt his name together.


## Psalms 34:4 (id: 1819034004)

4I sought the LORD, and he answered me, and delivered me from all my fears.


## Psalms 34:5 (id: 1819034005)

5They looked to him, and were radiant. Their faces shall never be covered with shame.


## Psalms 34:6 (id: 1819034006)

6This poor man cried, and the LORD heard him, and saved him out of all his troubles.


## Psalms 34:7 (id: 1819034007)

7The LORD’s angel encamps around those who fear him, and delivers them.


## Psalms 34:8 (id: 1819034008)

8Oh taste and see that the LORD is good. Blessed is the man who takes refuge in him.


## Psalms 34:9 (id: 1819034009)

9Oh fear the LORD, you his saints, for there is no lack with those who fear him.


## Psalms 34:10 (id: 1819034010)

10The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger, but those who seek the LORD shall not lack any good thing.


## Psalms 34:11 (id: 1819034011)

11Come, you children, listen to me. I will teach you the fear of the LORD.


## Psalms 34:12 (id: 1819034012)

12Who is someone who desires life, and loves many days, that he may see good?


## Psalms 34:13 (id: 1819034013)

13Keep your tongue from evil, and your lips from speaking lies.


## Psalms 34:14 (id: 1819034014)

14Depart from evil, and do good. Seek peace, and pursue it.


## Psalms 34:15 (id: 1819034015)

15The LORD’s eyes are toward the righteous. His ears listen to their cry.


## Psalms 34:16 (id: 1819034016)

16The LORD’s face is against those who do evil, to cut off their memory from the earth.


## Psalms 34:17 (id: 1819034017)

17The righteous cry, and the LORD hears, and delivers them out of all their troubles.


## Psalms 34:18 (id: 1819034018)

18The LORD is near to those who have a broken heart, and saves those who have a crushed spirit.


## Psalms 34:19 (id: 1819034019)

19Many are the afflictions of the righteous, but the LORD delivers him out of them all.


## Psalms 34:20 (id: 1819034020)

20He protects all of his bones. Not one of them is broken.


## Psalms 34:21 (id: 1819034021)

21Evil shall kill the wicked. Those who hate the righteous shall be condemned.


## Psalms 34:22 (id: 1819034022)

22The LORD redeems the soul of his servants. None of those who take refuge in him shall be condemned.


## Psalms 35:1 (id: 1819035001)

1By David. Contend, LORD, with those who contend with me. Fight against those who fight against me.


## Psalms 35:2 (id: 1819035002)

2Take hold of shield and buckler, and stand up for my help.


## Psalms 35:3 (id: 1819035003)

3Brandish the spear and block those who pursue me. Tell my soul, “I am your salvation.”


## Psalms 35:4 (id: 1819035004)

4Let those who seek after my soul be disappointed and brought to dishonor. Let those who plot my ruin be turned back and confounded.


## Psalms 35:5 (id: 1819035005)

5Let them be as chaff before the wind, the LORD’s angel driving them on.


## Psalms 35:6 (id: 1819035006)

6Let their way be dark and slippery, the LORD’s angel pursuing them.


## Psalms 35:7 (id: 1819035007)

7For without cause they have hidden their net in a pit for me. Without cause they have dug a pit for my soul.


## Psalms 35:8 (id: 1819035008)

8Let destruction come on him unawares. Let his net that he has hidden catch himself. Let him fall into that destruction.


## Psalms 35:9 (id: 1819035009)

9My soul shall be joyful in the LORD. It shall rejoice in his salvation.


## Psalms 35:10 (id: 1819035010)

10All my bones shall say, “LORD, who is like you, who delivers the poor from him who is too strong for him; yes, the poor and the needy from him who robs him?”


## Psalms 35:11 (id: 1819035011)

11Unrighteous witnesses rise up. They ask me about things that I don’t know about.


## Psalms 35:12 (id: 1819035012)

12They reward me evil for good, to the bereaving of my soul.


## Psalms 35:13 (id: 1819035013)

13But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was sackcloth. I afflicted my soul with fasting. My prayer returned into my own bosom.


## Psalms 35:14 (id: 1819035014)

14I behaved myself as though it had been my friend or my brother. I bowed down mourning, as one who mourns his mother.


## Psalms 35:15 (id: 1819035015)

15But in my adversity, they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together. The attackers gathered themselves together against me, and I didn’t know it. They tore at me, and didn’t cease.


## Psalms 35:16 (id: 1819035016)

16Like the profane mockers in feasts, they gnashed their teeth at me.


## Psalms 35:17 (id: 1819035017)

17Lord, how long will you look on? Rescue my soul from their destruction, my precious life from the lions.


## Psalms 35:18 (id: 1819035018)

18I will give you thanks in the great assembly. I will praise you among many people.


## Psalms 35:19 (id: 1819035019)

19Don’t let those who are my enemies wrongfully rejoice over me; neither let those who hate me without a cause wink their eyes.


## Psalms 35:20 (id: 1819035020)

20For they don’t speak peace, but they devise deceitful words against those who are quiet in the land.


## Psalms 35:21 (id: 1819035021)

21Yes, they opened their mouth wide against me. They said, “Aha! Aha! Our eye has seen it!”


## Psalms 35:22 (id: 1819035022)

22You have seen it, LORD. Don’t keep silent. Lord, don’t be far from me.


## Psalms 35:23 (id: 1819035023)

23Wake up! Rise up to defend me, my God! My Lord, contend for me!


## Psalms 35:24 (id: 1819035024)

24Vindicate me, LORD my God, according to your righteousness. Don’t let them gloat over me.


## Psalms 35:25 (id: 1819035025)

25Don’t let them say in their heart, “Aha! That’s the way we want it!” Don’t let them say, “We have swallowed him up!”


## Psalms 35:26 (id: 1819035026)

26Let them be disappointed and confounded together who rejoice at my calamity. Let them be clothed with shame and dishonor who magnify themselves against me.


## Psalms 35:27 (id: 1819035027)

27Let those who favor my righteous cause shout for joy and be glad. Yes, let them say continually, “May the LORD be magnified, who has pleasure in the prosperity of his servant!”


## Psalms 35:28 (id: 1819035028)

28My tongue shall talk about your righteousness and about your praise all day long.


## Psalms 36:1 (id: 1819036001)

1For the Chief Musician. By David, the servant of the LORD. A revelation is within my heart about the disobedience of the wicked: There is no fear of God before his eyes.


## Psalms 36:2 (id: 1819036002)

2For he flatters himself in his own eyes, too much to detect and hate his sin.


## Psalms 36:3 (id: 1819036003)

3The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit. He has ceased to be wise and to do good.


## Psalms 36:4 (id: 1819036004)

4He plots iniquity on his bed. He sets himself in a way that is not good. He doesn’t abhor evil.


## Psalms 36:5 (id: 1819036005)

5Your loving kindness, LORD, is in the heavens. Your faithfulness reaches to the skies.


## Psalms 36:6 (id: 1819036006)

6Your righteousness is like the mountains of God. Your judgments are like a great deep. LORD, you preserve man and animal.


## Psalms 36:7 (id: 1819036007)

7How precious is your loving kindness, God! The children of men take refuge under the shadow of your wings.


## Psalms 36:8 (id: 1819036008)

8They shall be abundantly satisfied with the abundance of your house. You will make them drink of the river of your pleasures.


## Psalms 36:9 (id: 1819036009)

9For with you is the spring of life. In your light we will see light.


## Psalms 36:10 (id: 1819036010)

10Oh continue your loving kindness to those who know you, your righteousness to the upright in heart.


## Psalms 36:11 (id: 1819036011)

11Don’t let the foot of pride come against me. Don’t let the hand of the wicked drive me away.


## Psalms 36:12 (id: 1819036012)

12There the workers of iniquity are fallen. They are thrust down, and shall not be able to rise.


## Psalms 37:1 (id: 1819037001)

1By David. Don’t fret because of evildoers, neither be envious against those who work unrighteousness.


## Psalms 37:2 (id: 1819037002)

2For they shall soon be cut down like the grass, and wither like the green herb.


## Psalms 37:3 (id: 1819037003)

3Trust in the LORD, and do good. Dwell in the land, and enjoy safe pasture.


## Psalms 37:4 (id: 1819037004)

4Also delight yourself in the LORD, and he will give you the desires of your heart.


## Psalms 37:5 (id: 1819037005)

5Commit your way to the LORD. Trust also in him, and he will do this:


## Psalms 37:6 (id: 1819037006)

6he will make your righteousness shine out like light, and your justice as the noon day sun.


## Psalms 37:7 (id: 1819037007)

7Rest in the LORD, and wait patiently for him. Don’t fret because of him who prospers in his way, because of the man who makes wicked plots happen.


## Psalms 37:8 (id: 1819037008)

8Cease from anger, and forsake wrath. Don’t fret; it leads only to evildoing.


## Psalms 37:9 (id: 1819037009)

9For evildoers shall be cut off, but those who wait for the LORD shall inherit the land.


## Psalms 37:10 (id: 1819037010)

10For yet a little while, and the wicked will be no more. Yes, though you look for his place, he isn’t there.


## Psalms 37:11 (id: 1819037011)

11But the humble shall inherit the land, and shall delight themselves in the abundance of peace.


## Psalms 37:12 (id: 1819037012)

12The wicked plots against the just, and gnashes at him with his teeth.


## Psalms 37:13 (id: 1819037013)

13The Lord will laugh at him, for he sees that his day is coming.


## Psalms 37:14 (id: 1819037014)

14The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their bow, to cast down the poor and needy, to kill those who are upright on the path.


## Psalms 37:15 (id: 1819037015)

15Their sword shall enter into their own heart. Their bows shall be broken.


## Psalms 37:16 (id: 1819037016)

16Better is a little that the righteous has, than the abundance of many wicked.


## Psalms 37:17 (id: 1819037017)

17For the arms of the wicked shall be broken, but the LORD upholds the righteous.


## Psalms 37:18 (id: 1819037018)

18The LORD knows the days of the perfect. Their inheritance shall be forever.


## Psalms 37:19 (id: 1819037019)

19They shall not be disappointed in the time of evil. In the days of famine they shall be satisfied.


## Psalms 37:20 (id: 1819037020)

20But the wicked shall perish. The enemies of the LORD shall be like the beauty of the fields. They will vanish— vanish like smoke.


## Psalms 37:21 (id: 1819037021)

21The wicked borrow, and don’t pay back, but the righteous give generously.


## Psalms 37:22 (id: 1819037022)

22For such as are blessed by him shall inherit the land. Those who are cursed by him shall be cut off.


## Psalms 37:23 (id: 1819037023)

23A man’s steps are established by the LORD. He delights in his way.


## Psalms 37:24 (id: 1819037024)

24Though he stumble, he shall not fall, for the LORD holds him up with his hand.


## Psalms 37:25 (id: 1819037025)

25I have been young, and now am old, yet I have not seen the righteous forsaken, nor his children begging for bread.


## Psalms 37:26 (id: 1819037026)

26All day long he deals graciously, and lends. His offspring is blessed.


## Psalms 37:27 (id: 1819037027)

27Depart from evil, and do good. Live securely forever.


## Psalms 37:28 (id: 1819037028)

28For the LORD loves justice, and doesn’t forsake his saints. They are preserved forever, but the children of the wicked shall be cut off.


## Psalms 37:29 (id: 1819037029)

29The righteous shall inherit the land, and live in it forever.


## Psalms 37:30 (id: 1819037030)

30The mouth of the righteous talks of wisdom. His tongue speaks justice.


## Psalms 37:31 (id: 1819037031)

31The law of his God is in his heart. None of his steps shall slide.


## Psalms 37:32 (id: 1819037032)

32The wicked watch the righteous, and seek to kill him.


## Psalms 37:33 (id: 1819037033)

33The LORD will not leave him in his hand, nor condemn him when he is judged.


## Psalms 37:34 (id: 1819037034)

34Wait for the LORD, and keep his way, and he will exalt you to inherit the land. When the wicked are cut off, you shall see it.


## Psalms 37:35 (id: 1819037035)

35I have seen the wicked in great power, spreading himself like a green tree in its native soil.


## Psalms 37:36 (id: 1819037036)

36But he passed away, and behold, he was not. Yes, I sought him, but he could not be found.


## Psalms 37:37 (id: 1819037037)

37Mark the perfect man, and see the upright, for there is a future for the man of peace.


## Psalms 37:38 (id: 1819037038)

38As for transgressors, they shall be destroyed together. The future of the wicked shall be cut off.


## Psalms 37:39 (id: 1819037039)

39But the salvation of the righteous is from the LORD. He is their stronghold in the time of trouble.


## Psalms 37:40 (id: 1819037040)

40The LORD helps them and rescues them. He rescues them from the wicked and saves them, because they have taken refuge in him.


## Psalms 38:1 (id: 1819038001)

1A Psalm by David, for a memorial. LORD, don’t rebuke me in your wrath, neither chasten me in your hot displeasure.


## Psalms 38:2 (id: 1819038002)

2For your arrows have pierced me, your hand presses hard on me.


## Psalms 38:3 (id: 1819038003)

3There is no soundness in my flesh because of your indignation, neither is there any health in my bones because of my sin.


## Psalms 38:4 (id: 1819038004)

4For my iniquities have gone over my head. As a heavy burden, they are too heavy for me.


## Psalms 38:5 (id: 1819038005)

5My wounds are loathsome and corrupt because of my foolishness.


## Psalms 38:6 (id: 1819038006)

6I am in pain and bowed down greatly. I go mourning all day long.


## Psalms 38:7 (id: 1819038007)

7For my waist is filled with burning. There is no soundness in my flesh.


## Psalms 38:8 (id: 1819038008)

8I am faint and severely bruised. I have groaned by reason of the anguish of my heart.


## Psalms 38:9 (id: 1819038009)

9Lord, all my desire is before you. My groaning is not hidden from you.


## Psalms 38:10 (id: 1819038010)

10My heart throbs. My strength fails me. As for the light of my eyes, it has also left me.


## Psalms 38:11 (id: 1819038011)

11My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my plague. My kinsmen stand far away.


## Psalms 38:12 (id: 1819038012)

12They also who seek after my life lay snares. Those who seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and meditate deceits all day long.


## Psalms 38:13 (id: 1819038013)

13But I, as a deaf man, don’t hear. I am as a mute man who doesn’t open his mouth.


## Psalms 38:14 (id: 1819038014)

14Yes, I am as a man who doesn’t hear, in whose mouth are no reproofs.


## Psalms 38:15 (id: 1819038015)

15For I hope in you, LORD. You will answer, Lord my God.


## Psalms 38:16 (id: 1819038016)

16For I said, “Don’t let them gloat over me, or exalt themselves over me when my foot slips.”


## Psalms 38:17 (id: 1819038017)

17For I am ready to fall. My pain is continually before me.


## Psalms 38:18 (id: 1819038018)

18For I will declare my iniquity. I will be sorry for my sin.


## Psalms 38:19 (id: 1819038019)

19But my enemies are vigorous and many. Those who hate me without reason are numerous.


## Psalms 38:20 (id: 1819038020)

20They who render evil for good are also adversaries to me, because I follow what is good.


## Psalms 38:21 (id: 1819038021)

21Don’t forsake me, LORD. My God, don’t be far from me.


## Psalms 38:22 (id: 1819038022)

22Hurry to help me, Lord, my salvation.


## Psalms 39:1 (id: 1819039001)

1For the Chief Musician. For Jeduthun. A Psalm by David. I said, “I will watch my ways, so that I don’t sin with my tongue. I will keep my mouth with a bridle while the wicked is before me.”


## Psalms 39:2 (id: 1819039002)

2I was mute with silence. I held my peace, even from good. My sorrow was stirred.


## Psalms 39:3 (id: 1819039003)

3My heart was hot within me. While I meditated, the fire burned. I spoke with my tongue:


## Psalms 39:4 (id: 1819039004)

4“LORD, show me my end, what is the measure of my days. Let me know how frail I am.


## Psalms 39:5 (id: 1819039005)

5Behold, you have made my days hand widths. My lifetime is as nothing before you. Surely every man stands as a breath.” Selah.


## Psalms 39:6 (id: 1819039006)

6“Surely every man walks like a shadow. Surely they busy themselves in vain. He heaps up, and doesn’t know who shall gather.


## Psalms 39:7 (id: 1819039007)

7Now, Lord, what do I wait for? My hope is in you.


## Psalms 39:8 (id: 1819039008)

8Deliver me from all my transgressions. Don’t make me the reproach of the foolish.


## Psalms 39:9 (id: 1819039009)

9I was mute. I didn’t open my mouth, because you did it.


## Psalms 39:10 (id: 1819039010)

10Remove your scourge away from me. I am overcome by the blow of your hand.


## Psalms 39:11 (id: 1819039011)

11When you rebuke and correct man for iniquity, you consume his wealth like a moth. Surely every man is but a breath.” Selah.


## Psalms 39:12 (id: 1819039012)

12“Hear my prayer, LORD, and give ear to my cry. Don’t be silent at my tears. For I am a stranger with you, a foreigner, as all my fathers were.


## Psalms 39:13 (id: 1819039013)

13Oh spare me, that I may recover strength, before I go away and exist no more.”


## Psalms 40:1 (id: 1819040001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. I waited patiently for the LORD. He turned to me, and heard my cry.


## Psalms 40:2 (id: 1819040002)

2He brought me up also out of a horrible pit, out of the miry clay. He set my feet on a rock, and gave me a firm place to stand.


## Psalms 40:3 (id: 1819040003)

3He has put a new song in my mouth, even praise to our God. Many shall see it, and fear, and shall trust in the LORD.


## Psalms 40:4 (id: 1819040004)

4Blessed is the man who makes the LORD his trust, and doesn’t respect the proud, nor such as turn away to lies.


## Psalms 40:5 (id: 1819040005)

5Many, LORD, my God, are the wonderful works which you have done, and your thoughts which are toward us. They can’t be declared back to you. If I would declare and speak of them, they are more than can be counted.


## Psalms 40:6 (id: 1819040006)

6Sacrifice and offering you didn’t desire. You have opened my ears. You have not required burnt offering and sin offering.


## Psalms 40:7 (id: 1819040007)

7Then I said, “Behold, I have come. It is written about me in the book in the scroll.


## Psalms 40:8 (id: 1819040008)

8I delight to do your will, my God. Yes, your law is within my heart.”


## Psalms 40:9 (id: 1819040009)

9I have proclaimed glad news of righteousness in the great assembly. Behold, I will not seal my lips, LORD, you know.


## Psalms 40:10 (id: 1819040010)

10I have not hidden your righteousness within my heart. I have declared your faithfulness and your salvation. I have not concealed your loving kindness and your truth from the great assembly.


## Psalms 40:11 (id: 1819040011)

11Don’t withhold your tender mercies from me, LORD. Let your loving kindness and your truth continually preserve me.


## Psalms 40:12 (id: 1819040012)

12For innumerable evils have surrounded me. My iniquities have overtaken me, so that I am not able to look up. They are more than the hairs of my head. My heart has failed me.


## Psalms 40:13 (id: 1819040013)

13Be pleased, LORD, to deliver me. Hurry to help me, LORD.


## Psalms 40:14 (id: 1819040014)
