14Let them be disappointed and confounded together who seek after my soul to destroy it. Let them be turned backward and brought to dishonor who delight in my hurt.


## Psalms 40:15 (id: 1819040015)

15Let them be desolate by reason of their shame that tell me, “Aha! Aha!”


## Psalms 40:16 (id: 1819040016)

16Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you. Let such as love your salvation say continually, “Let the LORD be exalted!”


## Psalms 40:17 (id: 1819040017)

17But I am poor and needy. May the Lord think about me. You are my help and my deliverer. Don’t delay, my God.


## Psalms 41:1 (id: 1819041001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. Blessed is he who considers the poor. The LORD will deliver him in the day of evil.


## Psalms 41:2 (id: 1819041002)

2The LORD will preserve him, and keep him alive. He shall be blessed on the earth, and he will not surrender him to the will of his enemies.


## Psalms 41:3 (id: 1819041003)

3The LORD will sustain him on his sickbed, and restore him from his bed of illness.


## Psalms 41:4 (id: 1819041004)

4I said, “LORD, have mercy on me! Heal me, for I have sinned against you.”


## Psalms 41:5 (id: 1819041005)

5My enemies speak evil against me: “When will he die, and his name perish?”


## Psalms 41:6 (id: 1819041006)

6If he comes to see me, he speaks falsehood. His heart gathers iniquity to itself. When he goes abroad, he tells it.


## Psalms 41:7 (id: 1819041007)

7All who hate me whisper together against me. They imagine the worst for me.


## Psalms 41:8 (id: 1819041008)

8“An evil disease”, they say, “has afflicted him. Now that he lies he shall rise up no more.”


## Psalms 41:9 (id: 1819041009)

9Yes, my own familiar friend, in whom I trusted, who ate bread with me, has lifted up his heel against me.


## Psalms 41:10 (id: 1819041010)

10But you, LORD, have mercy on me, and raise me up, that I may repay them.


## Psalms 41:11 (id: 1819041011)

11By this I know that you delight in me, because my enemy doesn’t triumph over me.


## Psalms 41:12 (id: 1819041012)

12As for me, you uphold me in my integrity, and set me in your presence forever.


## Psalms 41:13 (id: 1819041013)

13Blessed be the LORD, the God of Israel, from everlasting and to everlasting! Amen and amen.


## Psalms 42:1 (id: 1819042001)

1For the Chief Musician. A contemplation by the sons of Korah. As the deer pants for the water brooks, so my soul pants after you, God.


## Psalms 42:2 (id: 1819042002)

2My soul thirsts for God, for the living God. When shall I come and appear before God?


## Psalms 42:3 (id: 1819042003)

3My tears have been my food day and night, while they continually ask me, “Where is your God?”


## Psalms 42:4 (id: 1819042004)

4These things I remember, and pour out my soul within me, how I used to go with the crowd, and led them to God’s house, with the voice of joy and praise, a multitude keeping a holy day.


## Psalms 42:5 (id: 1819042005)

5Why are you in despair, my soul? Why are you disturbed within me? Hope in God! For I shall still praise him for the saving help of his presence.


## Psalms 42:6 (id: 1819042006)

6My God, my soul is in despair within me. Therefore I remember you from the land of the Jordan, the heights of Hermon, from the hill Mizar.


## Psalms 42:7 (id: 1819042007)

7Deep calls to deep at the noise of your waterfalls. All your waves and your billows have swept over me.


## Psalms 42:8 (id: 1819042008)

8GOD will command his loving kindness in the daytime. In the night his song shall be with me: a prayer to the God of my life.


## Psalms 42:9 (id: 1819042009)

9I will ask God, my rock, “Why have you forgotten me? Why do I go mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?”


## Psalms 42:10 (id: 1819042010)

10As with a sword in my bones, my adversaries reproach me, while they continually ask me, “Where is your God?”


## Psalms 42:11 (id: 1819042011)

11Why are you in despair, my soul? Why are you disturbed within me? Hope in God! For I shall still praise him, the saving help of my countenance, and my God.


## Psalms 43:1 (id: 1819043001)

1Vindicate me, God, and plead my cause against an ungodly nation. Oh, deliver me from deceitful and wicked men.


## Psalms 43:2 (id: 1819043002)

2For you are the God of my strength. Why have you rejected me? Why do I go mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?


## Psalms 43:3 (id: 1819043003)

3Oh, send out your light and your truth. Let them lead me. Let them bring me to your holy hill, to your tents.


## Psalms 43:4 (id: 1819043004)

4Then I will go to the altar of God, to God, my exceeding joy. I will praise you on the harp, God, my God.


## Psalms 43:5 (id: 1819043005)

5Why are you in despair, my soul? Why are you disturbed within me? Hope in God! For I shall still praise him: my Savior, my helper, and my God.


## Psalms 44:1 (id: 1819044001)

1For the Chief Musician. By the sons of Korah. A contemplative psalm. We have heard with our ears, God; our fathers have told us what work you did in their days, in the days of old.


## Psalms 44:2 (id: 1819044002)

2You drove out the nations with your hand, but you planted them. You afflicted the peoples, but you spread them abroad.


## Psalms 44:3 (id: 1819044003)

3For they didn’t get the land in possession by their own sword, neither did their own arm save them; but your right hand, your arm, and the light of your face, because you were favorable to them.


## Psalms 44:4 (id: 1819044004)

4God, you are my King. Command victories for Jacob!


## Psalms 44:5 (id: 1819044005)

5Through you, we will push down our adversaries. Through your name, we will tread down those who rise up against us.


## Psalms 44:6 (id: 1819044006)

6For I will not trust in my bow, neither will my sword save me.


## Psalms 44:7 (id: 1819044007)

7But you have saved us from our adversaries, and have shamed those who hate us.


## Psalms 44:8 (id: 1819044008)

8In God we have made our boast all day long. We will give thanks to your name forever. Selah.


## Psalms 44:9 (id: 1819044009)

9But now you rejected us, and brought us to dishonor, and don’t go out with our armies.


## Psalms 44:10 (id: 1819044010)

10You make us turn back from the adversary. Those who hate us take plunder for themselves.


## Psalms 44:11 (id: 1819044011)

11You have made us like sheep for food, and have scattered us among the nations.


## Psalms 44:12 (id: 1819044012)

12You sell your people for nothing, and have gained nothing from their sale.


## Psalms 44:13 (id: 1819044013)

13You make us a reproach to our neighbors, a scoffing and a derision to those who are around us.


## Psalms 44:14 (id: 1819044014)

14You make us a byword among the nations, a shaking of the head among the peoples.


## Psalms 44:15 (id: 1819044015)

15All day long my dishonor is before me, and shame covers my face,


## Psalms 44:16 (id: 1819044016)

16at the taunt of one who reproaches and verbally abuses, because of the enemy and the avenger.


## Psalms 44:17 (id: 1819044017)

17All this has come on us, yet we haven’t forgotten you. We haven’t been false to your covenant.


## Psalms 44:18 (id: 1819044018)

18Our heart has not turned back, neither have our steps strayed from your path,


## Psalms 44:19 (id: 1819044019)

19though you have crushed us in the haunt of jackals, and covered us with the shadow of death.


## Psalms 44:20 (id: 1819044020)

20If we have forgotten the name of our God, or spread out our hands to a strange god,


## Psalms 44:21 (id: 1819044021)

21won’t God search this out? For he knows the secrets of the heart.


## Psalms 44:22 (id: 1819044022)

22Yes, for your sake we are killed all day long. We are regarded as sheep for the slaughter.


## Psalms 44:23 (id: 1819044023)

23Wake up! Why do you sleep, Lord? Arise! Don’t reject us forever.


## Psalms 44:24 (id: 1819044024)

24Why do you hide your face, and forget our affliction and our oppression?


## Psalms 44:25 (id: 1819044025)

25For our soul is bowed down to the dust. Our body clings to the earth.


## Psalms 44:26 (id: 1819044026)

26Rise up to help us. Redeem us for your loving kindness’ sake.


## Psalms 45:1 (id: 1819045001)

1For the Chief Musician. Set to “The Lilies.” A contemplation by the sons of Korah. A wedding song. My heart overflows with a noble theme. I recite my verses for the king. My tongue is like the pen of a skillful writer.


## Psalms 45:2 (id: 1819045002)

2You are the most excellent of the sons of men. Grace has anointed your lips, therefore God has blessed you forever.


## Psalms 45:3 (id: 1819045003)

3Strap your sword on your thigh, O mighty one, in your splendor and your majesty.


## Psalms 45:4 (id: 1819045004)

4In your majesty ride on victoriously on behalf of truth, humility, and righteousness. Let your right hand display awesome deeds.


## Psalms 45:5 (id: 1819045005)

5Your arrows are sharp. The nations fall under you, with arrows in the heart of the king’s enemies.


## Psalms 45:6 (id: 1819045006)

6Your throne, God, is forever and ever. A scepter of equity is the scepter of your kingdom.


## Psalms 45:7 (id: 1819045007)

7You have loved righteousness, and hated wickedness. Therefore God, your God, has anointed you with the oil of gladness above your fellows.


## Psalms 45:8 (id: 1819045008)

8All your garments smell like myrrh, aloes, and cassia. Out of ivory palaces stringed instruments have made you glad.


## Psalms 45:9 (id: 1819045009)

9Kings’ daughters are among your honorable women. At your right hand the queen stands in gold of Ophir.


## Psalms 45:10 (id: 1819045010)

10Listen, daughter, consider, and turn your ear. Forget your own people, and also your father’s house.


## Psalms 45:11 (id: 1819045011)

11So the king will desire your beauty, honor him, for he is your lord.


## Psalms 45:12 (id: 1819045012)

12The daughter of Tyre comes with a gift. The rich among the people entreat your favor.


## Psalms 45:13 (id: 1819045013)

13The princess inside is all glorious. Her clothing is interwoven with gold.


## Psalms 45:14 (id: 1819045014)

14She shall be led to the king in embroidered work. The virgins, her companions who follow her, shall be brought to you.


## Psalms 45:15 (id: 1819045015)

15With gladness and rejoicing they shall be led. They shall enter into the king’s palace.


## Psalms 45:16 (id: 1819045016)

16Your sons will take the place of your fathers. You shall make them princes in all the earth.


## Psalms 45:17 (id: 1819045017)

17I will make your name to be remembered in all generations. Therefore the peoples shall give you thanks forever and ever.


## Psalms 46:1 (id: 1819046001)

1For the Chief Musician. By the sons of Korah. According to Alamoth. God is our refuge and strength, a very present help in trouble.


## Psalms 46:2 (id: 1819046002)

2Therefore we won’t be afraid, though the earth changes, though the mountains are shaken into the heart of the seas;


## Psalms 46:3 (id: 1819046003)

3though its waters roar and are troubled, though the mountains tremble with their swelling. Selah.


## Psalms 46:4 (id: 1819046004)

4There is a river, the streams of which make the city of God glad, the holy place of the tents of the Most High.


## Psalms 46:5 (id: 1819046005)

5God is within her. She shall not be moved. God will help her at dawn.


## Psalms 46:6 (id: 1819046006)

6The nations raged. The kingdoms were moved. He lifted his voice and the earth melted.


## Psalms 46:7 (id: 1819046007)

7The LORD of Armies is with us. The God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah.


## Psalms 46:8 (id: 1819046008)

8Come, see the LORD’s works, what desolations he has made in the earth.


## Psalms 46:9 (id: 1819046009)

9He makes wars cease to the end of the earth. He breaks the bow, and shatters the spear. He burns the chariots in the fire.


## Psalms 46:10 (id: 1819046010)

10“Be still, and know that I am God. I will be exalted among the nations. I will be exalted in the earth.”


## Psalms 46:11 (id: 1819046011)

11The LORD of Armies is with us. The God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah.


## Psalms 47:1 (id: 1819047001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. Oh clap your hands, all you nations. Shout to God with the voice of triumph!


## Psalms 47:2 (id: 1819047002)

2For the LORD Most High is awesome. He is a great King over all the earth.


## Psalms 47:3 (id: 1819047003)

3He subdues nations under us, and peoples under our feet.


## Psalms 47:4 (id: 1819047004)

4He chooses our inheritance for us, the glory of Jacob whom he loved. Selah.


## Psalms 47:5 (id: 1819047005)

5God has gone up with a shout, the LORD with the sound of a trumpet.


## Psalms 47:6 (id: 1819047006)

6Sing praises to God! Sing praises! Sing praises to our King! Sing praises!


## Psalms 47:7 (id: 1819047007)

7For God is the King of all the earth. Sing praises with understanding.


## Psalms 47:8 (id: 1819047008)

8God reigns over the nations. God sits on his holy throne.


## Psalms 47:9 (id: 1819047009)

9The princes of the peoples are gathered together, the people of the God of Abraham. For the shields of the earth belong to God. He is greatly exalted!


## Psalms 48:1 (id: 1819048001)

1A Song. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised, in the city of our God, in his holy mountain.


## Psalms 48:2 (id: 1819048002)

2Beautiful in elevation, the joy of the whole earth, is Mount Zion, on the north sides, the city of the great King.


## Psalms 48:3 (id: 1819048003)

3God has shown himself in her citadels as a refuge.


## Psalms 48:4 (id: 1819048004)

4For, behold, the kings assembled themselves, they passed by together.


## Psalms 48:5 (id: 1819048005)

5They saw it, then they were amazed. They were dismayed. They hurried away.


## Psalms 48:6 (id: 1819048006)

6Trembling took hold of them there, pain, as of a woman in travail.


## Psalms 48:7 (id: 1819048007)

7With the east wind, you break the ships of Tarshish.


## Psalms 48:8 (id: 1819048008)

8As we have heard, so we have seen, in the city of the LORD of Armies, in the city of our God. God will establish it forever. Selah.


## Psalms 48:9 (id: 1819048009)

9We have thought about your loving kindness, God, in the middle of your temple.


## Psalms 48:10 (id: 1819048010)

10As is your name, God, so is your praise to the ends of the earth. Your right hand is full of righteousness.


## Psalms 48:11 (id: 1819048011)

11Let Mount Zion be glad! Let the daughters of Judah rejoice because of your judgments.


## Psalms 48:12 (id: 1819048012)

12Walk about Zion, and go around her. Number its towers.


## Psalms 48:13 (id: 1819048013)

13Notice her bulwarks. Consider her palaces, that you may tell it to the next generation.


## Psalms 48:14 (id: 1819048014)

14For this God is our God forever and ever. He will be our guide even to death.


## Psalms 49:1 (id: 1819049001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. Hear this, all you peoples. Listen, all you inhabitants of the world,


## Psalms 49:2 (id: 1819049002)

2both low and high, rich and poor together.


## Psalms 49:3 (id: 1819049003)

3My mouth will speak words of wisdom. My heart will utter understanding.


## Psalms 49:4 (id: 1819049004)

4I will incline my ear to a proverb. I will solve my riddle on the harp.


## Psalms 49:5 (id: 1819049005)

5Why should I fear in the days of evil, when iniquity at my heels surrounds me?


## Psalms 49:6 (id: 1819049006)

6Those who trust in their wealth, and boast in the multitude of their riches—


## Psalms 49:7 (id: 1819049007)

7none of them can by any means redeem his brother, nor give God a ransom for him.


## Psalms 49:8 (id: 1819049008)

8For the redemption of their life is costly, no payment is ever enough,


## Psalms 49:9 (id: 1819049009)

9that he should live on forever, that he should not see corruption.


## Psalms 49:10 (id: 1819049010)

10For he sees that wise men die; likewise the fool and the senseless perish, and leave their wealth to others.


## Psalms 49:11 (id: 1819049011)

11Their inward thought is that their houses will endure forever, and their dwelling places to all generations. They name their lands after themselves.


## Psalms 49:12 (id: 1819049012)

12But man, despite his riches, doesn’t endure. He is like the animals that perish.


## Psalms 49:13 (id: 1819049013)

13This is the destiny of those who are foolish, and of those who approve their sayings. Selah.


## Psalms 49:14 (id: 1819049014)

14They are appointed as a flock for Sheol. Death shall be their shepherd. The upright shall have dominion over them in the morning. Their beauty shall decay in Sheol, far from their mansion.


## Psalms 49:15 (id: 1819049015)

15But God will redeem my soul from the power of Sheol, for he will receive me. Selah.


## Psalms 49:16 (id: 1819049016)

16Don’t be afraid when a man is made rich, when the glory of his house is increased;


## Psalms 49:17 (id: 1819049017)

17for when he dies he will carry nothing away. His glory won’t descend after him.


## Psalms 49:18 (id: 1819049018)

18Though while he lived he blessed his soul— and men praise you when you do well for yourself—


## Psalms 49:19 (id: 1819049019)

19he shall go to the generation of his fathers. They shall never see the light.


## Psalms 49:20 (id: 1819049020)

20A man who has riches without understanding, is like the animals that perish.


## Psalms 50:1 (id: 1819050001)

1A Psalm by Asaph. The Mighty One, God, the LORD, speaks, and calls the earth from sunrise to sunset.


## Psalms 50:2 (id: 1819050002)

2Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God shines out.


## Psalms 50:3 (id: 1819050003)

3Our God comes, and does not keep silent. A fire devours before him. It is very stormy around him.


## Psalms 50:4 (id: 1819050004)

4He calls to the heavens above, to the earth, that he may judge his people:


## Psalms 50:5 (id: 1819050005)

5“Gather my saints together to me, those who have made a covenant with me by sacrifice.”


## Psalms 50:6 (id: 1819050006)

6The heavens shall declare his righteousness, for God himself is judge. Selah.


## Psalms 50:7 (id: 1819050007)

7“Hear, my people, and I will speak. Israel, I will testify against you. I am God, your God.


## Psalms 50:8 (id: 1819050008)

8I don’t rebuke you for your sacrifices. Your burnt offerings are continually before me.


## Psalms 50:9 (id: 1819050009)

9I have no need for a bull from your stall, nor male goats from your pens.


## Psalms 50:10 (id: 1819050010)

10For every animal of the forest is mine, and the livestock on a thousand hills.


## Psalms 50:11 (id: 1819050011)

11I know all the birds of the mountains. The wild animals of the field are mine.


## Psalms 50:12 (id: 1819050012)

12If I were hungry, I would not tell you, for the world is mine, and all that is in it.


## Psalms 50:13 (id: 1819050013)

13Will I eat the meat of bulls, or drink the blood of goats?


## Psalms 50:14 (id: 1819050014)

14Offer to God the sacrifice of thanksgiving. Pay your vows to the Most High.


## Psalms 50:15 (id: 1819050015)

15Call on me in the day of trouble. I will deliver you, and you will honor me.”


## Psalms 50:16 (id: 1819050016)

16But to the wicked God says, “What right do you have to declare my statutes, that you have taken my covenant on your lips,


## Psalms 50:17 (id: 1819050017)

17since you hate instruction, and throw my words behind you?


## Psalms 50:18 (id: 1819050018)

18When you saw a thief, you consented with him, and have participated with adulterers.


## Psalms 50:19 (id: 1819050019)

19“You give your mouth to evil. Your tongue frames deceit.


## Psalms 50:20 (id: 1819050020)

20You sit and speak against your brother. You slander your own mother’s son.


## Psalms 50:21 (id: 1819050021)

21You have done these things, and I kept silent. You thought that I was just like you. I will rebuke you, and accuse you in front of your eyes.


## Psalms 50:22 (id: 1819050022)

22“Now consider this, you who forget God, lest I tear you into pieces, and there be no one to deliver.


## Psalms 50:23 (id: 1819050023)

23Whoever offers the sacrifice of thanksgiving glorifies me, and prepares his way so that I will show God’s salvation to him.”


## Psalms 51:1 (id: 1819051001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David, when Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bathsheba. Have mercy on me, God, according to your loving kindness. According to the multitude of your tender mercies, blot out my transgressions.


## Psalms 51:2 (id: 1819051002)

2Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity. Cleanse me from my sin.


## Psalms 51:3 (id: 1819051003)

3For I know my transgressions. My sin is constantly before me.


## Psalms 51:4 (id: 1819051004)

4Against you, and you only, I have sinned, and done that which is evil in your sight, so you may be proved right when you speak, and justified when you judge.


## Psalms 51:5 (id: 1819051005)

5Behold, I was born in iniquity. My mother conceived me in sin.


## Psalms 51:6 (id: 1819051006)

6Behold, you desire truth in the inward parts. You teach me wisdom in the inmost place.


## Psalms 51:7 (id: 1819051007)

7Purify me with hyssop, and I will be clean. Wash me, and I will be whiter than snow.


## Psalms 51:8 (id: 1819051008)

8Let me hear joy and gladness, that the bones which you have broken may rejoice.


## Psalms 51:9 (id: 1819051009)

9Hide your face from my sins, and blot out all of my iniquities.


## Psalms 51:10 (id: 1819051010)

10Create in me a clean heart, O God. Renew a right spirit within me.


## Psalms 51:11 (id: 1819051011)

11Don’t throw me from your presence, and don’t take your Holy Spirit from me.


## Psalms 51:12 (id: 1819051012)

12Restore to me the joy of your salvation. Uphold me with a willing spirit.


## Psalms 51:13 (id: 1819051013)

13Then I will teach transgressors your ways. Sinners will be converted to you.


## Psalms 51:14 (id: 1819051014)

14Deliver me from the guilt of bloodshed, O God, the God of my salvation. My tongue will sing aloud of your righteousness.


## Psalms 51:15 (id: 1819051015)

15Lord, open my lips. My mouth will declare your praise.


## Psalms 51:16 (id: 1819051016)

16For you don’t delight in sacrifice, or else I would give it. You have no pleasure in burnt offering.


## Psalms 51:17 (id: 1819051017)

17The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit. O God, you will not despise a broken and contrite heart.


## Psalms 51:18 (id: 1819051018)

18Do well in your good pleasure to Zion. Build the walls of Jerusalem.


## Psalms 51:19 (id: 1819051019)

19Then you will delight in the sacrifices of righteousness, in burnt offerings and in whole burnt offerings. Then they will offer bulls on your altar.


## Psalms 52:1 (id: 1819052001)

1For the Chief Musician. A contemplation by David, when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, “David has come to Ahimelech’s house.” Why do you boast of mischief, mighty man? God’s loving kindness endures continually.


## Psalms 52:2 (id: 1819052002)

2Your tongue plots destruction, like a sharp razor, working deceitfully.


## Psalms 52:3 (id: 1819052003)

3You love evil more than good, lying rather than speaking the truth. Selah.


## Psalms 52:4 (id: 1819052004)

4You love all devouring words, you deceitful tongue.


## Psalms 52:5 (id: 1819052005)

5God will likewise destroy you forever. He will take you up, and pluck you out of your tent, and root you out of the land of the living. Selah.


## Psalms 52:6 (id: 1819052006)

6The righteous also will see it, and fear, and laugh at him, saying,


## Psalms 52:7 (id: 1819052007)

7“Behold, this is the man who didn’t make God his strength, but trusted in the abundance of his riches, and strengthened himself in his wickedness.”


## Psalms 52:8 (id: 1819052008)

8But as for me, I am like a green olive tree in God’s house. I trust in God’s loving kindness forever and ever.


## Psalms 52:9 (id: 1819052009)

9I will give you thanks forever, because you have done it. I will hope in your name, for it is good, in the presence of your saints.


## Psalms 53:1 (id: 1819053001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Mahalath.” A contemplation by David. The fool has said in his heart, “There is no God.” They are corrupt, and have done abominable iniquity. There is no one who does good.


## Psalms 53:2 (id: 1819053002)

2God looks down from heaven on the children of men, to see if there are any who understood, who seek after God.


## Psalms 53:3 (id: 1819053003)

3Every one of them has gone back. They have become filthy together. There is no one who does good, no, not one.


## Psalms 53:4 (id: 1819053004)

4Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge, who eat up my people as they eat bread, and don’t call on God?


## Psalms 53:5 (id: 1819053005)

5There they were in great fear, where no fear was, for God has scattered the bones of him who encamps against you. You have put them to shame, because God has rejected them.


## Psalms 53:6 (id: 1819053006)

6Oh that the salvation of Israel would come out of Zion! When God brings back his people from captivity, then Jacob shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad.


## Psalms 54:1 (id: 1819054001)

1For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A contemplation by David, when the Ziphites came and said to Saul, “Isn’t David hiding himself among us?” Save me, God, by your name. Vindicate me in your might.


## Psalms 54:2 (id: 1819054002)

2Hear my prayer, God. Listen to the words of my mouth.


## Psalms 54:3 (id: 1819054003)

3For strangers have risen up against me. Violent men have sought after my soul. They haven’t set God before them. Selah.


## Psalms 54:4 (id: 1819054004)

4Behold, God is my helper. The Lord is the one who sustains my soul.


## Psalms 54:5 (id: 1819054005)

5He will repay the evil to my enemies. Destroy them in your truth.


## Psalms 54:6 (id: 1819054006)

6With a free will offering, I will sacrifice to you. I will give thanks to your name, LORD, for it is good.


## Psalms 54:7 (id: 1819054007)

7For he has delivered me out of all trouble. My eye has seen triumph over my enemies.


## Psalms 55:1 (id: 1819055001)

1For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A contemplation by David. Listen to my prayer, God. Don’t hide yourself from my supplication.


## Psalms 55:2 (id: 1819055002)

2Attend to me, and answer me. I am restless in my complaint, and moan


## Psalms 55:3 (id: 1819055003)

3because of the voice of the enemy, because of the oppression of the wicked. For they bring suffering on me. In anger they hold a grudge against me.


## Psalms 55:4 (id: 1819055004)

4My heart is severely pained within me. The terrors of death have fallen on me.


## Psalms 55:5 (id: 1819055005)

5Fearfulness and trembling have come on me. Horror has overwhelmed me.


## Psalms 55:6 (id: 1819055006)

6I said, “Oh that I had wings like a dove! Then I would fly away, and be at rest.


## Psalms 55:7 (id: 1819055007)

7Behold, then I would wander far off. I would lodge in the wilderness.” Selah.


## Psalms 55:8 (id: 1819055008)

8“I would hurry to a shelter from the stormy wind and storm.”


## Psalms 55:9 (id: 1819055009)

9Confuse them, Lord, and confound their language, for I have seen violence and strife in the city.


## Psalms 55:10 (id: 1819055010)

10Day and night they prowl around on its walls. Malice and abuse are also within her.


## Psalms 55:11 (id: 1819055011)

11Destructive forces are within her. Threats and lies don’t depart from her streets.


## Psalms 55:12 (id: 1819055012)

12For it was not an enemy who insulted me, then I could have endured it. Neither was it he who hated me who raised himself up against me, then I would have hidden myself from him.


## Psalms 55:13 (id: 1819055013)

13But it was you, a man like me, my companion, and my familiar friend.


## Psalms 55:14 (id: 1819055014)

14We took sweet fellowship together. We walked in God’s house with company.


## Psalms 55:15 (id: 1819055015)

15Let death come suddenly on them. Let them go down alive into Sheol. For wickedness is among them, in their dwelling.


## Psalms 55:16 (id: 1819055016)

16As for me, I will call on God. The LORD will save me.


## Psalms 55:17 (id: 1819055017)

17Evening, morning, and at noon, I will cry out in distress. He will hear my voice.


## Psalms 55:18 (id: 1819055018)

18He has redeemed my soul in peace from the battle that was against me, although there are many who oppose me.


## Psalms 55:19 (id: 1819055019)

19God, who is enthroned forever, will hear and answer them. Selah. They never change and don’t fear God.


## Psalms 55:20 (id: 1819055020)

20He raises his hands against his friends. He has violated his covenant.


## Psalms 55:21 (id: 1819055021)

21His mouth was smooth as butter, but his heart was war. His words were softer than oil, yet they were drawn swords.


## Psalms 55:22 (id: 1819055022)

22Cast your burden on the LORD and he will sustain you. He will never allow the righteous to be moved.


## Psalms 55:23 (id: 1819055023)

23But you, God, will bring them down into the pit of destruction. Bloodthirsty and deceitful men shall not live out half their days, but I will trust in you.


## Psalms 56:1 (id: 1819056001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Silent Dove in Distant Lands.” A poem by David, when the Philistines seized him in Gath. Be merciful to me, God, for man wants to swallow me up. All day long, he attacks and oppresses me.


## Psalms 56:2 (id: 1819056002)

2My enemies want to swallow me up all day long, for they are many who fight proudly against me.


## Psalms 56:3 (id: 1819056003)

3When I am afraid, I will put my trust in you.


## Psalms 56:4 (id: 1819056004)

4In God, I praise his word. In God, I put my trust. I will not be afraid. What can flesh do to me?


## Psalms 56:5 (id: 1819056005)

5All day long they twist my words. All their thoughts are against me for evil.


## Psalms 56:6 (id: 1819056006)

6They conspire and lurk, watching my steps. They are eager to take my life.


## Psalms 56:7 (id: 1819056007)

7Shall they escape by iniquity? In anger cast down the peoples, God.


## Psalms 56:8 (id: 1819056008)

8You count my wanderings. You put my tears into your container. Aren’t they in your book?


## Psalms 56:9 (id: 1819056009)

9Then my enemies shall turn back in the day that I call. I know this: that God is for me.


## Psalms 56:10 (id: 1819056010)

10In God, I will praise his word. In the LORD, I will praise his word.


## Psalms 56:11 (id: 1819056011)

11I have put my trust in God. I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?


## Psalms 56:12 (id: 1819056012)

12Your vows are on me, God. I will give thank offerings to you.


## Psalms 56:13 (id: 1819056013)

13For you have delivered my soul from death, and prevented my feet from falling, that I may walk before God in the light of the living.


## Psalms 57:1 (id: 1819057001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David, when he fled from Saul, in the cave. Be merciful to me, God, be merciful to me, for my soul takes refuge in you. Yes, in the shadow of your wings, I will take refuge, until disaster has passed.


## Psalms 57:2 (id: 1819057002)

2I cry out to God Most High, to God who accomplishes my requests for me.


## Psalms 57:3 (id: 1819057003)

3He will send from heaven, and save me, he rebukes the one who is pursuing me. Selah. God will send out his loving kindness and his truth.


## Psalms 57:4 (id: 1819057004)

4My soul is among lions. I lie among those who are set on fire, even the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword.


## Psalms 57:5 (id: 1819057005)

5Be exalted, God, above the heavens! Let your glory be above all the earth!


## Psalms 57:6 (id: 1819057006)

6They have prepared a net for my steps. My soul is bowed down. They dig a pit before me. They fall into the middle of it themselves. Selah.


## Psalms 57:7 (id: 1819057007)

7My heart is steadfast, God. My heart is steadfast. I will sing, yes, I will sing praises.


## Psalms 57:8 (id: 1819057008)

8Wake up, my glory! Wake up, lute and harp! I will wake up the dawn.


## Psalms 57:9 (id: 1819057009)

9I will give thanks to you, Lord, among the peoples. I will sing praises to you among the nations.


## Psalms 57:10 (id: 1819057010)

10For your great loving kindness reaches to the heavens, and your truth to the skies.


## Psalms 57:11 (id: 1819057011)

11Be exalted, God, above the heavens. Let your glory be over all the earth.


## Psalms 58:1 (id: 1819058001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David. Do you indeed speak righteousness, silent ones? Do you judge blamelessly, you sons of men?


## Psalms 58:2 (id: 1819058002)

2No, in your heart you plot injustice. You measure out the violence of your hands in the earth.


## Psalms 58:3 (id: 1819058003)

3The wicked go astray from the womb. They are wayward as soon as they are born, speaking lies.


## Psalms 58:4 (id: 1819058004)

4Their poison is like the poison of a snake, like a deaf cobra that stops its ear,


## Psalms 58:5 (id: 1819058005)

5which doesn’t listen to the voice of charmers, no matter how skillful the charmer may be.


## Psalms 58:6 (id: 1819058006)

6Break their teeth, God, in their mouth. Break out the great teeth of the young lions, LORD.


## Psalms 58:7 (id: 1819058007)

7Let them vanish like water that flows away. When they draw the bow, let their arrows be made blunt.


## Psalms 58:8 (id: 1819058008)

8Let them be like a snail which melts and passes away, like the stillborn child, who has not seen the sun.


## Psalms 58:9 (id: 1819058009)

9Before your pots can feel the heat of the thorns, he will sweep away the green and the burning alike.


## Psalms 58:10 (id: 1819058010)

10The righteous shall rejoice when he sees the vengeance. He shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked,


## Psalms 58:11 (id: 1819058011)

11so that men shall say, “Most certainly there is a reward for the righteous. Most certainly there is a God who judges the earth.”


## Psalms 59:1 (id: 1819059001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David, when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him. Deliver me from my enemies, my God. Set me on high from those who rise up against me.


## Psalms 59:2 (id: 1819059002)

2Deliver me from the workers of iniquity. Save me from the bloodthirsty men.


## Psalms 59:3 (id: 1819059003)

3For, behold, they lie in wait for my soul. The mighty gather themselves together against me, not for my disobedience, nor for my sin, LORD.


## Psalms 59:4 (id: 1819059004)

4I have done no wrong, yet they are ready to attack me. Rise up, behold, and help me!


## Psalms 59:5 (id: 1819059005)

5You, LORD God of Armies, the God of Israel, rouse yourself to punish the nations. Show no mercy to the wicked traitors. Selah.


## Psalms 59:6 (id: 1819059006)

6They return at evening, howling like dogs, and prowl around the city.


## Psalms 59:7 (id: 1819059007)

7Behold, they spew with their mouth. Swords are in their lips, “For”, they say, “who hears us?”


## Psalms 59:8 (id: 1819059008)

8But you, LORD, laugh at them. You scoff at all the nations.


## Psalms 59:9 (id: 1819059009)

9Oh, my Strength, I watch for you, for God is my high tower.


## Psalms 59:10 (id: 1819059010)

10My God will go before me with his loving kindness. God will let me look at my enemies in triumph.


## Psalms 59:11 (id: 1819059011)

11Don’t kill them, or my people may forget. Scatter them by your power, and bring them down, Lord our shield.


## Psalms 59:12 (id: 1819059012)

12For the sin of their mouth, and the words of their lips, let them be caught in their pride, for the curses and lies which they utter.


## Psalms 59:13 (id: 1819059013)

13Consume them in wrath. Consume them, and they will be no more. Let them know that God rules in Jacob, to the ends of the earth. Selah.


## Psalms 59:14 (id: 1819059014)

14At evening let them return. Let them howl like a dog, and go around the city.


## Psalms 59:15 (id: 1819059015)

15They shall wander up and down for food, and wait all night if they aren’t satisfied.


## Psalms 59:16 (id: 1819059016)

16But I will sing of your strength. Yes, I will sing aloud of your loving kindness in the morning. For you have been my high tower, a refuge in the day of my distress.


## Psalms 59:17 (id: 1819059017)

17To you, my strength, I will sing praises. For God is my high tower, the God of my mercy.


## Psalms 60:1 (id: 1819060001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Lily of the Covenant.” A teaching poem by David, when he fought with Aram Naharaim and with Aram Zobah, and Joab returned, and killed twelve thousand of Edom in the Valley of Salt. God, you have rejected us. You have broken us down. You have been angry. Restore us, again.


## Psalms 60:2 (id: 1819060002)

2You have made the land tremble. You have torn it. Mend its fractures, for it quakes.


## Psalms 60:3 (id: 1819060003)

3You have shown your people hard things. You have made us drink the wine that makes us stagger.


## Psalms 60:4 (id: 1819060004)

4You have given a banner to those who fear you, that it may be displayed because of the truth. Selah.


## Psalms 60:5 (id: 1819060005)

5So that your beloved may be delivered, save with your right hand, and answer us.


## Psalms 60:6 (id: 1819060006)

6God has spoken from his sanctuary: “I will triumph. I will divide Shechem, and measure out the valley of Succoth.


## Psalms 60:7 (id: 1819060007)

7Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine. Ephraim also is the defense of my head. Judah is my scepter.


## Psalms 60:8 (id: 1819060008)

8Moab is my wash basin. I will throw my sandal on Edom. I shout in triumph over Philistia.”


## Psalms 60:9 (id: 1819060009)

9Who will bring me into the strong city? Who has led me to Edom?


## Psalms 60:10 (id: 1819060010)

10Haven’t you, God, rejected us? You don’t go out with our armies, God.


## Psalms 60:11 (id: 1819060011)

11Give us help against the adversary, for the help of man is vain.


## Psalms 60:12 (id: 1819060012)

12Through God we will do valiantly, for it is he who will tread down our adversaries.


## Psalms 61:1 (id: 1819061001)

1For the Chief Musician. For a stringed instrument. By David. Hear my cry, God. Listen to my prayer.


## Psalms 61:2 (id: 1819061002)

2From the end of the earth, I will call to you when my heart is overwhelmed. Lead me to the rock that is higher than I.


## Psalms 61:3 (id: 1819061003)

3For you have been a refuge for me, a strong tower from the enemy.


## Psalms 61:4 (id: 1819061004)

4I will dwell in your tent forever. I will take refuge in the shelter of your wings. Selah.


## Psalms 61:5 (id: 1819061005)

5For you, God, have heard my vows. You have given me the heritage of those who fear your name.


## Psalms 61:6 (id: 1819061006)

6You will prolong the king’s life. His years will be for generations.


## Psalms 61:7 (id: 1819061007)

7He shall be enthroned in God’s presence forever. Appoint your loving kindness and truth, that they may preserve him.


## Psalms 61:8 (id: 1819061008)

8So I will sing praise to your name forever, that I may fulfill my vows daily.


## Psalms 62:1 (id: 1819062001)

1For the Chief Musician. To Jeduthun. A Psalm by David. My soul rests in God alone. My salvation is from him.


## Psalms 62:2 (id: 1819062002)

2He alone is my rock, my salvation, and my fortress. I will never be greatly shaken.


## Psalms 62:3 (id: 1819062003)

3How long will you assault a man? Would all of you throw him down, like a leaning wall, like a tottering fence?


## Psalms 62:4 (id: 1819062004)

4They fully intend to throw him down from his lofty place. They delight in lies. They bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly. Selah.


## Psalms 62:5 (id: 1819062005)

5My soul, wait in silence for God alone, for my expectation is from him.


## Psalms 62:6 (id: 1819062006)

6He alone is my rock and my salvation, my fortress. I will not be shaken.


## Psalms 62:7 (id: 1819062007)

7My salvation and my honor is with God. The rock of my strength, and my refuge, is in God.


## Psalms 62:8 (id: 1819062008)

8Trust in him at all times, you people. Pour out your heart before him. God is a refuge for us. Selah.


## Psalms 62:9 (id: 1819062009)

9Surely men of low degree are just a breath, and men of high degree are a lie. In the balances they will go up. They are together lighter than a breath.


## Psalms 62:10 (id: 1819062010)

10Don’t trust in oppression. Don’t become vain in robbery. If riches increase, don’t set your heart on them.


## Psalms 62:11 (id: 1819062011)

11God has spoken once; twice I have heard this, that power belongs to God.


## Psalms 62:12 (id: 1819062012)

12Also to you, Lord, belongs loving kindness, for you reward every man according to his work.


## Psalms 63:1 (id: 1819063001)

1A Psalm by David, when he was in the desert of Judah. God, you are my God. I will earnestly seek you. My soul thirsts for you. My flesh longs for you, in a dry and weary land, where there is no water.


## Psalms 63:2 (id: 1819063002)

2So I have seen you in the sanctuary, watching your power and your glory.


## Psalms 63:3 (id: 1819063003)

3Because your loving kindness is better than life, my lips shall praise you.


## Psalms 63:4 (id: 1819063004)

4So I will bless you while I live. I will lift up my hands in your name.


## Psalms 63:5 (id: 1819063005)

5My soul shall be satisfied as with the richest food. My mouth shall praise you with joyful lips,


## Psalms 63:6 (id: 1819063006)

6when I remember you on my bed, and think about you in the night watches.


## Psalms 63:7 (id: 1819063007)

7For you have been my help. I will rejoice in the shadow of your wings.


## Psalms 63:8 (id: 1819063008)

8My soul stays close to you. Your right hand holds me up.


## Psalms 63:9 (id: 1819063009)

9But those who seek my soul to destroy it shall go into the lower parts of the earth.


## Psalms 63:10 (id: 1819063010)

10They shall be given over to the power of the sword. They shall be jackal food.


## Psalms 63:11 (id: 1819063011)

11But the king shall rejoice in God. Everyone who swears by him will praise him, for the mouth of those who speak lies shall be silenced.


## Psalms 64:1 (id: 1819064001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. Hear my voice, God, in my complaint. Preserve my life from fear of the enemy.


## Psalms 64:2 (id: 1819064002)

2Hide me from the conspiracy of the wicked, from the noisy crowd of the ones doing evil;


## Psalms 64:3 (id: 1819064003)

3who sharpen their tongue like a sword, and aim their arrows, deadly words,


## Psalms 64:4 (id: 1819064004)

4to shoot innocent men from ambushes. They shoot at him suddenly and fearlessly.


## Psalms 64:5 (id: 1819064005)

5They encourage themselves in evil plans. They talk about laying snares secretly. They say, “Who will see them?”


## Psalms 64:6 (id: 1819064006)

6They plot injustice, saying, “We have made a perfect plan!” Surely man’s mind and heart are cunning.


## Psalms 64:7 (id: 1819064007)

7But God will shoot at them. They will be suddenly struck down with an arrow.


## Psalms 64:8 (id: 1819064008)

8Their own tongues shall ruin them. All who see them will shake their heads.


## Psalms 64:9 (id: 1819064009)

9All mankind shall be afraid. They shall declare the work of God, and shall wisely ponder what he has done.


## Psalms 64:10 (id: 1819064010)

10The righteous shall be glad in the LORD, and shall take refuge in him. All the upright in heart shall praise him!


## Psalms 65:1 (id: 1819065001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. A song. Praise waits for you, God, in Zion. Vows shall be performed to you.


## Psalms 65:2 (id: 1819065002)

2You who hear prayer, all men will come to you.


## Psalms 65:3 (id: 1819065003)

3Sins overwhelmed me, but you atoned for our transgressions.


## Psalms 65:4 (id: 1819065004)

4Blessed is the one whom you choose and cause to come near, that he may live in your courts. We will be filled with the goodness of your house, your holy temple.


## Psalms 65:5 (id: 1819065005)

5By awesome deeds of righteousness, you answer us, God of our salvation. You who are the hope of all the ends of the earth, of those who are far away on the sea.


## Psalms 65:6 (id: 1819065006)

6By your power, you form the mountains, having armed yourself with strength.


## Psalms 65:7 (id: 1819065007)

7You still the roaring of the seas, the roaring of their waves, and the turmoil of the nations.


## Psalms 65:8 (id: 1819065008)

8They also who dwell in faraway places are afraid at your wonders. You call the morning’s dawn and the evening with songs of joy.


## Psalms 65:9 (id: 1819065009)

9You visit the earth, and water it. You greatly enrich it. The river of God is full of water. You provide them grain, for so you have ordained it.


## Psalms 65:10 (id: 1819065010)

10You drench its furrows. You level its ridges. You soften it with showers. You bless it with a crop.


## Psalms 65:11 (id: 1819065011)

11You crown the year with your bounty. Your carts overflow with abundance.


## Psalms 65:12 (id: 1819065012)

12The wilderness grasslands overflow. The hills are clothed with gladness.


## Psalms 65:13 (id: 1819065013)

13The pastures are covered with flocks. The valleys also are clothed with grain. They shout for joy! They also sing.


## Psalms 66:1 (id: 1819066001)

1For the Chief Musician. A song. A Psalm. Make a joyful shout to God, all the earth!


## Psalms 66:2 (id: 1819066002)

2Sing to the glory of his name! Offer glory and praise!


## Psalms 66:3 (id: 1819066003)

3Tell God, “How awesome are your deeds! Through the greatness of your power, your enemies submit themselves to you.


## Psalms 66:4 (id: 1819066004)

4All the earth will worship you, and will sing to you; they will sing to your name.” Selah.


## Psalms 66:5 (id: 1819066005)

5Come, and see God’s deeds— awesome work on behalf of the children of men.


## Psalms 66:6 (id: 1819066006)

6He turned the sea into dry land. They went through the river on foot. There, we rejoiced in him.


## Psalms 66:7 (id: 1819066007)

7He rules by his might forever. His eyes watch the nations. Don’t let the rebellious rise up against him. Selah.


## Psalms 66:8 (id: 1819066008)

8Praise our God, you peoples! Make the sound of his praise heard,


## Psalms 66:9 (id: 1819066009)

9who preserves our life among the living, and doesn’t allow our feet to be moved.


## Psalms 66:10 (id: 1819066010)

10For you, God, have tested us. You have refined us, as silver is refined.


## Psalms 66:11 (id: 1819066011)

11You brought us into prison. You laid a burden on our backs.


## Psalms 66:12 (id: 1819066012)

12You allowed men to ride over our heads. We went through fire and through water, but you brought us to the place of abundance.


## Psalms 66:13 (id: 1819066013)

13I will come into your temple with burnt offerings. I will pay my vows to you,


## Psalms 66:14 (id: 1819066014)

14which my lips promised, and my mouth spoke, when I was in distress.


## Psalms 66:15 (id: 1819066015)

15I will offer to you burnt offerings of fat animals, with the offering of rams, I will offer bulls with goats. Selah.


## Psalms 66:16 (id: 1819066016)

16Come and hear, all you who fear God. I will declare what he has done for my soul.


## Psalms 66:17 (id: 1819066017)

17I cried to him with my mouth. He was extolled with my tongue.


## Psalms 66:18 (id: 1819066018)

18If I cherished sin in my heart, the Lord wouldn’t have listened.


## Psalms 66:19 (id: 1819066019)

19But most certainly, God has listened. He has heard the voice of my prayer.


## Psalms 66:20 (id: 1819066020)

20Blessed be God, who has not turned away my prayer, nor his loving kindness from me.


## Psalms 67:1 (id: 1819067001)

1For the Chief Musician. With stringed instruments. A Psalm. A song. May God be merciful to us, bless us, and cause his face to shine on us. Selah.


## Psalms 67:2 (id: 1819067002)

2That your way may be known on earth, and your salvation among all nations,


## Psalms 67:3 (id: 1819067003)

3let the peoples praise you, God. Let all the peoples praise you.


## Psalms 67:4 (id: 1819067004)

4Oh let the nations be glad and sing for joy, for you will judge the peoples with equity, and govern the nations on earth. Selah.


## Psalms 67:5 (id: 1819067005)

5Let the peoples praise you, God. Let all the peoples praise you.


## Psalms 67:6 (id: 1819067006)

6The earth has yielded its increase. God, even our own God, will bless us.


## Psalms 67:7 (id: 1819067007)

7God will bless us. All the ends of the earth shall fear him.


## Psalms 68:1 (id: 1819068001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. A song. Let God arise! Let his enemies be scattered! Let them who hate him also flee before him.


## Psalms 68:2 (id: 1819068002)

2As smoke is driven away, so drive them away. As wax melts before the fire, so let the wicked perish at the presence of God.


## Psalms 68:3 (id: 1819068003)

3But let the righteous be glad. Let them rejoice before God. Yes, let them rejoice with gladness.


## Psalms 68:4 (id: 1819068004)

4Sing to God! Sing praises to his name! Extol him who rides on the clouds: to the LORD, his name! Rejoice before him!


## Psalms 68:5 (id: 1819068005)

5A father of the fatherless, and a defender of the widows, is God in his holy habitation.


## Psalms 68:6 (id: 1819068006)

6God sets the lonely in families. He brings out the prisoners with singing, but the rebellious dwell in a sun\-scorched land.


## Psalms 68:7 (id: 1819068007)

7God, when you went out before your people, when you marched through the wilderness... Selah.


## Psalms 68:8 (id: 1819068008)

8The earth trembled. The sky also poured down rain at the presence of the God of Sinai— at the presence of God, the God of Israel.


## Psalms 68:9 (id: 1819068009)

9You, God, sent a plentiful rain. You confirmed your inheritance when it was weary.


## Psalms 68:10 (id: 1819068010)

10Your congregation lived therein. You, God, prepared your goodness for the poor.


## Psalms 68:11 (id: 1819068011)

11The Lord announced the word. The ones who proclaim it are a great company.


## Psalms 68:12 (id: 1819068012)

12“Kings of armies flee! They flee!” She who waits at home divides the plunder,


## Psalms 68:13 (id: 1819068013)

13while you sleep among the camp fires, the wings of a dove sheathed with silver, her feathers with shining gold.


## Psalms 68:14 (id: 1819068014)

14When the Almighty scattered kings in her, it snowed on Zalmon.


## Psalms 68:15 (id: 1819068015)

15The mountains of Bashan are majestic mountains. The mountains of Bashan are rugged.


## Psalms 68:16 (id: 1819068016)

16Why do you look in envy, you rugged mountains, at the mountain where God chooses to reign? Yes, the LORD will dwell there forever.


## Psalms 68:17 (id: 1819068017)

17The chariots of God are tens of thousands and thousands of thousands. The Lord is among them, from Sinai, into the sanctuary.


## Psalms 68:18 (id: 1819068018)

18You have ascended on high. You have led away captives. You have received gifts among people, yes, among the rebellious also, that the LORD God might dwell there.


## Psalms 68:19 (id: 1819068019)

19Blessed be the Lord, who daily bears our burdens, even the God who is our salvation. Selah.


## Psalms 68:20 (id: 1819068020)

20God is to us a God of deliverance. To GOD, the Lord, belongs escape from death.


## Psalms 68:21 (id: 1819068021)

21But God will strike through the head of his enemies, the hairy scalp of such a one as still continues in his guiltiness.


## Psalms 68:22 (id: 1819068022)

22The Lord said, “I will bring you again from Bashan, I will bring you again from the depths of the sea,


## Psalms 68:23 (id: 1819068023)

23that you may crush them, dipping your foot in blood, that the tongues of your dogs may have their portion from your enemies.”


## Psalms 68:24 (id: 1819068024)

24They have seen your processions, God, even the processions of my God, my King, into the sanctuary.


## Psalms 68:25 (id: 1819068025)

25The singers went before, the minstrels followed after, among the ladies playing with tambourines,


## Psalms 68:26 (id: 1819068026)

26“Bless God in the congregations, even the Lord in the assembly of Israel!”


## Psalms 68:27 (id: 1819068027)

27There is little Benjamin, their ruler, the princes of Judah, their council, the princes of Zebulun, and the princes of Naphtali.


## Psalms 68:28 (id: 1819068028)

28Your God has commanded your strength. Strengthen, God, that which you have done for us.


## Psalms 68:29 (id: 1819068029)

29Because of your temple at Jerusalem, kings shall bring presents to you.


## Psalms 68:30 (id: 1819068030)

30Rebuke the wild animal of the reeds, the multitude of the bulls with the calves of the peoples. Trample under foot the bars of silver. Scatter the nations who delight in war.


## Psalms 68:31 (id: 1819068031)

31Princes shall come out of Egypt. Ethiopia shall hurry to stretch out her hands to God.


## Psalms 68:32 (id: 1819068032)

32Sing to God, you kingdoms of the earth! Sing praises to the Lord—Selah—


## Psalms 68:33 (id: 1819068033)

33to him who rides on the heaven of heavens, which are of old; behold, he utters his voice, a mighty voice.


## Psalms 68:34 (id: 1819068034)

34Ascribe strength to God! His excellency is over Israel, his strength is in the skies.


## Psalms 68:35 (id: 1819068035)

35You are awesome, God, in your sanctuaries. The God of Israel gives strength and power to his people. Praise be to God!


## Psalms 69:1 (id: 1819069001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Lilies.” By David. Save me, God, for the waters have come up to my neck!


## Psalms 69:2 (id: 1819069002)

2I sink in deep mire, where there is no foothold. I have come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me.


## Psalms 69:3 (id: 1819069003)

3I am weary with my crying. My throat is dry. My eyes fail looking for my God.


## Psalms 69:4 (id: 1819069004)

4Those who hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of my head. Those who want to cut me off, being my enemies wrongfully, are mighty. I have to restore what I didn’t take away.


## Psalms 69:5 (id: 1819069005)

5God, you know my foolishness. My sins aren’t hidden from you.


## Psalms 69:6 (id: 1819069006)

6Don’t let those who wait for you be shamed through me, Lord GOD of Armies. Don’t let those who seek you be brought to dishonor through me, God of Israel.


## Psalms 69:7 (id: 1819069007)

7Because for your sake, I have borne reproach. Shame has covered my face.


## Psalms 69:8 (id: 1819069008)

8I have become a stranger to my brothers, an alien to my mother’s children.


## Psalms 69:9 (id: 1819069009)

9For the zeal of your house consumes me. The reproaches of those who reproach you have fallen on me.


## Psalms 69:10 (id: 1819069010)

10When I wept and I fasted, that was to my reproach.


## Psalms 69:11 (id: 1819069011)

11When I made sackcloth my clothing, I became a byword to them.


## Psalms 69:12 (id: 1819069012)

12Those who sit in the gate talk about me. I am the song of the drunkards.


## Psalms 69:13 (id: 1819069013)

13But as for me, my prayer is to you, LORD, in an acceptable time. God, in the abundance of your loving kindness, answer me in the truth of your salvation.


## Psalms 69:14 (id: 1819069014)

14Deliver me out of the mire, and don’t let me sink. Let me be delivered from those who hate me, and out of the deep waters.


## Psalms 69:15 (id: 1819069015)

15Don’t let the flood waters overwhelm me, neither let the deep swallow me up. Don’t let the pit shut its mouth on me.


## Psalms 69:16 (id: 1819069016)

16Answer me, LORD, for your loving kindness is good. According to the multitude of your tender mercies, turn to me.


## Psalms 69:17 (id: 1819069017)

17Don’t hide your face from your servant, for I am in distress. Answer me speedily!


## Psalms 69:18 (id: 1819069018)

18Draw near to my soul and redeem it. Ransom me because of my enemies.


## Psalms 69:19 (id: 1819069019)

19You know my reproach, my shame, and my dishonor. My adversaries are all before you.


## Psalms 69:20 (id: 1819069020)

20Reproach has broken my heart, and I am full of heaviness. I looked for some to take pity, but there was none; for comforters, but I found none.


## Psalms 69:21 (id: 1819069021)

21They also gave me poison for my food. In my thirst, they gave me vinegar to drink.


## Psalms 69:22 (id: 1819069022)

22Let their table before them become a snare. May it become a retribution and a trap.


## Psalms 69:23 (id: 1819069023)

23Let their eyes be darkened, so that they can’t see. Let their backs be continually bent.


## Psalms 69:24 (id: 1819069024)

24Pour out your indignation on them. Let the fierceness of your anger overtake them.


## Psalms 69:25 (id: 1819069025)

25Let their habitation be desolate. Let no one dwell in their tents.


## Psalms 69:26 (id: 1819069026)

26For they persecute him whom you have wounded. They tell of the sorrow of those whom you have hurt.


## Psalms 69:27 (id: 1819069027)

27Charge them with crime upon crime. Don’t let them come into your righteousness.


## Psalms 69:28 (id: 1819069028)

28Let them be blotted out of the book of life, and not be written with the righteous.


## Psalms 69:29 (id: 1819069029)

29But I am in pain and distress. Let your salvation, God, protect me.


## Psalms 69:30 (id: 1819069030)

30I will praise the name of God with a song, and will magnify him with thanksgiving.


## Psalms 69:31 (id: 1819069031)

31It will please the LORD better than an ox, or a bull that has horns and hoofs.


## Psalms 69:32 (id: 1819069032)

32The humble have seen it, and are glad. You who seek after God, let your heart live.


## Psalms 69:33 (id: 1819069033)

33For the LORD hears the needy, and doesn’t despise his captive people.


## Psalms 69:34 (id: 1819069034)

34Let heaven and earth praise him; the seas, and everything that moves therein!


## Psalms 69:35 (id: 1819069035)

35For God will save Zion, and build the cities of Judah. They shall settle there, and own it.


## Psalms 69:36 (id: 1819069036)

36The children also of his servants shall inherit it. Those who love his name shall dwell therein.


## Psalms 70:1 (id: 1819070001)

1For the Chief Musician. By David. A reminder. Hurry, God, to deliver me. Come quickly to help me, LORD.


## Psalms 70:2 (id: 1819070002)

2Let them be disappointed and confounded who seek my soul. Let those who desire my ruin be turned back in disgrace.


## Psalms 70:3 (id: 1819070003)

3Let them be turned because of their shame who say, “Aha! Aha!”


## Psalms 70:4 (id: 1819070004)

4Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you. Let those who love your salvation continually say, “Let God be exalted!”


## Psalms 70:5 (id: 1819070005)

5But I am poor and needy. Come to me quickly, God. You are my help and my deliverer. LORD, don’t delay.


## Psalms 71:1 (id: 1819071001)

1In you, LORD, I take refuge. Never let me be disappointed.


## Psalms 71:2 (id: 1819071002)

2Deliver me in your righteousness, and rescue me. Turn your ear to me, and save me.


## Psalms 71:3 (id: 1819071003)

3Be to me a rock of refuge to which I may always go. Give the command to save me, for you are my rock and my fortress.


## Psalms 71:4 (id: 1819071004)

4Rescue me, my God, from the hand of the wicked, from the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.


## Psalms 71:5 (id: 1819071005)

5For you are my hope, Lord GOD, my confidence from my youth.


## Psalms 71:6 (id: 1819071006)

6I have relied on you from the womb. You are he who took me out of my mother’s womb. I will always praise you.


## Psalms 71:7 (id: 1819071007)

7I am a marvel to many, but you are my strong refuge.


## Psalms 71:8 (id: 1819071008)

8My mouth shall be filled with your praise, with your honor all day long.


## Psalms 71:9 (id: 1819071009)

9Don’t reject me in my old age. Don’t forsake me when my strength fails.


## Psalms 71:10 (id: 1819071010)

10For my enemies talk about me. Those who watch for my soul conspire together,


## Psalms 71:11 (id: 1819071011)

11saying, “God has forsaken him. Pursue and take him, for no one will rescue him.”


## Psalms 71:12 (id: 1819071012)

12God, don’t be far from me. My God, hurry to help me.


## Psalms 71:13 (id: 1819071013)

13Let my accusers be disappointed and consumed. Let them be covered with disgrace and scorn who want to harm me.


## Psalms 71:14 (id: 1819071014)

14But I will always hope, and will add to all of your praise.


## Psalms 71:15 (id: 1819071015)

15My mouth will tell about your righteousness, and of your salvation all day, though I don’t know its full measure.


## Psalms 71:16 (id: 1819071016)

16I will come with the mighty acts of the Lord GOD. I will make mention of your righteousness, even of yours alone.


## Psalms 71:17 (id: 1819071017)

17God, you have taught me from my youth. Until now, I have declared your wondrous works.


## Psalms 71:18 (id: 1819071018)

18Yes, even when I am old and gray\-haired, God, don’t forsake me, until I have declared your strength to the next generation, your might to everyone who is to come.


## Psalms 71:19 (id: 1819071019)

19God, your righteousness also reaches to the heavens. You have done great things. God, who is like you?


## Psalms 71:20 (id: 1819071020)

20You, who have shown us many and bitter troubles, you will let me live. You will bring us up again from the depths of the earth.


## Psalms 71:21 (id: 1819071021)

21Increase my honor and comfort me again.


## Psalms 71:22 (id: 1819071022)

22I will also praise you with the harp for your faithfulness, my God. I sing praises to you with the lyre, Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 71:23 (id: 1819071023)

23My lips shall shout for joy! My soul, which you have redeemed, sings praises to you!


## Psalms 71:24 (id: 1819071024)

24My tongue will also talk about your righteousness all day long, for they are disappointed, and they are confounded, who want to harm me.


## Psalms 72:1 (id: 1819072001)

1By Solomon. God, give the king your justice; your righteousness to the royal son.


## Psalms 72:2 (id: 1819072002)

2He will judge your people with righteousness, and your poor with justice.


## Psalms 72:3 (id: 1819072003)

3The mountains shall bring prosperity to the people. The hills bring the fruit of righteousness.


## Psalms 72:4 (id: 1819072004)

4He will judge the poor of the people. He will save the children of the needy, and will break the oppressor in pieces.


## Psalms 72:5 (id: 1819072005)

5They shall fear you while the sun endures; and as long as the moon, throughout all generations.


## Psalms 72:6 (id: 1819072006)

6He will come down like rain on the mown grass, as showers that water the earth.


## Psalms 72:7 (id: 1819072007)

7In his days, the righteous shall flourish, and abundance of peace, until the moon is no more.


## Psalms 72:8 (id: 1819072008)

8He shall have dominion also from sea to sea, from the River to the ends of the earth.


## Psalms 72:9 (id: 1819072009)

9Those who dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him. His enemies shall lick the dust.


## Psalms 72:10 (id: 1819072010)

10The kings of Tarshish and of the islands will bring tribute. The kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.


## Psalms 72:11 (id: 1819072011)

11Yes, all kings shall fall down before him. All nations shall serve him.


## Psalms 72:12 (id: 1819072012)

12For he will deliver the needy when he cries; the poor, who has no helper.


## Psalms 72:13 (id: 1819072013)

13He will have pity on the poor and needy. He will save the souls of the needy.


## Psalms 72:14 (id: 1819072014)

14He will redeem their soul from oppression and violence. Their blood will be precious in his sight.


## Psalms 72:15 (id: 1819072015)

15He will live; and Sheba’s gold will be given to him. Men will pray for him continually. They will bless him all day long.


## Psalms 72:16 (id: 1819072016)

16Abundance of grain shall be throughout the land. Its fruit sways like Lebanon. Let it flourish, thriving like the grass of the field.


## Psalms 72:17 (id: 1819072017)

17His name endures forever. His name continues as long as the sun. Men shall be blessed by him. All nations will call him blessed.


## Psalms 72:18 (id: 1819072018)

18Praise be to the LORD God, the God of Israel, who alone does marvelous deeds.


## Psalms 72:19 (id: 1819072019)

19Blessed be his glorious name forever! Let the whole earth be filled with his glory! Amen and amen.


## Psalms 72:20 (id: 1819072020)

20This ends the prayers by David, the son of Jesse.


## Psalms 73:1 (id: 1819073001)

1A Psalm by Asaph. Surely God is good to Israel, to those who are pure in heart.


## Psalms 73:2 (id: 1819073002)

2But as for me, my feet were almost gone. My steps had nearly slipped.


## Psalms 73:3 (id: 1819073003)

3For I was envious of the arrogant, when I saw the prosperity of the wicked.


## Psalms 73:4 (id: 1819073004)

4For there are no struggles in their death, but their strength is firm.


## Psalms 73:5 (id: 1819073005)

5They are free from burdens of men, neither are they plagued like other men.


## Psalms 73:6 (id: 1819073006)

6Therefore pride is like a chain around their neck. Violence covers them like a garment.


## Psalms 73:7 (id: 1819073007)

7Their eyes bulge with fat. Their minds pass the limits of conceit.


## Psalms 73:8 (id: 1819073008)

8They scoff and speak with malice. In arrogance, they threaten oppression.


## Psalms 73:9 (id: 1819073009)

9They have set their mouth in the heavens. Their tongue walks through the earth.


## Psalms 73:10 (id: 1819073010)

10Therefore their people return to them, and they drink up waters of abundance.


## Psalms 73:11 (id: 1819073011)

11They say, “How does God know? Is there knowledge in the Most High?”


## Psalms 73:12 (id: 1819073012)

12Behold, these are the wicked. Being always at ease, they increase in riches.


## Psalms 73:13 (id: 1819073013)

13Surely I have cleansed my heart in vain, and washed my hands in innocence,


## Psalms 73:14 (id: 1819073014)

14For all day long I have been plagued, and punished every morning.


## Psalms 73:15 (id: 1819073015)

15If I had said, “I will speak thus”, behold, I would have betrayed the generation of your children.


## Psalms 73:16 (id: 1819073016)

16When I tried to understand this, it was too painful for me—


## Psalms 73:17 (id: 1819073017)

17until I entered God’s sanctuary, and considered their latter end.


## Psalms 73:18 (id: 1819073018)

18Surely you set them in slippery places. You throw them down to destruction.


## Psalms 73:19 (id: 1819073019)

19How they are suddenly destroyed! They are completely swept away with terrors.


## Psalms 73:20 (id: 1819073020)

20As a dream when one wakes up, so, Lord, when you awake, you will despise their fantasies.


## Psalms 73:21 (id: 1819073021)

21For my soul was grieved. I was embittered in my heart.


## Psalms 73:22 (id: 1819073022)

22I was so senseless and ignorant. I was a brute beast before you.


## Psalms 73:23 (id: 1819073023)

23Nevertheless, I am continually with you. You have held my right hand.


## Psalms 73:24 (id: 1819073024)

24You will guide me with your counsel, and afterward receive me to glory.


## Psalms 73:25 (id: 1819073025)

25Whom do I have in heaven? There is no one on earth whom I desire besides you.


## Psalms 73:26 (id: 1819073026)

26My flesh and my heart fails, but God is the strength of my heart and my portion forever.


## Psalms 73:27 (id: 1819073027)

27For, behold, those who are far from you shall perish. You have destroyed all those who are unfaithful to you.


## Psalms 73:28 (id: 1819073028)

28But it is good for me to come close to God. I have made the Lord GOD my refuge, that I may tell of all your works.


## Psalms 74:1 (id: 1819074001)

1A contemplation by Asaph. God, why have you rejected us forever? Why does your anger smolder against the sheep of your pasture?


## Psalms 74:2 (id: 1819074002)

2Remember your congregation, which you purchased of old, which you have redeemed to be the tribe of your inheritance: Mount Zion, in which you have lived.


## Psalms 74:3 (id: 1819074003)

3Lift up your feet to the perpetual ruins, all the evil that the enemy has done in the sanctuary.


## Psalms 74:4 (id: 1819074004)

4Your adversaries have roared in the middle of your assembly. They have set up their standards as signs.


## Psalms 74:5 (id: 1819074005)

5They behaved like men wielding axes, cutting through a thicket of trees.


## Psalms 74:6 (id: 1819074006)

6Now they break all its carved work down with hatchet and hammers.


## Psalms 74:7 (id: 1819074007)

7They have burned your sanctuary to the ground. They have profaned the dwelling place of your Name.


## Psalms 74:8 (id: 1819074008)

8They said in their heart, “We will crush them completely.” They have burned up all the places in the land where God was worshiped.


## Psalms 74:9 (id: 1819074009)

9We see no miraculous signs. There is no longer any prophet, neither is there among us anyone who knows how long.


## Psalms 74:10 (id: 1819074010)

10How long, God, shall the adversary reproach? Shall the enemy blaspheme your name forever?


## Psalms 74:11 (id: 1819074011)

11Why do you draw back your hand, even your right hand? Take it from your chest and consume them!


## Psalms 74:12 (id: 1819074012)

12Yet God is my King of old, working salvation throughout the earth.


## Psalms 74:13 (id: 1819074013)

13You divided the sea by your strength. You broke the heads of the sea monsters in the waters.


## Psalms 74:14 (id: 1819074014)

14You broke the heads of Leviathan in pieces. You gave him as food to people and desert creatures.


## Psalms 74:15 (id: 1819074015)

15You opened up spring and stream. You dried up mighty rivers.


## Psalms 74:16 (id: 1819074016)

16The day is yours, the night is also yours. You have prepared the light and the sun.


## Psalms 74:17 (id: 1819074017)

17You have set all the boundaries of the earth. You have made summer and winter.


## Psalms 74:18 (id: 1819074018)

18Remember this, that the enemy has mocked you, LORD. Foolish people have blasphemed your name.


## Psalms 74:19 (id: 1819074019)

19Don’t deliver the soul of your dove to wild beasts. Don’t forget the life of your poor forever.


## Psalms 74:20 (id: 1819074020)

20Honor your covenant, for haunts of violence fill the dark places of the earth.


## Psalms 74:21 (id: 1819074021)

21Don’t let the oppressed return ashamed. Let the poor and needy praise your name.


## Psalms 74:22 (id: 1819074022)

22Arise, God! Plead your own cause. Remember how the foolish man mocks you all day.


## Psalms 74:23 (id: 1819074023)

23Don’t forget the voice of your adversaries. The tumult of those who rise up against you ascends continually.


## Psalms 75:1 (id: 1819075001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Psalm by Asaph. A song. We give thanks to you, God. We give thanks, for your Name is near. Men tell about your wondrous works.


## Psalms 75:2 (id: 1819075002)

2When I choose the appointed time, I will judge blamelessly.


## Psalms 75:3 (id: 1819075003)

3The earth and all its inhabitants quake. I firmly hold its pillars. Selah.


## Psalms 75:4 (id: 1819075004)

4I said to the arrogant, “Don’t boast!” I said to the wicked, “Don’t lift up the horn.


## Psalms 75:5 (id: 1819075005)

5Don’t lift up your horn on high. Don’t speak with a stiff neck.”


## Psalms 75:6 (id: 1819075006)

6For neither from the east, nor from the west, nor yet from the south, comes exaltation.


## Psalms 75:7 (id: 1819075007)

7But God is the judge. He puts down one, and lifts up another.


## Psalms 75:8 (id: 1819075008)

8For in the LORD’s hand there is a cup, full of foaming wine mixed with spices. He pours it out. Indeed the wicked of the earth drink and drink it to its very dregs.


## Psalms 75:9 (id: 1819075009)

9But I will declare this forever: I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 75:10 (id: 1819075010)

10I will cut off all the horns of the wicked, but the horns of the righteous shall be lifted up.


## Psalms 76:1 (id: 1819076001)

1For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A Psalm by Asaph. A song. In Judah, God is known. His name is great in Israel.


## Psalms 76:2 (id: 1819076002)

2His tabernacle is also in Salem. His dwelling place in Zion.


## Psalms 76:3 (id: 1819076003)

3There he broke the flaming arrows of the bow, the shield, and the sword, and the weapons of war. Selah.


## Psalms 76:4 (id: 1819076004)

4Glorious are you, and excellent, more than mountains of game.


## Psalms 76:5 (id: 1819076005)

5Valiant men lie plundered, they have slept their last sleep. None of the men of war can lift their hands.


## Psalms 76:6 (id: 1819076006)

6At your rebuke, God of Jacob, both chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.


## Psalms 76:7 (id: 1819076007)

7You, even you, are to be feared. Who can stand in your sight when you are angry?


## Psalms 76:8 (id: 1819076008)

8You pronounced judgment from heaven. The earth feared, and was silent,


## Psalms 76:9 (id: 1819076009)

9when God arose to judgment, to save all the afflicted ones of the earth. Selah.


## Psalms 76:10 (id: 1819076010)

10Surely the wrath of man praises you. The survivors of your wrath are restrained.


## Psalms 76:11 (id: 1819076011)

11Make vows to the LORD your God, and fulfill them! Let all of his neighbors bring presents to him who is to be feared.


## Psalms 76:12 (id: 1819076012)

12He will cut off the spirit of princes. He is feared by the kings of the earth.


## Psalms 77:1 (id: 1819077001)

1For the Chief Musician. To Jeduthun. A Psalm by Asaph. My cry goes to God! Indeed, I cry to God for help, and for him to listen to me.


## Psalms 77:2 (id: 1819077002)

2In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord. My hand was stretched out in the night, and didn’t get tired. My soul refused to be comforted.


## Psalms 77:3 (id: 1819077003)

3I remember God, and I groan. I complain, and my spirit is overwhelmed. Selah.


## Psalms 77:4 (id: 1819077004)

4You hold my eyelids open. I am so troubled that I can’t speak.


## Psalms 77:5 (id: 1819077005)

5I have considered the days of old, the years of ancient times.


## Psalms 77:6 (id: 1819077006)

6I remember my song in the night. I consider in my own heart; my spirit diligently inquires:


## Psalms 77:7 (id: 1819077007)

7“Will the Lord reject us forever? Will he be favorable no more?


## Psalms 77:8 (id: 1819077008)

8Has his loving kindness vanished forever? Does his promise fail for generations?


## Psalms 77:9 (id: 1819077009)

9Has God forgotten to be gracious? Has he, in anger, withheld his compassion?” Selah.


## Psalms 77:10 (id: 1819077010)

10Then I thought, “I will appeal to this: the years of the right hand of the Most High.”


## Psalms 77:11 (id: 1819077011)

11I will remember the LORD’s deeds; for I will remember your wonders of old.


## Psalms 77:12 (id: 1819077012)

12I will also meditate on all your work, and consider your doings.


## Psalms 77:13 (id: 1819077013)

13Your way, God, is in the sanctuary. What god is great like God?


## Psalms 77:14 (id: 1819077014)

14You are the God who does wonders. You have made your strength known among the peoples.


## Psalms 77:15 (id: 1819077015)

15You have redeemed your people with your arm, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah.


## Psalms 77:16 (id: 1819077016)

16The waters saw you, God. The waters saw you, and they writhed. The depths also convulsed.


## Psalms 77:17 (id: 1819077017)

17The clouds poured out water. The skies resounded with thunder. Your arrows also flashed around.


## Psalms 77:18 (id: 1819077018)

18The voice of your thunder was in the whirlwind. The lightnings lit up the world. The earth trembled and shook.


## Psalms 77:19 (id: 1819077019)

19Your way was through the sea, your paths through the great waters. Your footsteps were not known.


## Psalms 77:20 (id: 1819077020)

20You led your people like a flock, by the hand of Moses and Aaron.


## Psalms 78:1 (id: 1819078001)

1A contemplation by Asaph. Hear my teaching, my people. Turn your ears to the words of my mouth.


## Psalms 78:2 (id: 1819078002)

2I will open my mouth in a parable. I will utter dark sayings of old,


## Psalms 78:3 (id: 1819078003)

3which we have heard and known, and our fathers have told us.


## Psalms 78:4 (id: 1819078004)

4We will not hide them from their children, telling to the generation to come the praises of the LORD, his strength, and his wondrous deeds that he has done.


## Psalms 78:5 (id: 1819078005)

5For he established a covenant in Jacob, and appointed a teaching in Israel, which he commanded our fathers, that they should make them known to their children;


## Psalms 78:6 (id: 1819078006)

6that the generation to come might know, even the children who should be born; who should arise and tell their children,


## Psalms 78:7 (id: 1819078007)

7that they might set their hope in God, and not forget God’s deeds, but keep his commandments,


## Psalms 78:8 (id: 1819078008)

8and might not be as their fathers— a stubborn and rebellious generation, a generation that didn’t make their hearts loyal, whose spirit was not steadfast with God.


## Psalms 78:9 (id: 1819078009)

9The children of Ephraim, being armed and carrying bows, turned back in the day of battle.


## Psalms 78:10 (id: 1819078010)

10They didn’t keep God’s covenant, and refused to walk in his law.


## Psalms 78:11 (id: 1819078011)

11They forgot his doings, his wondrous deeds that he had shown them.


## Psalms 78:12 (id: 1819078012)

12He did marvelous things in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan.


## Psalms 78:13 (id: 1819078013)

13He split the sea, and caused them to pass through. He made the waters stand as a heap.


## Psalms 78:14 (id: 1819078014)

14In the daytime he also led them with a cloud, and all night with a light of fire.


## Psalms 78:15 (id: 1819078015)

15He split rocks in the wilderness, and gave them drink abundantly as out of the depths.


## Psalms 78:16 (id: 1819078016)

16He brought streams also out of the rock, and caused waters to run down like rivers.


## Psalms 78:17 (id: 1819078017)

17Yet they still went on to sin against him, to rebel against the Most High in the desert.


## Psalms 78:18 (id: 1819078018)

18They tempted God in their heart by asking food according to their desire.


## Psalms 78:19 (id: 1819078019)

19Yes, they spoke against God. They said, “Can God prepare a table in the wilderness?


## Psalms 78:20 (id: 1819078020)

20Behold, he struck the rock, so that waters gushed out, and streams overflowed. Can he give bread also? Will he provide meat for his people?”


## Psalms 78:21 (id: 1819078021)

21Therefore the LORD heard, and was angry. A fire was kindled against Jacob, anger also went up against Israel,


## Psalms 78:22 (id: 1819078022)

22because they didn’t believe in God, and didn’t trust in his salvation.


## Psalms 78:23 (id: 1819078023)

23Yet he commanded the skies above, and opened the doors of heaven.


## Psalms 78:24 (id: 1819078024)

24He rained down manna on them to eat, and gave them food from the sky.


## Psalms 78:25 (id: 1819078025)

25Man ate the bread of angels. He sent them food to the full.


## Psalms 78:26 (id: 1819078026)

26He caused the east wind to blow in the sky. By his power he guided the south wind.


## Psalms 78:27 (id: 1819078027)

27He also rained meat on them as the dust, winged birds as the sand of the seas.


## Psalms 78:28 (id: 1819078028)

28He let them fall in the middle of their camp, around their habitations.


## Psalms 78:29 (id: 1819078029)
