29So they ate, and were well filled. He gave them their own desire.


## Psalms 78:30 (id: 1819078030)

30They didn’t turn from their cravings. Their food was yet in their mouths,


## Psalms 78:31 (id: 1819078031)

31when the anger of God went up against them, killed some of their strongest, and struck down the young men of Israel.


## Psalms 78:32 (id: 1819078032)

32For all this they still sinned, and didn’t believe in his wondrous works.


## Psalms 78:33 (id: 1819078033)

33Therefore he consumed their days in vanity, and their years in terror.


## Psalms 78:34 (id: 1819078034)

34When he killed them, then they inquired after him. They returned and sought God earnestly.


## Psalms 78:35 (id: 1819078035)

35They remembered that God was their rock, the Most High God, their redeemer.


## Psalms 78:36 (id: 1819078036)

36But they flattered him with their mouth, and lied to him with their tongue.


## Psalms 78:37 (id: 1819078037)

37For their heart was not right with him, neither were they faithful in his covenant.


## Psalms 78:38 (id: 1819078038)

38But he, being merciful, forgave iniquity, and didn’t destroy them. Yes, many times he turned his anger away, and didn’t stir up all his wrath.


## Psalms 78:39 (id: 1819078039)

39He remembered that they were but flesh, a wind that passes away, and doesn’t come again.


## Psalms 78:40 (id: 1819078040)

40How often they rebelled against him in the wilderness, and grieved him in the desert!


## Psalms 78:41 (id: 1819078041)

41They turned again and tempted God, and provoked the Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 78:42 (id: 1819078042)

42They didn’t remember his hand, nor the day when he redeemed them from the adversary;


## Psalms 78:43 (id: 1819078043)

43how he set his signs in Egypt, his wonders in the field of Zoan,


## Psalms 78:44 (id: 1819078044)

44he turned their rivers into blood, and their streams, so that they could not drink.


## Psalms 78:45 (id: 1819078045)

45He sent among them swarms of flies, which devoured them; and frogs, which destroyed them.


## Psalms 78:46 (id: 1819078046)

46He also gave their increase to the caterpillar, and their labor to the locust.


## Psalms 78:47 (id: 1819078047)

47He destroyed their vines with hail, their sycamore fig trees with frost.


## Psalms 78:48 (id: 1819078048)

48He also gave over their livestock to the hail, and their flocks to hot thunderbolts.


## Psalms 78:49 (id: 1819078049)

49He threw on them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, indignation, and trouble, and a band of angels of evil.


## Psalms 78:50 (id: 1819078050)

50He made a path for his anger. He didn’t spare their soul from death, but gave their life over to the pestilence,


## Psalms 78:51 (id: 1819078051)

51and struck all the firstborn in Egypt, the chief of their strength in the tents of Ham.


## Psalms 78:52 (id: 1819078052)

52But he led out his own people like sheep, and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.


## Psalms 78:53 (id: 1819078053)

53He led them safely, so that they weren’t afraid, but the sea overwhelmed their enemies.


## Psalms 78:54 (id: 1819078054)

54He brought them to the border of his sanctuary, to this mountain, which his right hand had taken.


## Psalms 78:55 (id: 1819078055)

55He also drove out the nations before them, allotted them for an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents.


## Psalms 78:56 (id: 1819078056)

56Yet they tempted and rebelled against the Most High God, and didn’t keep his testimonies,


## Psalms 78:57 (id: 1819078057)

57but turned back, and dealt treacherously like their fathers. They were twisted like a deceitful bow.


## Psalms 78:58 (id: 1819078058)

58For they provoked him to anger with their high places, and moved him to jealousy with their engraved images.


## Psalms 78:59 (id: 1819078059)

59When God heard this, he was angry, and greatly abhorred Israel,


## Psalms 78:60 (id: 1819078060)

60so that he abandoned the tent of Shiloh, the tent which he placed among men,


## Psalms 78:61 (id: 1819078061)

61and delivered his strength into captivity, his glory into the adversary’s hand.


## Psalms 78:62 (id: 1819078062)

62He also gave his people over to the sword, and was angry with his inheritance.


## Psalms 78:63 (id: 1819078063)

63Fire devoured their young men. Their virgins had no wedding song.


## Psalms 78:64 (id: 1819078064)

64Their priests fell by the sword, and their widows couldn’t weep.


## Psalms 78:65 (id: 1819078065)

65Then the Lord awakened as one out of sleep, like a mighty man who shouts by reason of wine.


## Psalms 78:66 (id: 1819078066)

66He struck his adversaries backward. He put them to a perpetual reproach.


## Psalms 78:67 (id: 1819078067)

67Moreover he rejected the tent of Joseph, and didn’t choose the tribe of Ephraim,


## Psalms 78:68 (id: 1819078068)

68But chose the tribe of Judah, Mount Zion which he loved.


## Psalms 78:69 (id: 1819078069)

69He built his sanctuary like the heights, like the earth which he has established forever.


## Psalms 78:70 (id: 1819078070)

70He also chose David his servant, and took him from the sheepfolds;


## Psalms 78:71 (id: 1819078071)

71from following the ewes that have their young, he brought him to be the shepherd of Jacob, his people, and Israel, his inheritance.


## Psalms 78:72 (id: 1819078072)

72So he was their shepherd according to the integrity of his heart, and guided them by the skillfulness of his hands.


## Psalms 79:1 (id: 1819079001)

1A Psalm by Asaph. God, the nations have come into your inheritance. They have defiled your holy temple. They have laid Jerusalem in heaps.


## Psalms 79:2 (id: 1819079002)

2They have given the dead bodies of your servants to be food for the birds of the sky, the flesh of your saints to the animals of the earth.


## Psalms 79:3 (id: 1819079003)

3They have shed their blood like water around Jerusalem. There was no one to bury them.


## Psalms 79:4 (id: 1819079004)

4We have become a reproach to our neighbors, a scoffing and derision to those who are around us.


## Psalms 79:5 (id: 1819079005)

5How long, LORD? Will you be angry forever? Will your jealousy burn like fire?


## Psalms 79:6 (id: 1819079006)

6Pour out your wrath on the nations that don’t know you, on the kingdoms that don’t call on your name,


## Psalms 79:7 (id: 1819079007)

7for they have devoured Jacob, and destroyed his homeland.


## Psalms 79:8 (id: 1819079008)

8Don’t hold the iniquities of our forefathers against us. Let your tender mercies speedily meet us, for we are in desperate need.


## Psalms 79:9 (id: 1819079009)

9Help us, God of our salvation, for the glory of your name. Deliver us, and forgive our sins, for your name’s sake.


## Psalms 79:10 (id: 1819079010)

10Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?” Let it be known among the nations, before our eyes, that vengeance for your servants’ blood is being poured out.


## Psalms 79:11 (id: 1819079011)

11Let the sighing of the prisoner come before you. According to the greatness of your power, preserve those who are sentenced to death.


## Psalms 79:12 (id: 1819079012)

12Pay back to our neighbors seven times into their bosom their reproach with which they have reproached you, Lord.


## Psalms 79:13 (id: 1819079013)

13So we, your people and sheep of your pasture, will give you thanks forever. We will praise you forever, to all generations.


## Psalms 80:1 (id: 1819080001)

1For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Lilies of the Covenant.” A Psalm by Asaph. Hear us, Shepherd of Israel, you who lead Joseph like a flock, you who sit above the cherubim, shine out.


## Psalms 80:2 (id: 1819080002)

2Before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasseh, stir up your might! Come to save us!


## Psalms 80:3 (id: 1819080003)

3Turn us again, God. Cause your face to shine, and we will be saved.


## Psalms 80:4 (id: 1819080004)

4LORD God of Armies, how long will you be angry against the prayer of your people?


## Psalms 80:5 (id: 1819080005)

5You have fed them with the bread of tears, and given them tears to drink in large measure.


## Psalms 80:6 (id: 1819080006)

6You make us a source of contention to our neighbors. Our enemies laugh among themselves.


## Psalms 80:7 (id: 1819080007)

7Turn us again, God of Armies. Cause your face to shine, and we will be saved.


## Psalms 80:8 (id: 1819080008)

8You brought a vine out of Egypt. You drove out the nations, and planted it.


## Psalms 80:9 (id: 1819080009)

9You cleared the ground for it. It took deep root, and filled the land.


## Psalms 80:10 (id: 1819080010)

10The mountains were covered with its shadow. Its boughs were like God’s cedars.


## Psalms 80:11 (id: 1819080011)

11It sent out its branches to the sea, its shoots to the River.


## Psalms 80:12 (id: 1819080012)

12Why have you broken down its walls, so that all those who pass by the way pluck it?


## Psalms 80:13 (id: 1819080013)

13The boar out of the wood ravages it. The wild animals of the field feed on it.


## Psalms 80:14 (id: 1819080014)

14Turn again, we beg you, God of Armies. Look down from heaven, and see, and visit this vine,


## Psalms 80:15 (id: 1819080015)

15the stock which your right hand planted, the branch that you made strong for yourself.


## Psalms 80:16 (id: 1819080016)

16It’s burned with fire. It’s cut down. They perish at your rebuke.


## Psalms 80:17 (id: 1819080017)

17Let your hand be on the man of your right hand, on the son of man whom you made strong for yourself.


## Psalms 80:18 (id: 1819080018)

18So we will not turn away from you. Revive us, and we will call on your name.


## Psalms 80:19 (id: 1819080019)

19Turn us again, LORD God of Armies. Cause your face to shine, and we will be saved.


## Psalms 81:1 (id: 1819081001)

1For the Chief Musician. On an instrument of Gath. By Asaph. Sing aloud to God, our strength! Make a joyful shout to the God of Jacob!


## Psalms 81:2 (id: 1819081002)

2Raise a song, and bring here the tambourine, the pleasant lyre with the harp.


## Psalms 81:3 (id: 1819081003)

3Blow the trumpet at the New Moon, at the full moon, on our feast day.


## Psalms 81:4 (id: 1819081004)

4For it is a statute for Israel, an ordinance of the God of Jacob.


## Psalms 81:5 (id: 1819081005)

5He appointed it in Joseph for a covenant, when he went out over the land of Egypt, I heard a language that I didn’t know.


## Psalms 81:6 (id: 1819081006)

6“I removed his shoulder from the burden. His hands were freed from the basket.


## Psalms 81:7 (id: 1819081007)

7You called in trouble, and I delivered you. I answered you in the secret place of thunder. I tested you at the waters of Meribah.” Selah.


## Psalms 81:8 (id: 1819081008)

8“Hear, my people, and I will testify to you, Israel, if you would listen to me!


## Psalms 81:9 (id: 1819081009)

9There shall be no strange god in you, neither shall you worship any foreign god.


## Psalms 81:10 (id: 1819081010)

10I am the LORD, your God, who brought you up out of the land of Egypt. Open your mouth wide, and I will fill it.


## Psalms 81:11 (id: 1819081011)

11But my people didn’t listen to my voice. Israel desired none of me.


## Psalms 81:12 (id: 1819081012)

12So I let them go after the stubbornness of their hearts, that they might walk in their own counsels.


## Psalms 81:13 (id: 1819081013)

13Oh that my people would listen to me, that Israel would walk in my ways!


## Psalms 81:14 (id: 1819081014)

14I would soon subdue their enemies, and turn my hand against their adversaries.


## Psalms 81:15 (id: 1819081015)

15The haters of the LORD would cringe before him, and their punishment would last forever.


## Psalms 81:16 (id: 1819081016)

16But he would have also fed them with the finest of the wheat. I will satisfy you with honey out of the rock.”


## Psalms 82:1 (id: 1819082001)

1A Psalm by Asaph. God presides in the great assembly. He judges among the gods.


## Psalms 82:2 (id: 1819082002)

2“How long will you judge unjustly, and show partiality to the wicked?” Selah.


## Psalms 82:3 (id: 1819082003)

3“Defend the weak, the poor, and the fatherless. Maintain the rights of the poor and oppressed.


## Psalms 82:4 (id: 1819082004)

4Rescue the weak and needy. Deliver them out of the hand of the wicked.”


## Psalms 82:5 (id: 1819082005)

5They don’t know, neither do they understand. They walk back and forth in darkness. All the foundations of the earth are shaken.


## Psalms 82:6 (id: 1819082006)

6I said, “You are gods, all of you are sons of the Most High.


## Psalms 82:7 (id: 1819082007)

7Nevertheless you shall die like men, and fall like one of the rulers.”


## Psalms 82:8 (id: 1819082008)

8Arise, God, judge the earth, for you inherit all of the nations.


## Psalms 83:1 (id: 1819083001)

1A song. A Psalm by Asaph. God, don’t keep silent. Don’t keep silent, and don’t be still, God.


## Psalms 83:2 (id: 1819083002)

2For, behold, your enemies are stirred up. Those who hate you have lifted up their heads.


## Psalms 83:3 (id: 1819083003)

3They conspire with cunning against your people. They plot against your cherished ones.


## Psalms 83:4 (id: 1819083004)

4“Come,” they say, “let’s destroy them as a nation, that the name of Israel may be remembered no more.”


## Psalms 83:5 (id: 1819083005)

5For they have conspired together with one mind. They form an alliance against you.


## Psalms 83:6 (id: 1819083006)

6The tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites; Moab, and the Hagrites;


## Psalms 83:7 (id: 1819083007)

7Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek; Philistia with the inhabitants of Tyre;


## Psalms 83:8 (id: 1819083008)

8Assyria also is joined with them. They have helped the children of Lot. Selah.


## Psalms 83:9 (id: 1819083009)

9Do to them as you did to Midian, as to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the river Kishon;


## Psalms 83:10 (id: 1819083010)

10who perished at Endor, who became as dung for the earth.


## Psalms 83:11 (id: 1819083011)

11Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb, yes, all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna,


## Psalms 83:12 (id: 1819083012)

12who said, “Let’s take possession of God’s pasture lands.”


## Psalms 83:13 (id: 1819083013)

13My God, make them like tumbleweed, like chaff before the wind.


## Psalms 83:14 (id: 1819083014)

14As the fire that burns the forest, as the flame that sets the mountains on fire,


## Psalms 83:15 (id: 1819083015)

15so pursue them with your tempest, and terrify them with your storm.


## Psalms 83:16 (id: 1819083016)

16Fill their faces with confusion, that they may seek your name, LORD.


## Psalms 83:17 (id: 1819083017)

17Let them be disappointed and dismayed forever. Yes, let them be confounded and perish;


## Psalms 83:18 (id: 1819083018)

18that they may know that you alone, whose name is the LORD, are the Most High over all the earth.


## Psalms 84:1 (id: 1819084001)

1For the Chief Musician. On an instrument of Gath. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. How lovely are your dwellings, LORD of Armies!


## Psalms 84:2 (id: 1819084002)

2My soul longs, and even faints for the courts of the LORD. My heart and my flesh cry out for the living God.


## Psalms 84:3 (id: 1819084003)

3Yes, the sparrow has found a home, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may have her young, near your altars, LORD of Armies, my King, and my God.


## Psalms 84:4 (id: 1819084004)

4Blessed are those who dwell in your house. They are always praising you. Selah.


## Psalms 84:5 (id: 1819084005)

5Blessed are those whose strength is in you, who have set their hearts on a pilgrimage.


## Psalms 84:6 (id: 1819084006)

6Passing through the valley of Weeping, they make it a place of springs. Yes, the autumn rain covers it with blessings.


## Psalms 84:7 (id: 1819084007)

7They go from strength to strength. Every one of them appears before God in Zion.


## Psalms 84:8 (id: 1819084008)

8LORD, God of Armies, hear my prayer. Listen, God of Jacob. Selah.


## Psalms 84:9 (id: 1819084009)

9Behold, God our shield, look at the face of your anointed.


## Psalms 84:10 (id: 1819084010)

10For a day in your courts is better than a thousand. I would rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God, than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.


## Psalms 84:11 (id: 1819084011)

11For the LORD God is a sun and a shield. The LORD will give grace and glory. He withholds no good thing from those who walk blamelessly.


## Psalms 84:12 (id: 1819084012)

12LORD of Armies, blessed is the man who trusts in you.


## Psalms 85:1 (id: 1819085001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. LORD, you have been favorable to your land. You have restored the fortunes of Jacob.


## Psalms 85:2 (id: 1819085002)

2You have forgiven the iniquity of your people. You have covered all their sin. Selah.


## Psalms 85:3 (id: 1819085003)

3You have taken away all your wrath. You have turned from the fierceness of your anger.


## Psalms 85:4 (id: 1819085004)

4Turn us, God of our salvation, and cause your indignation toward us to cease.


## Psalms 85:5 (id: 1819085005)

5Will you be angry with us forever? Will you draw out your anger to all generations?


## Psalms 85:6 (id: 1819085006)

## Psalms 85:7 (id: 1819085007)

## Psalms 85:8 (id: 1819085008)

## Psalms 85:9 (id: 1819085009)

9Surely his salvation is near those who fear him, that glory may dwell in our land.


## Psalms 85:10 (id: 1819085010)

10Mercy and truth meet together. Righteousness and peace have kissed each other.


## Psalms 85:11 (id: 1819085011)

## Psalms 85:12 (id: 1819085012)

## Psalms 85:13 (id: 1819085013)

## Psalms 86:1 (id: 1819086001)

1A Prayer by David. Hear, LORD, and answer me, for I am poor and needy.


## Psalms 86:2 (id: 1819086002)

2Preserve my soul, for I am godly. You, my God, save your servant who trusts in you.


## Psalms 86:3 (id: 1819086003)

3Be merciful to me, Lord, for I call to you all day long.


## Psalms 86:4 (id: 1819086004)

4Bring joy to the soul of your servant, for to you, Lord, do I lift up my soul.


## Psalms 86:5 (id: 1819086005)

5For you, Lord, are good, and ready to forgive, abundant in loving kindness to all those who call on you.


## Psalms 86:6 (id: 1819086006)

6Hear, LORD, my prayer. Listen to the voice of my petitions.


## Psalms 86:7 (id: 1819086007)

7In the day of my trouble I will call on you, for you will answer me.


## Psalms 86:8 (id: 1819086008)

8There is no one like you among the gods, Lord, nor any deeds like your deeds.


## Psalms 86:9 (id: 1819086009)

9All nations you have made will come and worship before you, Lord. They shall glorify your name.


## Psalms 86:10 (id: 1819086010)

10For you are great, and do wondrous things. You are God alone.


## Psalms 86:11 (id: 1819086011)

11Teach me your way, LORD. I will walk in your truth. Make my heart undivided to fear your name.


## Psalms 86:12 (id: 1819086012)

12I will praise you, Lord my God, with my whole heart. I will glorify your name forever more.


## Psalms 86:13 (id: 1819086013)

13For your loving kindness is great toward me. You have delivered my soul from the lowest Sheol.


## Psalms 86:14 (id: 1819086014)

14God, the proud have risen up against me. A company of violent men have sought after my soul, and they don’t hold regard for you before them.


## Psalms 86:15 (id: 1819086015)

15But you, Lord, are a merciful and gracious God, slow to anger, and abundant in loving kindness and truth.


## Psalms 86:16 (id: 1819086016)

16Turn to me, and have mercy on me! Give your strength to your servant. Save the son of your servant.


## Psalms 86:17 (id: 1819086017)

17Show me a sign of your goodness, that those who hate me may see it, and be shamed, because you, LORD, have helped me, and comforted me.


## Psalms 87:1 (id: 1819087001)

## Psalms 88:1 (id: 1819088001)

1A Song. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Suffering of Affliction.” A contemplation by Heman, the Ezrahite. LORD, the God of my salvation, I have cried day and night before you.


## Psalms 88:2 (id: 1819088002)

2Let my prayer enter into your presence. Turn your ear to my cry.


## Psalms 88:3 (id: 1819088003)

3For my soul is full of troubles. My life draws near to Sheol.


## Psalms 88:4 (id: 1819088004)

4I am counted among those who go down into the pit. I am like a man who has no help,


## Psalms 88:5 (id: 1819088005)

5set apart among the dead, like the slain who lie in the grave, whom you remember no more. They are cut off from your hand.


## Psalms 88:6 (id: 1819088006)

6You have laid me in the lowest pit, in the darkest depths.


## Psalms 88:7 (id: 1819088007)

7Your wrath lies heavily on me. You have afflicted me with all your waves. Selah.


## Psalms 88:8 (id: 1819088008)

8You have taken my friends from me. You have made me an abomination to them. I am confined, and I can’t escape.


## Psalms 88:9 (id: 1819088009)

9My eyes are dim from grief. I have called on you daily, LORD. I have spread out my hands to you.


## Psalms 88:10 (id: 1819088010)

10Do you show wonders to the dead? Do the departed spirits rise up and praise you? Selah.


## Psalms 88:11 (id: 1819088011)

11Is your loving kindness declared in the grave? Or your faithfulness in Destruction?


## Psalms 88:12 (id: 1819088012)

12Are your wonders made known in the dark? Or your righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?


## Psalms 88:13 (id: 1819088013)

13But to you, LORD, I have cried. In the morning, my prayer comes before you.


## Psalms 88:14 (id: 1819088014)

14LORD, why do you reject my soul? Why do you hide your face from me?


## Psalms 88:15 (id: 1819088015)

15I am afflicted and ready to die from my youth up. While I suffer your terrors, I am distracted.


## Psalms 88:16 (id: 1819088016)

16Your fierce wrath has gone over me. Your terrors have cut me off.


## Psalms 88:17 (id: 1819088017)

17They came around me like water all day long. They completely engulfed me.


## Psalms 88:18 (id: 1819088018)

18You have put lover and friend far from me, and my friends into darkness.


## Psalms 89:1 (id: 1819089001)

1A contemplation by Ethan, the Ezrahite. I will sing of the loving kindness of the LORD forever. With my mouth, I will make known your faithfulness to all generations.


## Psalms 89:2 (id: 1819089002)

2I indeed declare, “Love stands firm forever. You established the heavens. Your faithfulness is in them.”


## Psalms 89:3 (id: 1819089003)

3“I have made a covenant with my chosen one, I have sworn to David, my servant,


## Psalms 89:4 (id: 1819089004)

4‘I will establish your offspring forever, and build up your throne to all generations.’” Selah.


## Psalms 89:5 (id: 1819089005)

5The heavens will praise your wonders, LORD, your faithfulness also in the assembly of the holy ones.


## Psalms 89:6 (id: 1819089006)

6For who in the skies can be compared to the LORD? Who among the sons of the heavenly beings is like the LORD,


## Psalms 89:7 (id: 1819089007)

7a very awesome God in the council of the holy ones, to be feared above all those who are around him?


## Psalms 89:8 (id: 1819089008)

8LORD, God of Armies, who is a mighty one, like you? LORD, your faithfulness is around you.


## Psalms 89:9 (id: 1819089009)

9You rule the pride of the sea. When its waves rise up, you calm them.


## Psalms 89:10 (id: 1819089010)

10You have broken Rahab in pieces, like one of the slain. You have scattered your enemies with your mighty arm.


## Psalms 89:11 (id: 1819089011)

11The heavens are yours. The earth also is yours, the world and its fullness. You have founded them.


## Psalms 89:12 (id: 1819089012)

12You have created the north and the south. Tabor and Hermon rejoice in your name.


## Psalms 89:13 (id: 1819089013)

13You have a mighty arm. Your hand is strong, and your right hand is exalted.


## Psalms 89:14 (id: 1819089014)

14Righteousness and justice are the foundation of your throne. Loving kindness and truth go before your face.


## Psalms 89:15 (id: 1819089015)

15Blessed are the people who learn to acclaim you. They walk in the light of your presence, LORD.


## Psalms 89:16 (id: 1819089016)

16In your name they rejoice all day. In your righteousness, they are exalted.


## Psalms 89:17 (id: 1819089017)

17For you are the glory of their strength. In your favor, our horn will be exalted.


## Psalms 89:18 (id: 1819089018)

18For our shield belongs to the LORD, our king to the Holy One of Israel.


## Psalms 89:19 (id: 1819089019)

19Then you spoke in vision to your saints, and said, “I have given strength to the warrior. I have exalted a young man from the people.


## Psalms 89:20 (id: 1819089020)

20I have found David, my servant. I have anointed him with my holy oil,


## Psalms 89:21 (id: 1819089021)

21with whom my hand shall be established. My arm will also strengthen him.


## Psalms 89:22 (id: 1819089022)

22No enemy will tax him. No wicked man will oppress him.


## Psalms 89:23 (id: 1819089023)

23I will beat down his adversaries before him, and strike those who hate him.


## Psalms 89:24 (id: 1819089024)

24But my faithfulness and my loving kindness will be with him. In my name, his horn will be exalted.


## Psalms 89:25 (id: 1819089025)

25I will set his hand also on the sea, and his right hand on the rivers.


## Psalms 89:26 (id: 1819089026)

26He will call to me, ‘You are my Father, my God, and the rock of my salvation!’


## Psalms 89:27 (id: 1819089027)

27I will also appoint him my firstborn, the highest of the kings of the earth.


## Psalms 89:28 (id: 1819089028)

28I will keep my loving kindness for him forever more. My covenant will stand firm with him.


## Psalms 89:29 (id: 1819089029)

29I will also make his offspring endure forever, and his throne as the days of heaven.


## Psalms 89:30 (id: 1819089030)

30If his children forsake my law, and don’t walk in my ordinances;


## Psalms 89:31 (id: 1819089031)

31if they break my statutes, and don’t keep my commandments;


## Psalms 89:32 (id: 1819089032)

32then I will punish their sin with the rod, and their iniquity with stripes.


## Psalms 89:33 (id: 1819089033)

33But I will not completely take my loving kindness from him, nor allow my faithfulness to fail.


## Psalms 89:34 (id: 1819089034)

34I will not break my covenant, nor alter what my lips have uttered.


## Psalms 89:35 (id: 1819089035)

35Once I have sworn by my holiness, I will not lie to David.


## Psalms 89:36 (id: 1819089036)

36His offspring will endure forever, his throne like the sun before me.


## Psalms 89:37 (id: 1819089037)

37It will be established forever like the moon, the faithful witness in the sky.” Selah.


## Psalms 89:38 (id: 1819089038)

38But you have rejected and spurned. You have been angry with your anointed.


## Psalms 89:39 (id: 1819089039)

39You have renounced the covenant of your servant. You have defiled his crown in the dust.


## Psalms 89:40 (id: 1819089040)

40You have broken down all his hedges. You have brought his strongholds to ruin.


## Psalms 89:41 (id: 1819089041)

41All who pass by the way rob him. He has become a reproach to his neighbors.


## Psalms 89:42 (id: 1819089042)

42You have exalted the right hand of his adversaries. You have made all of his enemies rejoice.


## Psalms 89:43 (id: 1819089043)

43Yes, you turn back the edge of his sword, and haven’t supported him in battle.


## Psalms 89:44 (id: 1819089044)

44You have ended his splendor, and thrown his throne down to the ground.


## Psalms 89:45 (id: 1819089045)

45You have shortened the days of his youth. You have covered him with shame. Selah.


## Psalms 89:46 (id: 1819089046)

46How long, LORD? Will you hide yourself forever? Will your wrath burn like fire?


## Psalms 89:47 (id: 1819089047)

47Remember how short my time is, for what vanity you have created all the children of men!


## Psalms 89:48 (id: 1819089048)

48What man is he who shall live and not see death, who shall deliver his soul from the power of Sheol? Selah.


## Psalms 89:49 (id: 1819089049)

49Lord, where are your former loving kindnesses, which you swore to David in your faithfulness?


## Psalms 89:50 (id: 1819089050)

50Remember, Lord, the reproach of your servants, how I bear in my heart the taunts of all the mighty peoples,


## Psalms 89:51 (id: 1819089051)

51With which your enemies have mocked, LORD, with which they have mocked the footsteps of your anointed one.

52Blessed be the LORD forever more. Amen, and Amen.


## Psalms 90:1 (id: 1819090001)

1A Prayer by Moses, the man of God. Lord, you have been our dwelling place for all generations.


## Psalms 90:2 (id: 1819090002)

2Before the mountains were born, before you had formed the earth and the world, even from everlasting to everlasting, you are God.


## Psalms 90:3 (id: 1819090003)

3You turn man to destruction, saying, “Return, you children of men.”


## Psalms 90:4 (id: 1819090004)

4For a thousand years in your sight are just like yesterday when it is past, like a watch in the night.


## Psalms 90:5 (id: 1819090005)

5You sweep them away as they sleep. In the morning they sprout like new grass.


## Psalms 90:6 (id: 1819090006)

6In the morning it sprouts and springs up. By evening, it is withered and dry.


## Psalms 90:7 (id: 1819090007)

7For we are consumed in your anger. We are troubled in your wrath.


## Psalms 90:8 (id: 1819090008)

8You have set our iniquities before you, our secret sins in the light of your presence.


## Psalms 90:9 (id: 1819090009)

9For all our days have passed away in your wrath. We bring our years to an end as a sigh.


## Psalms 90:10 (id: 1819090010)

10The days of our years are seventy, or even by reason of strength eighty years; yet their pride is but labor and sorrow, for it passes quickly, and we fly away.


## Psalms 90:11 (id: 1819090011)

11Who knows the power of your anger, your wrath according to the fear that is due to you?


## Psalms 90:12 (id: 1819090012)

12So teach us to count our days, that we may gain a heart of wisdom.


## Psalms 90:13 (id: 1819090013)

13Relent, LORD! How long? Have compassion on your servants!


## Psalms 90:14 (id: 1819090014)

14Satisfy us in the morning with your loving kindness, that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.


## Psalms 90:15 (id: 1819090015)

15Make us glad for as many days as you have afflicted us, for as many years as we have seen evil.


## Psalms 90:16 (id: 1819090016)

16Let your work appear to your servants, your glory to their children.


## Psalms 90:17 (id: 1819090017)

17Let the favor of the Lord our God be on us. Establish the work of our hands for us. Yes, establish the work of our hands.


## Psalms 91:1 (id: 1819091001)

1He who dwells in the secret place of the Most High will rest in the shadow of the Almighty.


## Psalms 91:2 (id: 1819091002)

2I will say of the LORD, “He is my refuge and my fortress; my God, in whom I trust.”


## Psalms 91:3 (id: 1819091003)

3For he will deliver you from the snare of the fowler, and from the deadly pestilence.


## Psalms 91:4 (id: 1819091004)

4He will cover you with his feathers. Under his wings you will take refuge. His faithfulness is your shield and rampart.


## Psalms 91:5 (id: 1819091005)

5You shall not be afraid of the terror by night, nor of the arrow that flies by day,


## Psalms 91:6 (id: 1819091006)

6nor of the pestilence that walks in darkness, nor of the destruction that wastes at noonday.


## Psalms 91:7 (id: 1819091007)

7A thousand may fall at your side, and ten thousand at your right hand; but it will not come near you.


## Psalms 91:8 (id: 1819091008)

8You will only look with your eyes, and see the recompense of the wicked.


## Psalms 91:9 (id: 1819091009)

9Because you have made the LORD your refuge, and the Most High your dwelling place,


## Psalms 91:10 (id: 1819091010)

10no evil shall happen to you, neither shall any plague come near your dwelling.


## Psalms 91:11 (id: 1819091011)

11For he will put his angels in charge of you, to guard you in all your ways.


## Psalms 91:12 (id: 1819091012)

12They will bear you up in their hands, so that you won’t dash your foot against a stone.


## Psalms 91:13 (id: 1819091013)

13You will tread on the lion and cobra. You will trample the young lion and the serpent underfoot.


## Psalms 91:14 (id: 1819091014)

14“Because he has set his love on me, therefore I will deliver him. I will set him on high, because he has known my name.


## Psalms 91:15 (id: 1819091015)

15He will call on me, and I will answer him. I will be with him in trouble. I will deliver him, and honor him.


## Psalms 91:16 (id: 1819091016)

16I will satisfy him with long life, and show him my salvation.”


## Psalms 92:1 (id: 1819092001)

1A Psalm. A song for the Sabbath day. It is a good thing to give thanks to the LORD, to sing praises to your name, Most High,


## Psalms 92:2 (id: 1819092002)

2to proclaim your loving kindness in the morning, and your faithfulness every night,


## Psalms 92:3 (id: 1819092003)

3with the ten\-stringed lute, with the harp, and with the melody of the lyre.


## Psalms 92:4 (id: 1819092004)

4For you, LORD, have made me glad through your work. I will triumph in the works of your hands.


## Psalms 92:5 (id: 1819092005)

5How great are your works, LORD! Your thoughts are very deep.


## Psalms 92:6 (id: 1819092006)

6A senseless man doesn’t know, neither does a fool understand this:


## Psalms 92:7 (id: 1819092007)

7though the wicked spring up as the grass, and all the evildoers flourish, they will be destroyed forever.


## Psalms 92:8 (id: 1819092008)

8But you, LORD, are on high forever more.


## Psalms 92:9 (id: 1819092009)

9For behold, your enemies, LORD, for behold, your enemies shall perish. All the evildoers will be scattered.


## Psalms 92:10 (id: 1819092010)

10But you have exalted my horn like that of the wild ox. I am anointed with fresh oil.


## Psalms 92:11 (id: 1819092011)

11My eye has also seen my enemies. My ears have heard of the wicked enemies who rise up against me.


## Psalms 92:12 (id: 1819092012)

12The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree. He will grow like a cedar in Lebanon.


## Psalms 92:13 (id: 1819092013)

13They are planted in the LORD’s house. They will flourish in our God’s courts.


## Psalms 92:14 (id: 1819092014)

14They will still produce fruit in old age. They will be full of sap and green,


## Psalms 92:15 (id: 1819092015)

15to show that the LORD is upright. He is my rock, and there is no unrighteousness in him.

1The LORD reigns! He is clothed with majesty! The LORD is armed with strength. The world also is established. It can’t be moved.


## Psalms 93:2 (id: 1819093002)

2Your throne is established from long ago. You are from everlasting.

## Psalms 93:5 (id: 1819093005)
