## Psalms 94:1 (id: 1819094001)

1LORD, you God to whom vengeance belongs, you God to whom vengeance belongs, shine out.


## Psalms 94:2 (id: 1819094002)

2Rise up, you judge of the earth. Pay back the proud what they deserve.


## Psalms 94:3 (id: 1819094003)

3LORD, how long will the wicked, how long will the wicked triumph?


## Psalms 94:4 (id: 1819094004)

4They pour out arrogant words. All the evildoers boast.


## Psalms 94:5 (id: 1819094005)

5They break your people in pieces, LORD, and afflict your heritage.


## Psalms 94:6 (id: 1819094006)

6They kill the widow and the alien, and murder the fatherless.


## Psalms 94:7 (id: 1819094007)

7They say, “The LORD will not see, neither will Jacob’s God consider.”


## Psalms 94:8 (id: 1819094008)

8Consider, you senseless among the people; you fools, when will you be wise?


## Psalms 94:9 (id: 1819094009)

9He who implanted the ear, won’t he hear? He who formed the eye, won’t he see?


## Psalms 94:10 (id: 1819094010)

10He who disciplines the nations, won’t he punish? He who teaches man knows.


## Psalms 94:11 (id: 1819094011)

11The LORD knows the thoughts of man, that they are futile.


## Psalms 94:12 (id: 1819094012)

12Blessed is the man whom you discipline, LORD, and teach out of your law,


## Psalms 94:13 (id: 1819094013)

13that you may give him rest from the days of adversity, until the pit is dug for the wicked.


## Psalms 94:14 (id: 1819094014)

14For the LORD won’t reject his people, neither will he forsake his inheritance.


## Psalms 94:15 (id: 1819094015)

15For judgment will return to righteousness. All the upright in heart shall follow it.


## Psalms 94:16 (id: 1819094016)

16Who will rise up for me against the wicked? Who will stand up for me against the evildoers?


## Psalms 94:17 (id: 1819094017)

17Unless the LORD had been my help, my soul would have soon lived in silence.


## Psalms 94:18 (id: 1819094018)

18When I said, “My foot is slipping!” Your loving kindness, LORD, held me up.


## Psalms 94:19 (id: 1819094019)

19In the multitude of my thoughts within me, your comforts delight my soul.


## Psalms 94:20 (id: 1819094020)

20Shall the throne of wickedness have fellowship with you, which brings about mischief by statute?


## Psalms 94:21 (id: 1819094021)

21They gather themselves together against the soul of the righteous, and condemn the innocent blood.


## Psalms 94:22 (id: 1819094022)

22But the LORD has been my high tower, my God, the rock of my refuge.


## Psalms 94:23 (id: 1819094023)

23He has brought on them their own iniquity, and will cut them off in their own wickedness. The LORD, our God, will cut them off.


## Psalms 95:1 (id: 1819095001)

1Oh come, let’s sing to the LORD. Let’s shout aloud to the rock of our salvation!


## Psalms 95:2 (id: 1819095002)

2Let’s come before his presence with thanksgiving. Let’s extol him with songs!


## Psalms 95:3 (id: 1819095003)

3For the LORD is a great God, a great King above all gods.


## Psalms 95:4 (id: 1819095004)

4In his hand are the deep places of the earth. The heights of the mountains are also his.


## Psalms 95:5 (id: 1819095005)

5The sea is his, and he made it. His hands formed the dry land.


## Psalms 95:6 (id: 1819095006)

6Oh come, let’s worship and bow down. Let’s kneel before the LORD, our Maker,


## Psalms 95:7 (id: 1819095007)

7for he is our God. We are the people of his pasture, and the sheep in his care. Today, oh that you would hear his voice!


## Psalms 95:8 (id: 1819095008)

8Don’t harden your heart, as at Meribah, as in the day of Massah in the wilderness,


## Psalms 95:9 (id: 1819095009)

9when your fathers tempted me, tested me, and saw my work.


## Psalms 95:10 (id: 1819095010)

10Forty long years I was grieved with that generation, and said, “They are a people who err in their heart. They have not known my ways.”


## Psalms 95:11 (id: 1819095011)

11Therefore I swore in my wrath, “They won’t enter into my rest.”


## Psalms 96:1 (id: 1819096001)

1Sing to the LORD a new song! Sing to the LORD, all the earth.


## Psalms 96:2 (id: 1819096002)

2Sing to the LORD! Bless his name! Proclaim his salvation from day to day!


## Psalms 96:3 (id: 1819096003)

3Declare his glory among the nations, his marvelous works among all the peoples.


## Psalms 96:4 (id: 1819096004)

4For the LORD is great, and greatly to be praised! He is to be feared above all gods.


## Psalms 96:5 (id: 1819096005)

5For all the gods of the peoples are idols, but the LORD made the heavens.


## Psalms 96:6 (id: 1819096006)

6Honor and majesty are before him. Strength and beauty are in his sanctuary.


## Psalms 96:7 (id: 1819096007)

7Ascribe to the LORD, you families of nations, ascribe to the LORD glory and strength.


## Psalms 96:8 (id: 1819096008)

8Ascribe to the LORD the glory due to his name. Bring an offering, and come into his courts.


## Psalms 96:9 (id: 1819096009)

9Worship the LORD in holy array. Tremble before him, all the earth.


## Psalms 96:10 (id: 1819096010)

10Say among the nations, “The LORD reigns.” The world is also established. It can’t be moved. He will judge the peoples with equity.


## Psalms 96:11 (id: 1819096011)

11Let the heavens be glad, and let the earth rejoice. Let the sea roar, and its fullness!


## Psalms 96:12 (id: 1819096012)

12Let the field and all that is in it exult! Then all the trees of the woods shall sing for joy


## Psalms 96:13 (id: 1819096013)

13before the LORD; for he comes, for he comes to judge the earth. He will judge the world with righteousness, the peoples with his truth.


## Psalms 97:1 (id: 1819097001)

1The LORD reigns! Let the earth rejoice! Let the multitude of islands be glad!


## Psalms 97:2 (id: 1819097002)

2Clouds and darkness are around him. Righteousness and justice are the foundation of his throne.


## Psalms 97:3 (id: 1819097003)

3A fire goes before him, and burns up his adversaries on every side.


## Psalms 97:4 (id: 1819097004)

4His lightning lights up the world. The earth sees, and trembles.


## Psalms 97:5 (id: 1819097005)

5The mountains melt like wax at the presence of the LORD, at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.


## Psalms 97:6 (id: 1819097006)

6The heavens declare his righteousness. All the peoples have seen his glory.


## Psalms 97:7 (id: 1819097007)

7Let all them be shamed who serve engraved images, who boast in their idols. Worship him, all you gods!


## Psalms 97:8 (id: 1819097008)

8Zion heard and was glad. The daughters of Judah rejoiced because of your judgments, LORD.


## Psalms 97:9 (id: 1819097009)

9For you, LORD, are most high above all the earth. You are exalted far above all gods.


## Psalms 97:10 (id: 1819097010)

10You who love the LORD, hate evil! He preserves the souls of his saints. He delivers them out of the hand of the wicked.


## Psalms 97:11 (id: 1819097011)

11Light is sown for the righteous, and gladness for the upright in heart.


## Psalms 97:12 (id: 1819097012)

12Be glad in the LORD, you righteous people! Give thanks to his holy Name.


## Psalms 98:1 (id: 1819098001)

1A Psalm. Sing to the LORD a new song, for he has done marvelous things! His right hand and his holy arm have worked salvation for him.


## Psalms 98:2 (id: 1819098002)

2The LORD has made known his salvation. He has openly shown his righteousness in the sight of the nations.


## Psalms 98:3 (id: 1819098003)

3He has remembered his loving kindness and his faithfulness toward the house of Israel. All the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.


## Psalms 98:4 (id: 1819098004)

4Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth! Burst out and sing for joy, yes, sing praises!


## Psalms 98:5 (id: 1819098005)

5Sing praises to the LORD with the harp, with the harp and the voice of melody.


## Psalms 98:6 (id: 1819098006)

6With trumpets and sound of the ram’s horn, make a joyful noise before the King, the LORD.


## Psalms 98:7 (id: 1819098007)

7Let the sea roar with its fullness; the world, and those who dwell therein.


## Psalms 98:8 (id: 1819098008)

8Let the rivers clap their hands. Let the mountains sing for joy together.


## Psalms 98:9 (id: 1819098009)

9Let them sing before the LORD, for he comes to judge the earth. He will judge the world with righteousness, and the peoples with equity.


## Psalms 99:1 (id: 1819099001)

1The LORD reigns! Let the peoples tremble. He sits enthroned among the cherubim. Let the earth be moved.


## Psalms 99:2 (id: 1819099002)

2The LORD is great in Zion. He is high above all the peoples.


## Psalms 99:3 (id: 1819099003)

3Let them praise your great and awesome name. He is Holy!


## Psalms 99:4 (id: 1819099004)

4The King’s strength also loves justice. You establish equity. You execute justice and righteousness in Jacob.


## Psalms 99:5 (id: 1819099005)

5Exalt the LORD our God. Worship at his footstool. He is Holy!


## Psalms 99:6 (id: 1819099006)

6Moses and Aaron were among his priests, Samuel was among those who call on his name. They called on the LORD, and he answered them.


## Psalms 99:7 (id: 1819099007)

7He spoke to them in the pillar of cloud. They kept his testimonies, the statute that he gave them.


## Psalms 99:8 (id: 1819099008)

8You answered them, LORD our God. You are a God who forgave them, although you took vengeance for their doings.


## Psalms 99:9 (id: 1819099009)

9Exalt the LORD, our God. Worship at his holy hill, for the LORD, our God, is holy!


## Psalms 100:1 (id: 1819100001)

1A Psalm of thanksgiving. Shout for joy to the LORD, all you lands!


## Psalms 100:2 (id: 1819100002)

2Serve the LORD with gladness. Come before his presence with singing.


## Psalms 100:3 (id: 1819100003)

3Know that the LORD, he is God. It is he who has made us, and we are his. We are his people, and the sheep of his pasture.


## Psalms 100:4 (id: 1819100004)

4Enter into his gates with thanksgiving, and into his courts with praise. Give thanks to him, and bless his name.


## Psalms 100:5 (id: 1819100005)

5For the LORD is good. His loving kindness endures forever, his faithfulness to all generations.


## Psalms 101:1 (id: 1819101001)

1A Psalm by David. I will sing of loving kindness and justice. To you, LORD, I will sing praises.


## Psalms 101:2 (id: 1819101002)

2I will be careful to live a blameless life. When will you come to me? I will walk within my house with a blameless heart.


## Psalms 101:3 (id: 1819101003)

3I will set no vile thing before my eyes. I hate the deeds of faithless men. They will not cling to me.


## Psalms 101:4 (id: 1819101004)

4A perverse heart will be far from me. I will have nothing to do with evil.


## Psalms 101:5 (id: 1819101005)

5I will silence whoever secretly slanders his neighbor. I won’t tolerate one who is arrogant and conceited.


## Psalms 101:6 (id: 1819101006)

6My eyes will be on the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me. He who walks in a perfect way, he will serve me.


## Psalms 101:7 (id: 1819101007)

7He who practices deceit won’t dwell within my house. He who speaks falsehood won’t be established before my eyes.


## Psalms 101:8 (id: 1819101008)

8Morning by morning, I will destroy all the wicked of the land, to cut off all the workers of iniquity from the LORD’s city.


## Psalms 102:1 (id: 1819102001)

1A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed and pours out his complaint before the LORD. Hear my prayer, LORD! Let my cry come to you.


## Psalms 102:2 (id: 1819102002)

2Don’t hide your face from me in the day of my distress. Turn your ear to me. Answer me quickly in the day when I call.


## Psalms 102:3 (id: 1819102003)

3For my days consume away like smoke. My bones are burned as a torch.


## Psalms 102:4 (id: 1819102004)

4My heart is blighted like grass, and withered, for I forget to eat my bread.


## Psalms 102:5 (id: 1819102005)

5By reason of the voice of my groaning, my bones stick to my skin.


## Psalms 102:6 (id: 1819102006)

6I am like a pelican of the wilderness. I have become as an owl of the waste places.


## Psalms 102:7 (id: 1819102007)

7I watch, and have become like a sparrow that is alone on the housetop.


## Psalms 102:8 (id: 1819102008)

8My enemies reproach me all day. Those who are mad at me use my name as a curse.


## Psalms 102:9 (id: 1819102009)

9For I have eaten ashes like bread, and mixed my drink with tears,


## Psalms 102:10 (id: 1819102010)

10because of your indignation and your wrath; for you have taken me up and thrown me away.


## Psalms 102:11 (id: 1819102011)

11My days are like a long shadow. I have withered like grass.


## Psalms 102:12 (id: 1819102012)

12But you, LORD, will remain forever; your renown endures to all generations.


## Psalms 102:13 (id: 1819102013)

13You will arise and have mercy on Zion, for it is time to have pity on her. Yes, the set time has come.


## Psalms 102:14 (id: 1819102014)

14For your servants take pleasure in her stones, and have pity on her dust.


## Psalms 102:15 (id: 1819102015)

15So the nations will fear the LORD’s name, all the kings of the earth your glory.


## Psalms 102:16 (id: 1819102016)

16For the LORD has built up Zion. He has appeared in his glory.


## Psalms 102:17 (id: 1819102017)

17He has responded to the prayer of the destitute, and has not despised their prayer.


## Psalms 102:18 (id: 1819102018)

18This will be written for the generation to come. A people which will be created will praise the LORD,


## Psalms 102:19 (id: 1819102019)

19for he has looked down from the height of his sanctuary. From heaven, the LORD saw the earth,


## Psalms 102:20 (id: 1819102020)

20to hear the groans of the prisoner, to free those who are condemned to death,


## Psalms 102:21 (id: 1819102021)

21that men may declare the LORD’s name in Zion, and his praise in Jerusalem,


## Psalms 102:22 (id: 1819102022)

22when the peoples are gathered together, the kingdoms, to serve the LORD.


## Psalms 102:23 (id: 1819102023)

23He weakened my strength along the course. He shortened my days.


## Psalms 102:24 (id: 1819102024)

24I said, “My God, don’t take me away in the middle of my days. Your years are throughout all generations.


## Psalms 102:25 (id: 1819102025)

25Of old, you laid the foundation of the earth. The heavens are the work of your hands.


## Psalms 102:26 (id: 1819102026)

26They will perish, but you will endure. Yes, all of them will wear out like a garment. You will change them like a cloak, and they will be changed.


## Psalms 102:27 (id: 1819102027)

27But you are the same. Your years will have no end.


## Psalms 102:28 (id: 1819102028)

28The children of your servants will continue. Their offspring will be established before you.”


## Psalms 103:1 (id: 1819103001)

1By David. Praise the LORD, my soul! All that is within me, praise his holy name!


## Psalms 103:2 (id: 1819103002)

2Praise the LORD, my soul, and don’t forget all his benefits,


## Psalms 103:3 (id: 1819103003)

3who forgives all your sins, who heals all your diseases,


## Psalms 103:4 (id: 1819103004)

4who redeems your life from destruction, who crowns you with loving kindness and tender mercies,


## Psalms 103:5 (id: 1819103005)

5who satisfies your desire with good things, so that your youth is renewed like the eagle’s.


## Psalms 103:6 (id: 1819103006)

6The LORD executes righteous acts, and justice for all who are oppressed.


## Psalms 103:7 (id: 1819103007)

7He made known his ways to Moses, his deeds to the children of Israel.


## Psalms 103:8 (id: 1819103008)

8The LORD is merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and abundant in loving kindness.


## Psalms 103:9 (id: 1819103009)

9He will not always accuse; neither will he stay angry forever.


## Psalms 103:10 (id: 1819103010)

10He has not dealt with us according to our sins, nor repaid us for our iniquities.


## Psalms 103:11 (id: 1819103011)

11For as the heavens are high above the earth, so great is his loving kindness toward those who fear him.


## Psalms 103:12 (id: 1819103012)

12As far as the east is from the west, so far has he removed our transgressions from us.


## Psalms 103:13 (id: 1819103013)

13Like a father has compassion on his children, so the LORD has compassion on those who fear him.


## Psalms 103:14 (id: 1819103014)

14For he knows how we are made. He remembers that we are dust.


## Psalms 103:15 (id: 1819103015)

15As for man, his days are like grass. As a flower of the field, so he flourishes.


## Psalms 103:16 (id: 1819103016)

16For the wind passes over it, and it is gone. Its place remembers it no more.


## Psalms 103:17 (id: 1819103017)

17But the LORD’s loving kindness is from everlasting to everlasting with those who fear him, his righteousness to children’s children,


## Psalms 103:18 (id: 1819103018)

18to those who keep his covenant, to those who remember to obey his precepts.


## Psalms 103:19 (id: 1819103019)

19The LORD has established his throne in the heavens. His kingdom rules over all.


## Psalms 103:20 (id: 1819103020)

20Praise the LORD, you angels of his, who are mighty in strength, who fulfill his word, obeying the voice of his word.


## Psalms 103:21 (id: 1819103021)

21Praise the LORD, all you armies of his, you servants of his, who do his pleasure.


## Psalms 103:22 (id: 1819103022)

22Praise the LORD, all you works of his, in all places of his dominion. Praise the LORD, my soul!


## Psalms 104:1 (id: 1819104001)

1Bless the LORD, my soul. The LORD, my God, you are very great. You are clothed with honor and majesty.


## Psalms 104:2 (id: 1819104002)

2He covers himself with light as with a garment. He stretches out the heavens like a curtain.


## Psalms 104:3 (id: 1819104003)

3He lays the beams of his rooms in the waters. He makes the clouds his chariot. He walks on the wings of the wind.


## Psalms 104:4 (id: 1819104004)

4He makes his messengers winds, and his servants flames of fire.


## Psalms 104:5 (id: 1819104005)

5He laid the foundations of the earth, that it should not be moved forever.


## Psalms 104:6 (id: 1819104006)

6You covered it with the deep as with a cloak. The waters stood above the mountains.


## Psalms 104:7 (id: 1819104007)

7At your rebuke they fled. At the voice of your thunder they hurried away.


## Psalms 104:8 (id: 1819104008)

8The mountains rose, the valleys sank down, to the place which you had assigned to them.


## Psalms 104:9 (id: 1819104009)

9You have set a boundary that they may not pass over, that they don’t turn again to cover the earth.


## Psalms 104:10 (id: 1819104010)

10He sends springs into the valleys. They run among the mountains.


## Psalms 104:11 (id: 1819104011)

11They give drink to every animal of the field. The wild donkeys quench their thirst.


## Psalms 104:12 (id: 1819104012)

12The birds of the sky nest by them. They sing among the branches.


## Psalms 104:13 (id: 1819104013)

13He waters the mountains from his rooms. The earth is filled with the fruit of your works.


## Psalms 104:14 (id: 1819104014)

14He causes the grass to grow for the livestock, and plants for man to cultivate, that he may produce food out of the earth:


## Psalms 104:15 (id: 1819104015)

15wine that makes the heart of man glad, oil to make his face to shine, and bread that strengthens man’s heart.


## Psalms 104:16 (id: 1819104016)

16The LORD’s trees are well watered, the cedars of Lebanon, which he has planted,


## Psalms 104:17 (id: 1819104017)

17where the birds make their nests. The stork makes its home in the cypress trees.


## Psalms 104:18 (id: 1819104018)

18The high mountains are for the wild goats. The rocks are a refuge for the rock badgers.


## Psalms 104:19 (id: 1819104019)

19He appointed the moon for seasons. The sun knows when to set.


## Psalms 104:20 (id: 1819104020)

20You make darkness, and it is night, in which all the animals of the forest prowl.


## Psalms 104:21 (id: 1819104021)

21The young lions roar after their prey, and seek their food from God.


## Psalms 104:22 (id: 1819104022)

22The sun rises, and they steal away, and lie down in their dens.


## Psalms 104:23 (id: 1819104023)

23Man goes out to his work, to his labor until the evening.


## Psalms 104:24 (id: 1819104024)

24LORD, how many are your works! In wisdom, you have made them all. The earth is full of your riches.


## Psalms 104:25 (id: 1819104025)

25There is the sea, great and wide, in which are innumerable living things, both small and large animals.


## Psalms 104:26 (id: 1819104026)

26There the ships go, and leviathan, whom you formed to play there.


## Psalms 104:27 (id: 1819104027)

27These all wait for you, that you may give them their food in due season.


## Psalms 104:28 (id: 1819104028)

28You give to them; they gather. You open your hand; they are satisfied with good.


## Psalms 104:29 (id: 1819104029)

29You hide your face; they are troubled. You take away their breath; they die and return to the dust.


## Psalms 104:30 (id: 1819104030)

30You send out your Spirit and they are created. You renew the face of the ground.


## Psalms 104:31 (id: 1819104031)

31Let the LORD’s glory endure forever. Let the LORD rejoice in his works.


## Psalms 104:32 (id: 1819104032)

32He looks at the earth, and it trembles. He touches the mountains, and they smoke.


## Psalms 104:33 (id: 1819104033)

33I will sing to the LORD as long as I live. I will sing praise to my God while I have any being.


## Psalms 104:34 (id: 1819104034)

34Let my meditation be sweet to him. I will rejoice in the LORD.


## Psalms 104:35 (id: 1819104035)

35Let sinners be consumed out of the earth. Let the wicked be no more. Bless the LORD, my soul. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 105:1 (id: 1819105001)

1Give thanks to the LORD! Call on his name! Make his doings known among the peoples.


## Psalms 105:2 (id: 1819105002)

2Sing to him, sing praises to him! Tell of all his marvelous works.


## Psalms 105:3 (id: 1819105003)

3Glory in his holy name. Let the heart of those who seek the LORD rejoice.


## Psalms 105:4 (id: 1819105004)

4Seek the LORD and his strength. Seek his face forever more.


## Psalms 105:5 (id: 1819105005)

5Remember his marvelous works that he has done: his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth,


## Psalms 105:6 (id: 1819105006)

6you offspring of Abraham, his servant, you children of Jacob, his chosen ones.


## Psalms 105:7 (id: 1819105007)

7He is the LORD, our God. His judgments are in all the earth.


## Psalms 105:8 (id: 1819105008)

8He has remembered his covenant forever, the word which he commanded to a thousand generations,


## Psalms 105:9 (id: 1819105009)

9the covenant which he made with Abraham, his oath to Isaac,


## Psalms 105:10 (id: 1819105010)

10and confirmed it to Jacob for a statute; to Israel for an everlasting covenant,


## Psalms 105:11 (id: 1819105011)

11saying, “To you I will give the land of Canaan, the lot of your inheritance,”


## Psalms 105:12 (id: 1819105012)

12when they were but a few men in number, yes, very few, and foreigners in it.


## Psalms 105:13 (id: 1819105013)

13They went about from nation to nation, from one kingdom to another people.


## Psalms 105:14 (id: 1819105014)

14He allowed no one to do them wrong. Yes, he reproved kings for their sakes,


## Psalms 105:15 (id: 1819105015)

15“Don’t touch my anointed ones! Do my prophets no harm!”


## Psalms 105:16 (id: 1819105016)

16He called for a famine on the land. He destroyed the food supplies.


## Psalms 105:17 (id: 1819105017)

17He sent a man before them. Joseph was sold for a slave.


## Psalms 105:18 (id: 1819105018)

18They bruised his feet with shackles. His neck was locked in irons,


## Psalms 105:19 (id: 1819105019)

19until the time that his word happened, and the LORD’s word proved him true.


## Psalms 105:20 (id: 1819105020)

20The king sent and freed him, even the ruler of peoples, and let him go free.


## Psalms 105:21 (id: 1819105021)

21He made him lord of his house, and ruler of all of his possessions,


## Psalms 105:22 (id: 1819105022)

22to discipline his princes at his pleasure, and to teach his elders wisdom.


## Psalms 105:23 (id: 1819105023)

23Israel also came into Egypt. Jacob lived in the land of Ham.


## Psalms 105:24 (id: 1819105024)

24He increased his people greatly, and made them stronger than their adversaries.


## Psalms 105:25 (id: 1819105025)

25He turned their heart to hate his people, to conspire against his servants.


## Psalms 105:26 (id: 1819105026)

26He sent Moses, his servant, and Aaron, whom he had chosen.


## Psalms 105:27 (id: 1819105027)

27They performed miracles among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.


## Psalms 105:28 (id: 1819105028)

28He sent darkness, and made it dark. They didn’t rebel against his words.


## Psalms 105:29 (id: 1819105029)

29He turned their waters into blood, and killed their fish.


## Psalms 105:30 (id: 1819105030)

30Their land swarmed with frogs, even in the rooms of their kings.


## Psalms 105:31 (id: 1819105031)

31He spoke, and swarms of flies came, and lice in all their borders.


## Psalms 105:32 (id: 1819105032)

32He gave them hail for rain, with lightning in their land.


## Psalms 105:33 (id: 1819105033)

33He struck their vines and also their fig trees, and shattered the trees of their country.


## Psalms 105:34 (id: 1819105034)

34He spoke, and the locusts came with the grasshoppers, without number.


## Psalms 105:35 (id: 1819105035)

35They ate up every plant in their land, and ate up the fruit of their ground.


## Psalms 105:36 (id: 1819105036)

36He struck also all the firstborn in their land, the first fruits of all their manhood.


## Psalms 105:37 (id: 1819105037)

37He brought them out with silver and gold. There was not one feeble person among his tribes.


## Psalms 105:38 (id: 1819105038)

38Egypt was glad when they departed, for the fear of them had fallen on them.


## Psalms 105:39 (id: 1819105039)

39He spread a cloud for a covering, fire to give light in the night.


## Psalms 105:40 (id: 1819105040)

40They asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them with the bread of the sky.


## Psalms 105:41 (id: 1819105041)

41He opened the rock, and waters gushed out. They ran as a river in the dry places.


## Psalms 105:42 (id: 1819105042)

42For he remembered his holy word, and Abraham, his servant.


## Psalms 105:43 (id: 1819105043)

43He brought his people out with joy, his chosen with singing.


## Psalms 105:44 (id: 1819105044)

44He gave them the lands of the nations. They took the labor of the peoples in possession,


## Psalms 105:45 (id: 1819105045)

45that they might keep his statutes, and observe his laws. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 106:1 (id: 1819106001)

1Praise the LORD! Give thanks to the LORD, for he is good, for his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 106:2 (id: 1819106002)

2Who can utter the mighty acts of the LORD, or fully declare all his praise?


## Psalms 106:3 (id: 1819106003)

3Blessed are those who keep justice. Blessed is one who does what is right at all times.


## Psalms 106:4 (id: 1819106004)

4Remember me, LORD, with the favor that you show to your people. Visit me with your salvation,


## Psalms 106:5 (id: 1819106005)

5that I may see the prosperity of your chosen, that I may rejoice in the gladness of your nation, that I may glory with your inheritance.


## Psalms 106:6 (id: 1819106006)

6We have sinned with our fathers. We have committed iniquity. We have done wickedly.


## Psalms 106:7 (id: 1819106007)

7Our fathers didn’t understand your wonders in Egypt. They didn’t remember the multitude of your loving kindnesses, but were rebellious at the sea, even at the Red Sea.


## Psalms 106:8 (id: 1819106008)

8Nevertheless he saved them for his name’s sake, that he might make his mighty power known.


## Psalms 106:9 (id: 1819106009)

9He rebuked the Red Sea also, and it was dried up; so he led them through the depths, as through a desert.


## Psalms 106:10 (id: 1819106010)

10He saved them from the hand of him who hated them, and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.


## Psalms 106:11 (id: 1819106011)

11The waters covered their adversaries. There was not one of them left.


## Psalms 106:12 (id: 1819106012)

12Then they believed his words. They sang his praise.


## Psalms 106:13 (id: 1819106013)

13They soon forgot his works. They didn’t wait for his counsel,


## Psalms 106:14 (id: 1819106014)

14but gave in to craving in the desert, and tested God in the wasteland.


## Psalms 106:15 (id: 1819106015)

15He gave them their request, but sent leanness into their soul.


## Psalms 106:16 (id: 1819106016)

16They envied Moses also in the camp, and Aaron, the LORD’s saint.


## Psalms 106:17 (id: 1819106017)

17The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, and covered the company of Abiram.


## Psalms 106:18 (id: 1819106018)

18A fire was kindled in their company. The flame burned up the wicked.


## Psalms 106:19 (id: 1819106019)

19They made a calf in Horeb, and worshiped a molten image.


## Psalms 106:20 (id: 1819106020)

20Thus they exchanged their glory for an image of a bull that eats grass.


## Psalms 106:21 (id: 1819106021)

21They forgot God, their Savior, who had done great things in Egypt,


## Psalms 106:22 (id: 1819106022)

22wondrous works in the land of Ham, and awesome things by the Red Sea.


## Psalms 106:23 (id: 1819106023)

23Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had Moses, his chosen, not stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, so that he wouldn’t destroy them.


## Psalms 106:24 (id: 1819106024)

24Yes, they despised the pleasant land. They didn’t believe his word,


## Psalms 106:25 (id: 1819106025)

25but murmured in their tents, and didn’t listen to the LORD’s voice.


## Psalms 106:26 (id: 1819106026)

26Therefore he swore to them that he would overthrow them in the wilderness,


## Psalms 106:27 (id: 1819106027)

27that he would overthrow their offspring among the nations, and scatter them in the lands.


## Psalms 106:28 (id: 1819106028)

28They joined themselves also to Baal Peor, and ate the sacrifices of the dead.


## Psalms 106:29 (id: 1819106029)

29Thus they provoked him to anger with their deeds. The plague broke in on them.


## Psalms 106:30 (id: 1819106030)

30Then Phinehas stood up and executed judgment, so the plague was stopped.


## Psalms 106:31 (id: 1819106031)

31That was credited to him for righteousness, for all generations to come.


## Psalms 106:32 (id: 1819106032)

32They angered him also at the waters of Meribah, so that Moses was troubled for their sakes;


## Psalms 106:33 (id: 1819106033)

33because they were rebellious against his spirit, he spoke rashly with his lips.


## Psalms 106:34 (id: 1819106034)

34They didn’t destroy the peoples, as the LORD commanded them,


## Psalms 106:35 (id: 1819106035)

35but mixed themselves with the nations, and learned their works.


## Psalms 106:36 (id: 1819106036)

36They served their idols, which became a snare to them.


## Psalms 106:37 (id: 1819106037)

37Yes, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons.


## Psalms 106:38 (id: 1819106038)

38They shed innocent blood, even the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan. The land was polluted with blood.


## Psalms 106:39 (id: 1819106039)

39Thus they were defiled with their works, and prostituted themselves in their deeds.


## Psalms 106:40 (id: 1819106040)

40Therefore the LORD burned with anger against his people. He abhorred his inheritance.


## Psalms 106:41 (id: 1819106041)

41He gave them into the hand of the nations. Those who hated them ruled over them.


## Psalms 106:42 (id: 1819106042)

42Their enemies also oppressed them. They were brought into subjection under their hand.


## Psalms 106:43 (id: 1819106043)

43He rescued them many times, but they were rebellious in their counsel, and were brought low in their iniquity.


## Psalms 106:44 (id: 1819106044)

44Nevertheless he regarded their distress, when he heard their cry.


## Psalms 106:45 (id: 1819106045)

45He remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his loving kindnesses.


## Psalms 106:46 (id: 1819106046)

46He made them also to be pitied by all those who carried them captive.


## Psalms 106:47 (id: 1819106047)

47Save us, LORD, our God, gather us from among the nations, to give thanks to your holy name, to triumph in your praise!


## Psalms 106:48 (id: 1819106048)

48Blessed be the LORD, the God of Israel, from everlasting even to everlasting! Let all the people say, “Amen.” Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 107:1 (id: 1819107001)

1Give thanks to the LORD, for he is good, for his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 107:2 (id: 1819107002)

2Let the redeemed by the LORD say so, whom he has redeemed from the hand of the adversary,


## Psalms 107:3 (id: 1819107003)

3and gathered out of the lands, from the east and from the west, from the north and from the south.


## Psalms 107:4 (id: 1819107004)

4They wandered in the wilderness in a desert way. They found no city to live in.


## Psalms 107:5 (id: 1819107005)

5Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them.


## Psalms 107:6 (id: 1819107006)

6Then they cried to the LORD in their trouble, and he delivered them out of their distresses.


## Psalms 107:7 (id: 1819107007)

7He led them also by a straight way, that they might go to a city to live in.


## Psalms 107:8 (id: 1819107008)

8Let them praise the LORD for his loving kindness, for his wonderful deeds to the children of men!


## Psalms 107:9 (id: 1819107009)

9For he satisfies the longing soul. He fills the hungry soul with good.


## Psalms 107:10 (id: 1819107010)

10Some sat in darkness and in the shadow of death, being bound in affliction and iron,


## Psalms 107:11 (id: 1819107011)

11because they rebelled against the words of God, and condemned the counsel of the Most High.


## Psalms 107:12 (id: 1819107012)

12Therefore he brought down their heart with labor. They fell down, and there was no one to help.


## Psalms 107:13 (id: 1819107013)

13Then they cried to the LORD in their trouble, and he saved them out of their distresses.


## Psalms 107:14 (id: 1819107014)

14He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, and broke away their chains.


## Psalms 107:15 (id: 1819107015)

15Let them praise the LORD for his loving kindness, for his wonderful deeds to the children of men!


## Psalms 107:16 (id: 1819107016)

16For he has broken the gates of bronze, and cut through bars of iron.


## Psalms 107:17 (id: 1819107017)

17Fools are afflicted because of their disobedience, and because of their iniquities.


## Psalms 107:18 (id: 1819107018)

18Their soul abhors all kinds of food. They draw near to the gates of death.


## Psalms 107:19 (id: 1819107019)

19Then they cry to the LORD in their trouble, and he saves them out of their distresses.


## Psalms 107:20 (id: 1819107020)

20He sends his word, and heals them, and delivers them from their graves.


## Psalms 107:21 (id: 1819107021)

21Let them praise the LORD for his loving kindness, for his wonderful deeds to the children of men!


## Psalms 107:22 (id: 1819107022)

22Let them offer the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and declare his deeds with singing.


## Psalms 107:23 (id: 1819107023)

23Those who go down to the sea in ships, who do business in great waters,


## Psalms 107:24 (id: 1819107024)

24these see the LORD’s deeds, and his wonders in the deep.


## Psalms 107:25 (id: 1819107025)

25For he commands, and raises the stormy wind, which lifts up its waves.


## Psalms 107:26 (id: 1819107026)

26They mount up to the sky; they go down again to the depths. Their soul melts away because of trouble.


## Psalms 107:27 (id: 1819107027)

27They reel back and forth, and stagger like a drunken man, and are at their wits’ end.


## Psalms 107:28 (id: 1819107028)

28Then they cry to the LORD in their trouble, and he brings them out of their distress.


## Psalms 107:29 (id: 1819107029)

29He makes the storm a calm, so that its waves are still.


## Psalms 107:30 (id: 1819107030)

30Then they are glad because it is calm, so he brings them to their desired haven.


## Psalms 107:31 (id: 1819107031)

31Let them praise the LORD for his loving kindness, for his wonderful deeds for the children of men!


## Psalms 107:32 (id: 1819107032)

32Let them exalt him also in the assembly of the people, and praise him in the seat of the elders.


## Psalms 107:33 (id: 1819107033)

33He turns rivers into a desert, water springs into a thirsty ground,


## Psalms 107:34 (id: 1819107034)

34and a fruitful land into a salt waste, for the wickedness of those who dwell in it.


## Psalms 107:35 (id: 1819107035)

35He turns a desert into a pool of water, and a dry land into water springs.


## Psalms 107:36 (id: 1819107036)

36There he makes the hungry live, that they may prepare a city to live in,


## Psalms 107:37 (id: 1819107037)

37sow fields, plant vineyards, and reap the fruits of increase.


## Psalms 107:38 (id: 1819107038)

38He blesses them also, so that they are multiplied greatly. He doesn’t allow their livestock to decrease.


## Psalms 107:39 (id: 1819107039)

39Again, they are diminished and bowed down through oppression, trouble, and sorrow.


## Psalms 107:40 (id: 1819107040)

40He pours contempt on princes, and causes them to wander in a trackless waste.


## Psalms 107:41 (id: 1819107041)

41Yet he lifts the needy out of their affliction, and increases their families like a flock.


## Psalms 107:42 (id: 1819107042)

42The upright will see it, and be glad. All the wicked will shut their mouths.


## Psalms 107:43 (id: 1819107043)

43Whoever is wise will pay attention to these things. They will consider the loving kindnesses of the LORD.


## Psalms 108:1 (id: 1819108001)

1A Song. A Psalm by David. My heart is steadfast, God. I will sing and I will make music with my soul.


## Psalms 108:2 (id: 1819108002)

2Wake up, harp and lyre! I will wake up the dawn.


## Psalms 108:3 (id: 1819108003)

3I will give thanks to you, LORD, among the nations. I will sing praises to you among the peoples.


## Psalms 108:4 (id: 1819108004)

4For your loving kindness is great above the heavens. Your faithfulness reaches to the skies.


## Psalms 108:5 (id: 1819108005)

5Be exalted, God, above the heavens! Let your glory be over all the earth.


## Psalms 108:6 (id: 1819108006)

6That your beloved may be delivered, save with your right hand, and answer us.


## Psalms 108:7 (id: 1819108007)

7God has spoken from his sanctuary: “In triumph, I will divide Shechem, and measure out the valley of Succoth.


## Psalms 108:8 (id: 1819108008)

8Gilead is mine. Manasseh is mine. Ephraim also is my helmet. Judah is my scepter.


## Psalms 108:9 (id: 1819108009)

9Moab is my wash pot. I will toss my sandal on Edom. I will shout over Philistia.”


## Psalms 108:10 (id: 1819108010)

10Who will bring me into the fortified city? Who will lead me to Edom?


## Psalms 108:11 (id: 1819108011)

11Haven’t you rejected us, God? You don’t go out, God, with our armies.


## Psalms 108:12 (id: 1819108012)

12Give us help against the enemy, for the help of man is vain.


## Psalms 108:13 (id: 1819108013)

13Through God, we will do valiantly, for it is he who will tread down our enemies.


## Psalms 109:1 (id: 1819109001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. God of my praise, don’t remain silent,


## Psalms 109:2 (id: 1819109002)

2for they have opened the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of deceit against me. They have spoken to me with a lying tongue.


## Psalms 109:3 (id: 1819109003)

3They have also surrounded me with words of hatred, and fought against me without a cause.


## Psalms 109:4 (id: 1819109004)

4In return for my love, they are my adversaries; but I am in prayer.


## Psalms 109:5 (id: 1819109005)

5They have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love.


## Psalms 109:6 (id: 1819109006)

6Set a wicked man over him. Let an adversary stand at his right hand.


## Psalms 109:7 (id: 1819109007)

7When he is judged, let him come out guilty. Let his prayer be turned into sin.


## Psalms 109:8 (id: 1819109008)

8Let his days be few. Let another take his office.


## Psalms 109:9 (id: 1819109009)

9Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow.


## Psalms 109:10 (id: 1819109010)

10Let his children be wandering beggars. Let them be sought from their ruins.


## Psalms 109:11 (id: 1819109011)

11Let the creditor seize all that he has. Let strangers plunder the fruit of his labor.


## Psalms 109:12 (id: 1819109012)

12Let there be no one to extend kindness to him, neither let there be anyone to have pity on his fatherless children.


## Psalms 109:13 (id: 1819109013)

13Let his posterity be cut off. In the generation following let their name be blotted out.


## Psalms 109:14 (id: 1819109014)

14Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered by the LORD. Don’t let the sin of his mother be blotted out.


## Psalms 109:15 (id: 1819109015)

15Let them be before the LORD continually, that he may cut off their memory from the earth;


## Psalms 109:16 (id: 1819109016)

16because he didn’t remember to show kindness, but persecuted the poor and needy man, the broken in heart, to kill them.


## Psalms 109:17 (id: 1819109017)

17Yes, he loved cursing, and it came to him. He didn’t delight in blessing, and it was far from him.


## Psalms 109:18 (id: 1819109018)

18He clothed himself also with cursing as with his garment. It came into his inward parts like water, like oil into his bones.


## Psalms 109:19 (id: 1819109019)

19Let it be to him as the clothing with which he covers himself, for the belt that is always around him.


## Psalms 109:20 (id: 1819109020)

20This is the reward of my adversaries from the LORD, of those who speak evil against my soul.


## Psalms 109:21 (id: 1819109021)

21But deal with me, GOD the Lord, for your name’s sake, because your loving kindness is good, deliver me;


## Psalms 109:22 (id: 1819109022)

22for I am poor and needy. My heart is wounded within me.


## Psalms 109:23 (id: 1819109023)

23I fade away like an evening shadow. I am shaken off like a locust.


## Psalms 109:24 (id: 1819109024)

24My knees are weak through fasting. My body is thin and lacks fat.


## Psalms 109:25 (id: 1819109025)

25I have also become a reproach to them. When they see me, they shake their head.


## Psalms 109:26 (id: 1819109026)

26Help me, LORD, my God. Save me according to your loving kindness;


## Psalms 109:27 (id: 1819109027)

27that they may know that this is your hand; that you, LORD, have done it.


## Psalms 109:28 (id: 1819109028)

28They may curse, but you bless. When they arise, they will be shamed, but your servant shall rejoice.


## Psalms 109:29 (id: 1819109029)

29Let my adversaries be clothed with dishonor. Let them cover themselves with their own shame as with a robe.


## Psalms 109:30 (id: 1819109030)

30I will give great thanks to the LORD with my mouth. Yes, I will praise him among the multitude.


## Psalms 109:31 (id: 1819109031)

31For he will stand at the right hand of the needy, to save him from those who judge his soul.


## Psalms 110:1 (id: 1819110001)

1A Psalm by David. The LORD says to my Lord, “Sit at my right hand, until I make your enemies your footstool for your feet.”


## Psalms 110:2 (id: 1819110002)

2The LORD will send out the rod of your strength out of Zion. Rule among your enemies.


## Psalms 110:3 (id: 1819110003)

3Your people offer themselves willingly in the day of your power, in holy array. Out of the womb of the morning, you have the dew of your youth.


## Psalms 110:4 (id: 1819110004)

4The LORD has sworn, and will not change his mind: “You are a priest forever in the order of Melchizedek.”


## Psalms 110:5 (id: 1819110005)

5The Lord is at your right hand. He will crush kings in the day of his wrath.


## Psalms 110:6 (id: 1819110006)

6He will judge among the nations. He will heap up dead bodies. He will crush the ruler of the whole earth.


## Psalms 110:7 (id: 1819110007)

7He will drink of the brook on the way; therefore he will lift up his head.


## Psalms 111:1 (id: 1819111001)

1Praise the LORD! I will give thanks to the LORD with my whole heart, in the council of the upright, and in the congregation.


## Psalms 111:2 (id: 1819111002)

2The LORD’s works are great, pondered by all those who delight in them.


## Psalms 111:3 (id: 1819111003)

3His work is honor and majesty. His righteousness endures forever.


## Psalms 111:4 (id: 1819111004)

4He has caused his wonderful works to be remembered. The LORD is gracious and merciful.


## Psalms 111:5 (id: 1819111005)

5He has given food to those who fear him. He always remembers his covenant.


## Psalms 111:6 (id: 1819111006)

6He has shown his people the power of his works, in giving them the heritage of the nations.


## Psalms 111:7 (id: 1819111007)

7The works of his hands are truth and justice. All his precepts are sure.


## Psalms 111:8 (id: 1819111008)

8They are established forever and ever. They are done in truth and uprightness.


## Psalms 111:9 (id: 1819111009)

9He has sent redemption to his people. He has ordained his covenant forever. His name is holy and awesome!


## Psalms 111:10 (id: 1819111010)

10The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom. All those who do his work have a good understanding. His praise endures forever!


## Psalms 112:1 (id: 1819112001)

1Praise the LORD! Blessed is the man who fears the LORD, who delights greatly in his commandments.


## Psalms 112:2 (id: 1819112002)

2His offspring will be mighty in the land. The generation of the upright will be blessed.


## Psalms 112:3 (id: 1819112003)

3Wealth and riches are in his house. His righteousness endures forever.


## Psalms 112:4 (id: 1819112004)

4Light dawns in the darkness for the upright, gracious, merciful, and righteous.


## Psalms 112:5 (id: 1819112005)

5It is well with the man who deals graciously and lends. He will maintain his cause in judgment.


## Psalms 112:6 (id: 1819112006)

6For he will never be shaken. The righteous will be remembered forever.


## Psalms 112:7 (id: 1819112007)

7He will not be afraid of evil news. His heart is steadfast, trusting in the LORD.


## Psalms 112:8 (id: 1819112008)

8His heart is established. He will not be afraid in the end when he sees his adversaries.


## Psalms 112:9 (id: 1819112009)

9He has dispersed, he has given to the poor. His righteousness endures forever. His horn will be exalted with honor.


## Psalms 112:10 (id: 1819112010)

10The wicked will see it, and be grieved. He shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away. The desire of the wicked will perish.


## Psalms 113:1 (id: 1819113001)

1Praise the LORD! Praise, you servants of the LORD, praise the LORD’s name.


## Psalms 113:2 (id: 1819113002)

2Blessed be the LORD’s name, from this time forward and forever more.


## Psalms 113:3 (id: 1819113003)

3From the rising of the sun to its going down, the LORD’s name is to be praised.


## Psalms 113:4 (id: 1819113004)

4The LORD is high above all nations, his glory above the heavens.


## Psalms 113:5 (id: 1819113005)

5Who is like the LORD, our God, who has his seat on high,


## Psalms 113:6 (id: 1819113006)

6who stoops down to see in heaven and in the earth?


## Psalms 113:7 (id: 1819113007)

7He raises up the poor out of the dust, and lifts up the needy from the ash heap,


## Psalms 113:8 (id: 1819113008)

8that he may set him with princes, even with the princes of his people.


## Psalms 113:9 (id: 1819113009)

9He settles the barren woman in her home as a joyful mother of children. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 114:1 (id: 1819114001)

1When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of foreign language,


## Psalms 114:2 (id: 1819114002)

2Judah became his sanctuary, Israel his dominion.


## Psalms 114:3 (id: 1819114003)

3The sea saw it, and fled. The Jordan was driven back.


## Psalms 114:4 (id: 1819114004)

4The mountains skipped like rams, the little hills like lambs.


## Psalms 114:5 (id: 1819114005)

5What was it, you sea, that you fled? You Jordan, that you turned back?


## Psalms 114:6 (id: 1819114006)

6You mountains, that you skipped like rams? You little hills, like lambs?


## Psalms 114:7 (id: 1819114007)

7Tremble, you earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob,


## Psalms 114:8 (id: 1819114008)

8who turned the rock into a pool of water, the flint into a spring of waters.


## Psalms 115:1 (id: 1819115001)

1Not to us, LORD, not to us, but to your name give glory, for your loving kindness, and for your truth’s sake.


## Psalms 115:2 (id: 1819115002)

2Why should the nations say, “Where is their God, now?”


## Psalms 115:3 (id: 1819115003)

3But our God is in the heavens. He does whatever he pleases.


## Psalms 115:4 (id: 1819115004)

4Their idols are silver and gold, the work of men’s hands.


## Psalms 115:5 (id: 1819115005)

5They have mouths, but they don’t speak. They have eyes, but they don’t see.


## Psalms 115:6 (id: 1819115006)

6They have ears, but they don’t hear. They have noses, but they don’t smell.


## Psalms 115:7 (id: 1819115007)

7They have hands, but they don’t feel. They have feet, but they don’t walk, neither do they speak through their throat.


## Psalms 115:8 (id: 1819115008)

8Those who make them will be like them; yes, everyone who trusts in them.


## Psalms 115:9 (id: 1819115009)

9Israel, trust in the LORD! He is their help and their shield.


## Psalms 115:10 (id: 1819115010)

10House of Aaron, trust in the LORD! He is their help and their shield.


## Psalms 115:11 (id: 1819115011)

11You who fear the LORD, trust in the LORD! He is their help and their shield.


## Psalms 115:12 (id: 1819115012)

12The LORD remembers us. He will bless us. He will bless the house of Israel. He will bless the house of Aaron.


## Psalms 115:13 (id: 1819115013)

13He will bless those who fear the LORD, both small and great.


## Psalms 115:14 (id: 1819115014)

14May the LORD increase you more and more, you and your children.


## Psalms 115:15 (id: 1819115015)

15Blessed are you by the LORD, who made heaven and earth.


## Psalms 115:16 (id: 1819115016)

16The heavens are the LORD’s heavens, but he has given the earth to the children of men.


## Psalms 115:17 (id: 1819115017)

17The dead don’t praise the LORD, nor any who go down into silence,


## Psalms 115:18 (id: 1819115018)

18but we will bless the LORD, from this time forward and forever more. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 116:1 (id: 1819116001)

1I love the LORD, because he listens to my voice, and my cries for mercy.


## Psalms 116:2 (id: 1819116002)

2Because he has turned his ear to me, therefore I will call on him as long as I live.


## Psalms 116:3 (id: 1819116003)

3The cords of death surrounded me, the pains of Sheol got a hold of me. I found trouble and sorrow.


## Psalms 116:4 (id: 1819116004)

4Then I called on the LORD’s name: “LORD, I beg you, deliver my soul.”


## Psalms 116:5 (id: 1819116005)

5The LORD is gracious and righteous. Yes, our God is merciful.


## Psalms 116:6 (id: 1819116006)

6The LORD preserves the simple. I was brought low, and he saved me.


## Psalms 116:7 (id: 1819116007)

7Return to your rest, my soul, for the LORD has dealt bountifully with you.


## Psalms 116:8 (id: 1819116008)

8For you have delivered my soul from death, my eyes from tears, and my feet from falling.


## Psalms 116:9 (id: 1819116009)

9I will walk before the LORD in the land of the living.


## Psalms 116:10 (id: 1819116010)

10I believed, therefore I said, “I was greatly afflicted.”


## Psalms 116:11 (id: 1819116011)

11I said in my haste, “All people are liars.”


## Psalms 116:12 (id: 1819116012)

12What will I give to the LORD for all his benefits toward me?


## Psalms 116:13 (id: 1819116013)

13I will take the cup of salvation, and call on the LORD’s name.


## Psalms 116:14 (id: 1819116014)

14I will pay my vows to the LORD, yes, in the presence of all his people.


## Psalms 116:15 (id: 1819116015)

15Precious in the LORD’s sight is the death of his saints.


## Psalms 116:16 (id: 1819116016)

16LORD, truly I am your servant. I am your servant, the son of your servant girl. You have freed me from my chains.


## Psalms 116:17 (id: 1819116017)

17I will offer to you the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and will call on the LORD’s name.


## Psalms 116:18 (id: 1819116018)

18I will pay my vows to the LORD, yes, in the presence of all his people,


## Psalms 116:19 (id: 1819116019)

19in the courts of the LORD’s house, in the middle of you, Jerusalem. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 117:1 (id: 1819117001)

1Praise the LORD, all you nations! Extol him, all you peoples!


## Psalms 117:2 (id: 1819117002)

2For his loving kindness is great toward us. The LORD’s faithfulness endures forever. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 118:1 (id: 1819118001)

1Give thanks to the LORD, for he is good, for his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 118:2 (id: 1819118002)

2Let Israel now say that his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 118:3 (id: 1819118003)

3Let the house of Aaron now say that his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 118:4 (id: 1819118004)

4Now let those who fear the LORD say that his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 118:5 (id: 1819118005)

5Out of my distress, I called on the LORD. The LORD answered me with freedom.


## Psalms 118:6 (id: 1819118006)

6The LORD is on my side. I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?


## Psalms 118:7 (id: 1819118007)

7The LORD is on my side among those who help me. Therefore I will look in triumph at those who hate me.


## Psalms 118:8 (id: 1819118008)

8It is better to take refuge in the LORD, than to put confidence in man.


## Psalms 118:9 (id: 1819118009)

9It is better to take refuge in the LORD, than to put confidence in princes.


## Psalms 118:10 (id: 1819118010)

10All the nations surrounded me, but in the LORD’s name I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:11 (id: 1819118011)

11They surrounded me, yes, they surrounded me. In the LORD’s name I indeed cut them off.


## Psalms 118:12 (id: 1819118012)

12They surrounded me like bees. They are quenched like the burning thorns. In the LORD’s name I cut them off.


## Psalms 118:13 (id: 1819118013)

13You pushed me back hard, to make me fall, but the LORD helped me.


## Psalms 118:14 (id: 1819118014)

14The LORD is my strength and song. He has become my salvation.


## Psalms 118:15 (id: 1819118015)

15The voice of rejoicing and salvation is in the tents of the righteous. “The right hand of the LORD does valiantly.


## Psalms 118:16 (id: 1819118016)

16The right hand of the LORD is exalted! The right hand of the LORD does valiantly!”


## Psalms 118:17 (id: 1819118017)

17I will not die, but live, and declare the LORD’s works.


## Psalms 118:18 (id: 1819118018)

18The LORD has punished me severely, but he has not given me over to death.


## Psalms 118:19 (id: 1819118019)

19Open to me the gates of righteousness. I will enter into them. I will give thanks to the LORD.


## Psalms 118:20 (id: 1819118020)

20This is the gate of the LORD; the righteous will enter into it.


## Psalms 118:21 (id: 1819118021)

21I will give thanks to you, for you have answered me, and have become my salvation.


## Psalms 118:22 (id: 1819118022)

22The stone which the builders rejected has become the cornerstone.


## Psalms 118:23 (id: 1819118023)

23This is the LORD’s doing. It is marvelous in our eyes.


## Psalms 118:24 (id: 1819118024)

24This is the day that the LORD has made. We will rejoice and be glad in it!


## Psalms 118:25 (id: 1819118025)

25Save us now, we beg you, LORD! LORD, we beg you, send prosperity now.


## Psalms 118:26 (id: 1819118026)

26Blessed is he who comes in the LORD’s name! We have blessed you out of the LORD’s house.


## Psalms 118:27 (id: 1819118027)

27The LORD is God, and he has given us light. Bind the sacrifice with cords, even to the horns of the altar.


## Psalms 118:28 (id: 1819118028)

28You are my God, and I will give thanks to you. You are my God, I will exalt you.


## Psalms 118:29 (id: 1819118029)

29Oh give thanks to the LORD, for he is good, for his loving kindness endures forever.


## Psalms 119:1 (id: 1819119001)

1ALEPH BETH GIMEL DALETH HE VAV ZAYIN HETH TETH YODH KAPF LAMEDH MEM NUN SAMEKH AYIN PE TZADHE QOPH RESH SIN AND SHIN TAV; Blessed are those whose ways are blameless, who walk according to the LORD’s law.


## Psalms 119:2 (id: 1819119002)

2Blessed are those who keep his statutes, who seek him with their whole heart.


## Psalms 119:3 (id: 1819119003)

3Yes, they do nothing wrong. They walk in his ways.


## Psalms 119:4 (id: 1819119004)

4You have commanded your precepts, that we should fully obey them.


## Psalms 119:5 (id: 1819119005)

5Oh that my ways were steadfast to obey your statutes!


## Psalms 119:6 (id: 1819119006)

6Then I wouldn’t be disappointed, when I consider all of your commandments.


## Psalms 119:7 (id: 1819119007)

7I will give thanks to you with uprightness of heart, when I learn your righteous judgments.


## Psalms 119:8 (id: 1819119008)

8I will observe your statutes. Don’t utterly forsake me.


## Psalms 119:9 (id: 1819119009)

9How can a young man keep his way pure? By living according to your word.


## Psalms 119:10 (id: 1819119010)

10With my whole heart I have sought you. Don’t let me wander from your commandments.


## Psalms 119:11 (id: 1819119011)

11I have hidden your word in my heart, that I might not sin against you.


## Psalms 119:12 (id: 1819119012)

12Blessed are you, LORD. Teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:13 (id: 1819119013)

13With my lips, I have declared all the ordinances of your mouth.


## Psalms 119:14 (id: 1819119014)

14I have rejoiced in the way of your testimonies, as much as in all riches.


## Psalms 119:15 (id: 1819119015)

15I will meditate on your precepts, and consider your ways.


## Psalms 119:16 (id: 1819119016)

16I will delight myself in your statutes. I will not forget your word.


## Psalms 119:17 (id: 1819119017)

17Do good to your servant. I will live and I will obey your word.


## Psalms 119:18 (id: 1819119018)

18Open my eyes, that I may see wondrous things out of your law.


## Psalms 119:19 (id: 1819119019)

19I am a stranger on the earth. Don’t hide your commandments from me.


## Psalms 119:20 (id: 1819119020)

20My soul is consumed with longing for your ordinances at all times.


## Psalms 119:21 (id: 1819119021)

21You have rebuked the proud who are cursed, who wander from your commandments.


## Psalms 119:22 (id: 1819119022)

22Take reproach and contempt away from me, for I have kept your statutes.


## Psalms 119:23 (id: 1819119023)

23Though princes sit and slander me, your servant will meditate on your statutes.


## Psalms 119:24 (id: 1819119024)

24Indeed your statutes are my delight, and my counselors.


## Psalms 119:25 (id: 1819119025)

25My soul is laid low in the dust. Revive me according to your word!


## Psalms 119:26 (id: 1819119026)

26I declared my ways, and you answered me. Teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:27 (id: 1819119027)

27Let me understand the teaching of your precepts! Then I will meditate on your wondrous works.


## Psalms 119:28 (id: 1819119028)

28My soul is weary with sorrow; strengthen me according to your word.


## Psalms 119:29 (id: 1819119029)

29Keep me from the way of deceit. Grant me your law graciously!


## Psalms 119:30 (id: 1819119030)

30I have chosen the way of truth. I have set your ordinances before me.


## Psalms 119:31 (id: 1819119031)

31I cling to your statutes, LORD. Don’t let me be disappointed.


## Psalms 119:32 (id: 1819119032)

32I run in the path of your commandments, for you have set my heart free.


## Psalms 119:33 (id: 1819119033)

33Teach me, LORD, the way of your statutes. I will keep them to the end.


## Psalms 119:34 (id: 1819119034)

34Give me understanding, and I will keep your law. Yes, I will obey it with my whole heart.


## Psalms 119:35 (id: 1819119035)

35Direct me in the path of your commandments, for I delight in them.


## Psalms 119:36 (id: 1819119036)

36Turn my heart toward your statutes, not toward selfish gain.


## Psalms 119:37 (id: 1819119037)

37Turn my eyes away from looking at worthless things. Revive me in your ways.


## Psalms 119:38 (id: 1819119038)

38Fulfill your promise to your servant, that you may be feared.


## Psalms 119:39 (id: 1819119039)

39Take away my disgrace that I dread, for your ordinances are good.


## Psalms 119:40 (id: 1819119040)

40Behold, I long for your precepts! Revive me in your righteousness.


## Psalms 119:41 (id: 1819119041)

41Let your loving kindness also come to me, LORD, your salvation, according to your word.


## Psalms 119:42 (id: 1819119042)

42So I will have an answer for him who reproaches me, for I trust in your word.


## Psalms 119:43 (id: 1819119043)

43Don’t snatch the word of truth out of my mouth, for I put my hope in your ordinances.


## Psalms 119:44 (id: 1819119044)

44So I will obey your law continually, forever and ever.


## Psalms 119:45 (id: 1819119045)

45I will walk in liberty, for I have sought your precepts.


## Psalms 119:46 (id: 1819119046)

46I will also speak of your statutes before kings, and will not be disappointed.


## Psalms 119:47 (id: 1819119047)

47I will delight myself in your commandments, because I love them.


## Psalms 119:48 (id: 1819119048)

48I reach out my hands for your commandments, which I love. I will meditate on your statutes.


## Psalms 119:49 (id: 1819119049)

49Remember your word to your servant, because you gave me hope.


## Psalms 119:50 (id: 1819119050)

50This is my comfort in my affliction, for your word has revived me.


## Psalms 119:51 (id: 1819119051)

51The arrogant mock me excessively, but I don’t swerve from your law.


## Psalms 119:52 (id: 1819119052)

52I remember your ordinances of old, LORD, and have comforted myself.


## Psalms 119:53 (id: 1819119053)

53Indignation has taken hold on me, because of the wicked who forsake your law.


## Psalms 119:54 (id: 1819119054)

54Your statutes have been my songs in the house where I live.


## Psalms 119:55 (id: 1819119055)

55I have remembered your name, LORD, in the night, and I obey your law.


## Psalms 119:56 (id: 1819119056)

56This is my way, that I keep your precepts.


## Psalms 119:57 (id: 1819119057)

57The LORD is my portion. I promised to obey your words.


## Psalms 119:58 (id: 1819119058)

58I sought your favor with my whole heart. Be merciful to me according to your word.


## Psalms 119:59 (id: 1819119059)

59I considered my ways, and turned my steps to your statutes.


## Psalms 119:60 (id: 1819119060)

60I will hurry, and not delay, to obey your commandments.


## Psalms 119:61 (id: 1819119061)

61The ropes of the wicked bind me, but I won’t forget your law.


## Psalms 119:62 (id: 1819119062)

62At midnight I will rise to give thanks to you, because of your righteous ordinances.


## Psalms 119:63 (id: 1819119063)

63I am a friend of all those who fear you, of those who observe your precepts.


## Psalms 119:64 (id: 1819119064)

64The earth is full of your loving kindness, LORD. Teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:65 (id: 1819119065)

65You have treated your servant well, according to your word, LORD.


## Psalms 119:66 (id: 1819119066)

66Teach me good judgment and knowledge, for I believe in your commandments.


## Psalms 119:67 (id: 1819119067)

67Before I was afflicted, I went astray; but now I observe your word.


## Psalms 119:68 (id: 1819119068)

68You are good, and do good. Teach me your statutes.


## Psalms 119:69 (id: 1819119069)

69The proud have smeared a lie upon me. With my whole heart, I will keep your precepts.


## Psalms 119:70 (id: 1819119070)

70Their heart is as callous as the fat, but I delight in your law.


## Psalms 119:71 (id: 1819119071)

71It is good for me that I have been afflicted, that I may learn your statutes.


## Psalms 119:72 (id: 1819119072)

72The law of your mouth is better to me than thousands of pieces of gold and silver.


## Psalms 119:73 (id: 1819119073)

73Your hands have made me and formed me. Give me understanding, that I may learn your commandments.


## Psalms 119:74 (id: 1819119074)

74Those who fear you will see me and be glad, because I have put my hope in your word.


## Psalms 119:75 (id: 1819119075)

75LORD, I know that your judgments are righteous, that in faithfulness you have afflicted me.


## Psalms 119:76 (id: 1819119076)

76Please let your loving kindness be for my comfort, according to your word to your servant.


## Psalms 119:77 (id: 1819119077)

77Let your tender mercies come to me, that I may live; for your law is my delight.


## Psalms 119:78 (id: 1819119078)

78Let the proud be disappointed, for they have overthrown me wrongfully. I will meditate on your precepts.


## Psalms 119:79 (id: 1819119079)

## Psalms 119:80 (id: 1819119080)

## Psalms 119:81 (id: 1819119081)

81My soul faints for your salvation. I hope in your word.


## Psalms 119:82 (id: 1819119082)

82My eyes fail for your word. I say, “When will you comfort me?”


## Psalms 119:83 (id: 1819119083)

83For I have become like a wineskin in the smoke. I don’t forget your statutes.

173Let your hand be ready to help me, for I have chosen your precepts.
