## Psalms 137:1 (id: 1819137001)

1By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down. Yes, we wept, when we remembered Zion.


## Psalms 137:2 (id: 1819137002)

2On the willows in that land, we hung up our harps.


## Psalms 137:3 (id: 1819137003)

3For there, those who led us captive asked us for songs. Those who tormented us demanded songs of joy: “Sing us one of the songs of Zion!”


## Psalms 137:4 (id: 1819137004)

4How can we sing the LORD’s song in a foreign land?


## Psalms 137:5 (id: 1819137005)

5If I forget you, Jerusalem, let my right hand forget its skill.


## Psalms 137:6 (id: 1819137006)

6Let my tongue stick to the roof of my mouth if I don’t remember you, if I don’t prefer Jerusalem above my chief joy.


## Psalms 137:7 (id: 1819137007)

7Remember, LORD, against the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem, who said, “Raze it! Raze it even to its foundation!”


## Psalms 137:8 (id: 1819137008)

8Daughter of Babylon, doomed to destruction, he will be happy who repays you, as you have done to us.


## Psalms 137:9 (id: 1819137009)

9Happy shall he be, who takes and dashes your little ones against the rock.


## Psalms 138:1 (id: 1819138001)

1By David. I will give you thanks with my whole heart. Before the gods, I will sing praises to you.


## Psalms 138:2 (id: 1819138002)

2I will bow down toward your holy temple, and give thanks to your Name for your loving kindness and for your truth; for you have exalted your Name and your Word above all.


## Psalms 138:3 (id: 1819138003)

3In the day that I called, you answered me. You encouraged me with strength in my soul.


## Psalms 138:4 (id: 1819138004)

4All the kings of the earth will give you thanks, LORD, for they have heard the words of your mouth.


## Psalms 138:5 (id: 1819138005)

5Yes, they will sing of the ways of the LORD, for the LORD’s glory is great!


## Psalms 138:6 (id: 1819138006)

6For though the LORD is high, yet he looks after the lowly; but he knows the proud from afar.


## Psalms 138:7 (id: 1819138007)

7Though I walk in the middle of trouble, you will revive me. You will stretch out your hand against the wrath of my enemies. Your right hand will save me.


## Psalms 138:8 (id: 1819138008)

8The LORD will fulfill that which concerns me. Your loving kindness, LORD, endures forever. Don’t forsake the works of your own hands.


## Psalms 139:1 (id: 1819139001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. LORD, you have searched me, and you know me.


## Psalms 139:2 (id: 1819139002)

2You know my sitting down and my rising up. You perceive my thoughts from afar.


## Psalms 139:3 (id: 1819139003)

3You search out my path and my lying down, and are acquainted with all my ways.


## Psalms 139:4 (id: 1819139004)

4For there is not a word on my tongue, but behold, LORD, you know it altogether.


## Psalms 139:5 (id: 1819139005)

5You hem me in behind and before. You laid your hand on me.


## Psalms 139:6 (id: 1819139006)

6This knowledge is beyond me. It’s lofty. I can’t attain it.


## Psalms 139:7 (id: 1819139007)

7Where could I go from your Spirit? Or where could I flee from your presence?


## Psalms 139:8 (id: 1819139008)

8If I ascend up into heaven, you are there. If I make my bed in Sheol, behold, you are there!


## Psalms 139:9 (id: 1819139009)

9If I take the wings of the dawn, and settle in the uttermost parts of the sea,


## Psalms 139:10 (id: 1819139010)

10even there your hand will lead me, and your right hand will hold me.


## Psalms 139:11 (id: 1819139011)

11If I say, “Surely the darkness will overwhelm me. The light around me will be night,”


## Psalms 139:12 (id: 1819139012)

12even the darkness doesn’t hide from you, but the night shines as the day. The darkness is like light to you.


## Psalms 139:13 (id: 1819139013)

13For you formed my inmost being. You knit me together in my mother’s womb.


## Psalms 139:14 (id: 1819139014)

14I will give thanks to you, for I am fearfully and wonderfully made. Your works are wonderful. My soul knows that very well.


## Psalms 139:15 (id: 1819139015)

15My frame wasn’t hidden from you, when I was made in secret, woven together in the depths of the earth.


## Psalms 139:16 (id: 1819139016)

16Your eyes saw my body. In your book they were all written, the days that were ordained for me, when as yet there were none of them.


## Psalms 139:17 (id: 1819139017)

17How precious to me are your thoughts, God! How vast is their sum!


## Psalms 139:18 (id: 1819139018)

18If I would count them, they are more in number than the sand. When I wake up, I am still with you.


## Psalms 139:19 (id: 1819139019)

19If only you, God, would kill the wicked. Get away from me, you bloodthirsty men!


## Psalms 139:20 (id: 1819139020)

20For they speak against you wickedly. Your enemies take your name in vain.


## Psalms 139:21 (id: 1819139021)

21LORD, don’t I hate those who hate you? Am I not grieved with those who rise up against you?


## Psalms 139:22 (id: 1819139022)

22I hate them with perfect hatred. They have become my enemies.


## Psalms 139:23 (id: 1819139023)

23Search me, God, and know my heart. Try me, and know my thoughts.


## Psalms 139:24 (id: 1819139024)

24See if there is any wicked way in me, and lead me in the everlasting way.


## Psalms 140:1 (id: 1819140001)

1For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. Deliver me, LORD, from evil men. Preserve me from violent men:


## Psalms 140:2 (id: 1819140002)

2those who devise mischief in their hearts. They continually gather themselves together for war.


## Psalms 140:3 (id: 1819140003)

3They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent. Viper’s poison is under their lips. Selah.


## Psalms 140:4 (id: 1819140004)

4LORD, keep me from the hands of the wicked. Preserve me from the violent men who have determined to trip my feet.


## Psalms 140:5 (id: 1819140005)

5The proud have hidden a snare for me, they have spread the cords of a net by the path. They have set traps for me. Selah.


## Psalms 140:6 (id: 1819140006)

6I said to the LORD, “You are my God.” Listen to the cry of my petitions, LORD.


## Psalms 140:7 (id: 1819140007)

7LORD, the Lord, the strength of my salvation, you have covered my head in the day of battle.


## Psalms 140:8 (id: 1819140008)

8LORD, don’t grant the desires of the wicked. Don’t let their evil plans succeed, or they will become proud. Selah.


## Psalms 140:9 (id: 1819140009)

9As for the head of those who surround me, let the mischief of their own lips cover them.


## Psalms 140:10 (id: 1819140010)

10Let burning coals fall on them. Let them be thrown into the fire, into miry pits, from where they never rise.


## Psalms 140:11 (id: 1819140011)

11An evil speaker won’t be established in the earth. Evil will hunt the violent man to overthrow him.


## Psalms 140:12 (id: 1819140012)

12I know that the LORD will maintain the cause of the afflicted, and justice for the needy.


## Psalms 140:13 (id: 1819140013)

13Surely the righteous will give thanks to your name. The upright will dwell in your presence.


## Psalms 141:1 (id: 1819141001)

1A Psalm by David. LORD, I have called on you. Come to me quickly! Listen to my voice when I call to you.


## Psalms 141:2 (id: 1819141002)

2Let my prayer be set before you like incense; the lifting up of my hands like the evening sacrifice.


## Psalms 141:3 (id: 1819141003)

3Set a watch, LORD, before my mouth. Keep the door of my lips.


## Psalms 141:4 (id: 1819141004)

4Don’t incline my heart to any evil thing, to practice deeds of wickedness with men who work iniquity. Don’t let me eat of their delicacies.


## Psalms 141:5 (id: 1819141005)

5Let the righteous strike me, it is kindness; let him reprove me, it is like oil on the head; don’t let my head refuse it; Yet my prayer is always against evil deeds.


## Psalms 141:6 (id: 1819141006)

6Their judges are thrown down by the sides of the rock. They will hear my words, for they are well spoken.


## Psalms 141:7 (id: 1819141007)

7“As when one plows and breaks up the earth, our bones are scattered at the mouth of Sheol.”


## Psalms 141:8 (id: 1819141008)

8For my eyes are on you, LORD, the Lord. I take refuge in you. Don’t leave my soul destitute.


## Psalms 141:9 (id: 1819141009)

9Keep me from the snare which they have laid for me, from the traps of the workers of iniquity.


## Psalms 141:10 (id: 1819141010)

10Let the wicked fall together into their own nets while I pass by.


## Psalms 142:1 (id: 1819142001)

1A contemplation by David, when he was in the cave. A Prayer. I cry with my voice to the LORD. With my voice, I ask the LORD for mercy.


## Psalms 142:2 (id: 1819142002)

2I pour out my complaint before him. I tell him my troubles.


## Psalms 142:3 (id: 1819142003)

3When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, you knew my route. On the path in which I walk, they have hidden a snare for me.


## Psalms 142:4 (id: 1819142004)

4Look on my right, and see; for there is no one who is concerned for me. Refuge has fled from me. No one cares for my soul.


## Psalms 142:5 (id: 1819142005)

5I cried to you, LORD. I said, “You are my refuge, my portion in the land of the living.”


## Psalms 142:6 (id: 1819142006)

6Listen to my cry, for I am in desperate need. Deliver me from my persecutors, for they are too strong for me.


## Psalms 142:7 (id: 1819142007)

7Bring my soul out of prison, that I may give thanks to your name. The righteous will surround me, for you will be good to me.


## Psalms 143:1 (id: 1819143001)

1A Psalm by David. Hear my prayer, LORD. Listen to my petitions. In your faithfulness and righteousness, relieve me.


## Psalms 143:2 (id: 1819143002)

2Don’t enter into judgment with your servant, for in your sight no man living is righteous.


## Psalms 143:3 (id: 1819143003)

3For the enemy pursues my soul. He has struck my life down to the ground. He has made me live in dark places, as those who have been long dead.


## Psalms 143:4 (id: 1819143004)

4Therefore my spirit is overwhelmed within me. My heart within me is desolate.


## Psalms 143:5 (id: 1819143005)

5I remember the days of old. I meditate on all your doings. I contemplate the work of your hands.


## Psalms 143:6 (id: 1819143006)

6I spread out my hands to you. My soul thirsts for you, like a parched land. Selah.


## Psalms 143:7 (id: 1819143007)

7Hurry to answer me, LORD. My spirit fails. Don’t hide your face from me, so that I don’t become like those who go down into the pit.


## Psalms 143:8 (id: 1819143008)

8Cause me to hear your loving kindness in the morning, for I trust in you. Cause me to know the way in which I should walk, for I lift up my soul to you.


## Psalms 143:9 (id: 1819143009)

9Deliver me, LORD, from my enemies. I flee to you to hide me.


## Psalms 143:10 (id: 1819143010)

10Teach me to do your will, for you are my God. Your Spirit is good. Lead me in the land of uprightness.


## Psalms 143:11 (id: 1819143011)

11Revive me, LORD, for your name’s sake. In your righteousness, bring my soul out of trouble.


## Psalms 143:12 (id: 1819143012)

12In your loving kindness, cut off my enemies, and destroy all those who afflict my soul, for I am your servant.


## Psalms 144:1 (id: 1819144001)

1By David. Blessed be the LORD, my rock, who trains my hands to war, and my fingers to battle—


## Psalms 144:2 (id: 1819144002)

2my loving kindness, my fortress, my high tower, my deliverer, my shield, and he in whom I take refuge, who subdues my people under me.


## Psalms 144:3 (id: 1819144003)

3LORD, what is man, that you care for him? Or the son of man, that you think of him?


## Psalms 144:4 (id: 1819144004)

4Man is like a breath. His days are like a shadow that passes away.


## Psalms 144:5 (id: 1819144005)

5Part your heavens, LORD, and come down. Touch the mountains, and they will smoke.


## Psalms 144:6 (id: 1819144006)

6Throw out lightning, and scatter them. Send out your arrows, and rout them.


## Psalms 144:7 (id: 1819144007)

7Stretch out your hand from above, rescue me, and deliver me out of great waters, out of the hands of foreigners,


## Psalms 144:8 (id: 1819144008)

8whose mouths speak deceit, whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.


## Psalms 144:9 (id: 1819144009)

9I will sing a new song to you, God. On a ten\-stringed lyre, I will sing praises to you.


## Psalms 144:10 (id: 1819144010)

10You are he who gives salvation to kings, who rescues David, his servant, from the deadly sword.


## Psalms 144:11 (id: 1819144011)

11Rescue me, and deliver me out of the hands of foreigners, whose mouths speak deceit, whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.


## Psalms 144:12 (id: 1819144012)

12Then our sons will be like well\-nurtured plants, our daughters like pillars carved to adorn a palace.


## Psalms 144:13 (id: 1819144013)

13Our barns are full, filled with all kinds of provision. Our sheep produce thousands and ten thousands in our fields.


## Psalms 144:14 (id: 1819144014)

14Our oxen will pull heavy loads. There is no breaking in, and no going away, and no outcry in our streets.


## Psalms 144:15 (id: 1819144015)

15Happy are the people who are in such a situation. Happy are the people whose God is the LORD.


## Psalms 145:1 (id: 1819145001)

1A praise psalm by David. I will exalt you, my God, the King. I will praise your name forever and ever.


## Psalms 145:2 (id: 1819145002)

2Every day I will praise you. I will extol your name forever and ever.


## Psalms 145:3 (id: 1819145003)

3Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised! His greatness is unsearchable.


## Psalms 145:4 (id: 1819145004)

4One generation will commend your works to another, and will declare your mighty acts.


## Psalms 145:5 (id: 1819145005)

5I will meditate on the glorious majesty of your honor, on your wondrous works.


## Psalms 145:6 (id: 1819145006)

6Men will speak of the might of your awesome acts. I will declare your greatness.


## Psalms 145:7 (id: 1819145007)

7They will utter the memory of your great goodness, and will sing of your righteousness.


## Psalms 145:8 (id: 1819145008)

8The LORD is gracious, merciful, slow to anger, and of great loving kindness.


## Psalms 145:9 (id: 1819145009)

9The LORD is good to all. His tender mercies are over all his works.


## Psalms 145:10 (id: 1819145010)

10All your works will give thanks to you, LORD. Your saints will extol you.


## Psalms 145:11 (id: 1819145011)

11They will speak of the glory of your kingdom, and talk about your power,


## Psalms 145:12 (id: 1819145012)

12to make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, the glory of the majesty of his kingdom.


## Psalms 145:13 (id: 1819145013)

13Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom. Your dominion endures throughout all generations. The LORD is faithful in all his words, and loving in all his deeds.


## Psalms 145:14 (id: 1819145014)

14The LORD upholds all who fall, and raises up all those who are bowed down.


## Psalms 145:15 (id: 1819145015)

15The eyes of all wait for you. You give them their food in due season.


## Psalms 145:16 (id: 1819145016)

16You open your hand, and satisfy the desire of every living thing.


## Psalms 145:17 (id: 1819145017)

17The LORD is righteous in all his ways, and gracious in all his works.


## Psalms 145:18 (id: 1819145018)

18The LORD is near to all those who call on him, to all who call on him in truth.


## Psalms 145:19 (id: 1819145019)

19He will fulfill the desire of those who fear him. He also will hear their cry, and will save them.


## Psalms 145:20 (id: 1819145020)

20The LORD preserves all those who love him, but he will destroy all the wicked.


## Psalms 145:21 (id: 1819145021)

21My mouth will speak the praise of the LORD. Let all flesh bless his holy name forever and ever.


## Psalms 146:1 (id: 1819146001)

1Praise the LORD! Praise the LORD, my soul.


## Psalms 146:2 (id: 1819146002)

2While I live, I will praise the LORD. I will sing praises to my God as long as I exist.


## Psalms 146:3 (id: 1819146003)

3Don’t put your trust in princes, in a son of man in whom there is no help.


## Psalms 146:4 (id: 1819146004)

4His spirit departs, and he returns to the earth. In that very day, his thoughts perish.


## Psalms 146:5 (id: 1819146005)

5Happy is he who has the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope is in the LORD, his God,


## Psalms 146:6 (id: 1819146006)

6who made heaven and earth, the sea, and all that is in them; who keeps truth forever;


## Psalms 146:7 (id: 1819146007)

7who executes justice for the oppressed; who gives food to the hungry. The LORD frees the prisoners.


## Psalms 146:8 (id: 1819146008)

8The LORD opens the eyes of the blind. The LORD raises up those who are bowed down. The LORD loves the righteous.


## Psalms 146:9 (id: 1819146009)

9The LORD preserves the foreigners. He upholds the fatherless and widow, but he turns the way of the wicked upside down.


## Psalms 146:10 (id: 1819146010)

10The LORD will reign forever; your God, O Zion, to all generations. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 147:1 (id: 1819147001)

1Praise the LORD, for it is good to sing praises to our God; for it is pleasant and fitting to praise him.


## Psalms 147:2 (id: 1819147002)

2The LORD builds up Jerusalem. He gathers together the outcasts of Israel.


## Psalms 147:3 (id: 1819147003)

3He heals the broken in heart, and binds up their wounds.


## Psalms 147:4 (id: 1819147004)

4He counts the number of the stars. He calls them all by their names.


## Psalms 147:5 (id: 1819147005)

5Great is our Lord, and mighty in power. His understanding is infinite.


## Psalms 147:6 (id: 1819147006)

6The LORD upholds the humble. He brings the wicked down to the ground.


## Psalms 147:7 (id: 1819147007)

7Sing to the LORD with thanksgiving. Sing praises on the harp to our God,


## Psalms 147:8 (id: 1819147008)

8who covers the sky with clouds, who prepares rain for the earth, who makes grass grow on the mountains.


## Psalms 147:9 (id: 1819147009)

9He provides food for the livestock, and for the young ravens when they call.


## Psalms 147:10 (id: 1819147010)

10He doesn’t delight in the strength of the horse. He takes no pleasure in the legs of a man.


## Psalms 147:11 (id: 1819147011)

11The LORD takes pleasure in those who fear him, in those who hope in his loving kindness.


## Psalms 147:12 (id: 1819147012)

12Praise the LORD, Jerusalem! Praise your God, Zion!


## Psalms 147:13 (id: 1819147013)

13For he has strengthened the bars of your gates. He has blessed your children within you.


## Psalms 147:14 (id: 1819147014)

14He makes peace in your borders. He fills you with the finest of the wheat.


## Psalms 147:15 (id: 1819147015)

15He sends out his commandment to the earth. His word runs very swiftly.


## Psalms 147:16 (id: 1819147016)

16He gives snow like wool, and scatters frost like ashes.


## Psalms 147:17 (id: 1819147017)

17He hurls down his hail like pebbles. Who can stand before his cold?


## Psalms 147:18 (id: 1819147018)

18He sends out his word, and melts them. He causes his wind to blow, and the waters flow.


## Psalms 147:19 (id: 1819147019)

19He shows his word to Jacob, his statutes and his ordinances to Israel.


## Psalms 147:20 (id: 1819147020)

20He has not done this for just any nation. They don’t know his ordinances. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 148:1 (id: 1819148001)

1Praise the LORD! Praise the LORD from the heavens! Praise him in the heights!


## Psalms 148:2 (id: 1819148002)

2Praise him, all his angels! Praise him, all his army!


## Psalms 148:3 (id: 1819148003)

3Praise him, sun and moon! Praise him, all you shining stars!


## Psalms 148:4 (id: 1819148004)

4Praise him, you heavens of heavens, you waters that are above the heavens.


## Psalms 148:5 (id: 1819148005)

5Let them praise the LORD’s name, for he commanded, and they were created.


## Psalms 148:6 (id: 1819148006)

6He has also established them forever and ever. He has made a decree which will not pass away.


## Psalms 148:7 (id: 1819148007)

7Praise the LORD from the earth, you great sea creatures, and all depths,


## Psalms 148:8 (id: 1819148008)

8lightning and hail, snow and clouds, stormy wind, fulfilling his word,


## Psalms 148:9 (id: 1819148009)

9mountains and all hills, fruit trees and all cedars,


## Psalms 148:10 (id: 1819148010)

10wild animals and all livestock, small creatures and flying birds,


## Psalms 148:11 (id: 1819148011)

11kings of the earth and all peoples, princes and all judges of the earth,


## Psalms 148:12 (id: 1819148012)

12both young men and maidens, old men and children.


## Psalms 148:13 (id: 1819148013)

13Let them praise the LORD’s name, for his name alone is exalted. His glory is above the earth and the heavens.


## Psalms 148:14 (id: 1819148014)

14He has lifted up the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints, even of the children of Israel, a people near to him. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 149:1 (id: 1819149001)

1Praise the LORD! Sing to the LORD a new song, his praise in the assembly of the saints.


## Psalms 149:2 (id: 1819149002)

2Let Israel rejoice in him who made them. Let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.


## Psalms 149:3 (id: 1819149003)

3Let them praise his name in the dance! Let them sing praises to him with tambourine and harp!


## Psalms 149:4 (id: 1819149004)

4For the LORD takes pleasure in his people. He crowns the humble with salvation.


## Psalms 149:5 (id: 1819149005)

5Let the saints rejoice in honor. Let them sing for joy on their beds.


## Psalms 149:6 (id: 1819149006)

6May the high praises of God be in their mouths, and a two\-edged sword in their hand,


## Psalms 149:7 (id: 1819149007)

7to execute vengeance on the nations, and punishments on the peoples;


## Psalms 149:8 (id: 1819149008)

8to bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron;


## Psalms 149:9 (id: 1819149009)

9to execute on them the written judgment. All his saints have this honor. Praise the LORD!


## Psalms 150:1 (id: 1819150001)

1Praise the LORD! Praise God in his sanctuary! Praise him in his heavens for his acts of power!


## Psalms 150:2 (id: 1819150002)

2Praise him for his mighty acts! Praise him according to his excellent greatness!


## Psalms 150:3 (id: 1819150003)

3Praise him with the sounding of the trumpet! Praise him with harp and lyre!


## Psalms 150:4 (id: 1819150004)

4Praise him with tambourine and dancing! Praise him with stringed instruments and flute!


## Psalms 150:5 (id: 1819150005)

5Praise him with loud cymbals! Praise him with resounding cymbals!


## Psalms 150:6 (id: 1819150006)

6Let everything that has breath praise the LORD! Praise the LORD!
